Sura 002

Verse 1

الم

Alif-Lãm-Mĩm.

These letters and other disjointed letters at the beginning of the surahs are an indication of the miraculous nature of the Quran; it was used to challenge the polytheists, who were unable to oppose it, even though it is composed of the same letters that make up the Arabic language. The Arabs' inability to produce something like it - even though they are the most eloquent of people - proves that the Quran is a revelation from Allah.

These disjointed letters at the beginning of the surah are a challenge to those who doubted the Quran's divine origin. It shows that despite using the same Arabic letters, no one could produce something similar to the Quran.

Verse 2

ذَٰلِكَ الْكِتَابُ لَا رَيْبَ ۛ فِيهِ ۛ هُدًى لِلْمُتَّقِينَ

This is the Book! There is no doubt about it—a guide for those mindful ˹of Allah˺,

That Quran is the great book, about which there is no doubt that it is from Allah. So, no one should have any doubts about it because it is clear. The righteous benefit from it through beneficial knowledge and righteous deeds, and they are the ones who fear Allah and follow His commands.

The Quran is a book without doubt, a guide for those who are mindful of Allah. Those who fear Allah and follow His commands can benefit from its teachings.

Verse 3

الَّذِينَ يُؤْمِنُونَ بِالْغَيْبِ وَيُقِيمُونَ الصَّلَاةَ وَمِمَّا رَزَقْنَاهُمْ يُنْفِقُونَ

who believe in the unseen, establish prayer, and donate from what We have provided for them,

And they are the ones who believe in the unseen, which cannot be perceived by their senses or their minds alone; because it can only be known through the revelation of Allah to His messengers, such as the belief in angels, Paradise, Hellfire, and other things that Allah has informed about, or that His Messenger has informed about. (And faith: a comprehensive word for acknowledging Allah, His angels, His books, His messengers, the Last Day, and destiny, both good and bad, and confirming that acknowledgement with words, actions, and in the heart, tongue, and limbs). And along with their belief in the unseen, they are diligent in performing prayer at its appointed times, correctly according to what Allah prescribed for His prophet Muhammad, may Allah bless him and grant him peace, and from what We have provided them with of wealth, they give the obligatory and recommended charity of their wealth.

The righteous are those who believe in the unseen, such as angels and the afterlife, establish prayer properly, and give charity from what Allah has provided them.

Verse 4

وَالَّذِينَ يُؤْمِنُونَ بِمَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْكَ وَمَا أُنْزِلَ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ وَبِالْآخِرَةِ هُمْ يُوقِنُونَ

and who believe in what has been revealed to you ˹O Prophet˺ and what was revealed before you, and have sure faith in the Hereafter.

And those who believe in what was revealed to you, O Messenger, of the Quran, and in what was revealed to you of wisdom, which is the Sunnah, and in all that was revealed before you to the messengers of books, such as the Torah, the Gospel, and others. And they believe in the abode of life after death and what it contains of reckoning and recompense, a belief in their hearts which manifests on their tongues and limbs. And the Last Day is specifically mentioned because belief in it is one of the greatest motivators for performing acts of obedience, avoiding prohibitions, and holding oneself accountable.

The righteous also believe in the Quran and the revelations before it, including previous scriptures. They have firm faith in the Hereafter, which motivates them to do good and avoid evil.

Verse 5

أُولَٰئِكَ عَلَىٰ هُدًى مِنْ رَبِّهِمْ ۖ وَأُولَٰئِكَ هُمُ الْمُفْلِحُونَ

It is they who are ˹truly˺ guided by their Lord, and it is they who will be successful.

Those with these characteristics are guided by a light from their Lord and with the success of their Creator and Guide, and they are the successful ones who have attained what they sought and have escaped the evil from which they fled.

Those with these characteristics are rightly guided by their Lord. They are the ones who are successful in this life and the Hereafter.

Verse 6

إِنَّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا سَوَاءٌ عَلَيْهِمْ أَأَنْذَرْتَهُمْ أَمْ لَمْ تُنْذِرْهُمْ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ

As for those who persist in disbelief, it is the same whether you warn them or not—they will never believe.

Indeed, those who have denied what was revealed to you from your Lord out of arrogance and transgression, faith will not occur from them, whether you warn them and caution them against the punishment of Allah, or you leave that; because of their insistence on their falsehood.

This verse describes those who stubbornly reject faith. Whether they are warned or not, they will not believe due to their arrogance and persistence in disbelief.

Verse 7

خَتَمَ اللَّهُ عَلَىٰ قُلُوبِهِمْ وَعَلَىٰ سَمْعِهِمْ ۖ وَعَلَىٰ أَبْصَارِهِمْ غِشَاوَةٌ ۖ وَلَهُمْ عَذَابٌ عَظِيمٌ

Allah has sealed their hearts and their hearing, and their sight is covered. They will suffer a tremendous punishment.

Allah has set a seal upon their hearts and upon their hearing, and has placed a cover over their sight; because of their disbelief and defiance after the truth became clear to them, so they were not guided to the right path, and for them is a severe punishment in the Fire of Hell.

Allah has sealed their hearts and hearing, and veiled their sight, as a result of their deliberate rejection of the truth. This leads to severe punishment.

Verse 8

وَمِنَ النَّاسِ مَنْ يَقُولُ آمَنَّا بِاللَّهِ وَبِالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ وَمَا هُمْ بِمُؤْمِنِينَ

And there are some who say, “We believe in Allah and the Last Day,” yet they are not ˹true˺ believers.

And among the people is a group that hesitates, confused between the believers and the disbelievers, and they are the hypocrites who say with their tongues, "We have believed in Allah and in the Last Day," while in their hearts they are liars, they have not believed.

This verse introduces the hypocrites who claim to believe in Allah and the Last Day with their tongues but do not have faith in their hearts.

Verse 9

يُخَادِعُونَ اللَّهَ وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَمَا يَخْدَعُونَ إِلَّا أَنْفُسَهُمْ وَمَا يَشْعُرُونَ

They seek to deceive Allah and the believers, yet they only deceive themselves, but they fail to perceive it.

They believe in their ignorance that they deceive Allah and those who have believed by showing belief and concealing disbelief, but they only deceive themselves; because the consequence of their deception returns upon them. And from the excess of their ignorance, they do not perceive that; due to the corruption of their hearts.

Hypocrites think they are deceiving Allah and the believers by showing faith and hiding disbelief. In reality, they only deceive themselves, though they don't realize it.

Verse 10

فِي قُلُوبِهِمْ مَرَضٌ فَزَادَهُمُ اللَّهُ مَرَضًا ۖ وَلَهُمْ عَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌ بِمَا كَانُوا يَكْذِبُونَ

There is sickness in their hearts, and Allah ˹only˺ lets their sickness increase. They will suffer a painful punishment for their lies.

In their hearts is doubt and corruption, so they were afflicted with sins that necessitate their punishment, so Allah increased them in doubt, and for them is a painful punishment because of their lies and hypocrisy.

The hearts of the hypocrites are sick with doubt and corruption. Allah allows their sickness to increase, leading to a painful punishment for their lies.

Verse 11

وَإِذَا قِيلَ لَهُمْ لَا تُفْسِدُوا فِي الْأَرْضِ قَالُوا إِنَّمَا نَحْنُ مُصْلِحُونَ

When they are told, “Do not spread corruption in the land,” they reply, “We are only peace-makers!”

And when they are advised to refrain from causing corruption on earth through disbelief and sins, and disclosing the secrets of the believers, and befriending the disbelievers, they say, falsely and argumentatively, "We are but reformers."

When told not to cause corruption, hypocrites claim they are peacemakers, concealing their malicious actions and intentions.

Verse 12

أَلَا إِنَّهُمْ هُمُ الْمُفْسِدُونَ وَلَٰكِنْ لَا يَشْعُرُونَ

Indeed, it is they who are the corruptors, but they fail to perceive it.

Indeed, what they do and claim to be reform is the essence of corruption, but because of their ignorance and obstinacy, they do not perceive it.

Hypocrites are in fact the corruptors, but their ignorance and stubbornness prevent them from acknowledging this truth.

Verse 13

وَإِذَا قِيلَ لَهُمْ آمِنُوا كَمَا آمَنَ النَّاسُ قَالُوا أَنُؤْمِنُ كَمَا آمَنَ السُّفَهَاءُ ۗ أَلَا إِنَّهُمْ هُمُ السُّفَهَاءُ وَلَٰكِنْ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ

And when they are told, “Believe as others believe,” they reply, “Will we believe as the fools believe?” Indeed, it is they who are fools, but they do not know.

And when it is said to the hypocrites: "Believe - like the belief of the companions, which is belief in the heart, tongue, and limbs"-, they argue and say: "Shall we believe like the belief of the weak of mind and opinion, so that we and they are equal in foolishness?" So Allah responded to them that foolishness is exclusive to them, and they do not know that what they are in is misguidance and loss.

When asked to believe as the believers do, hypocrites ask if they should believe like the 'fools.' They are the true fools, unaware of their misguidance.

Verse 14

وَإِذَا لَقُوا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا قَالُوا آمَنَّا وَإِذَا خَلَوْا إِلَىٰ شَيَاطِينِهِمْ قَالُوا إِنَّا مَعَكُمْ إِنَّمَا نَحْنُ مُسْتَهْزِئُونَ

When they meet the believers they say, “We believe.” But when alone with their evil associates they say, “We are definitely with you; we were only mocking.”

These hypocrites, when they meet the believers, say: "We have believed in Islam like you," and when they turn away and go to their leaders, the disbelievers who rebel against Allah, they confirm to them that they are on the path of disbelief and have not left it, but they were mocking the believers and making fun of them.

Hypocrites pretend to believe when with believers but reveal their true allegiance to the disbelievers, admitting they were only mocking the believers.

Verse 15

اللَّهُ يَسْتَهْزِئُ بِهِمْ وَيَمُدُّهُمْ فِي طُغْيَانِهِمْ يَعْمَهُونَ

Allah will throw their mockery back at them, leaving them to continue wandering blindly in their defiance.

Allah mocks them and gives them respite; so that they increase in misguidance, confusion, and hesitation, and He will recompense them for their mockery of the believers.

Allah will repay their mockery, leaving them lost in their arrogance and defiance, and they will be punished for their actions.

Verse 16

أُولَٰئِكَ الَّذِينَ اشْتَرَوُا الضَّلَالَةَ بِالْهُدَىٰ فَمَا رَبِحَتْ تِجَارَتُهُمْ وَمَا كَانُوا مُهْتَدِينَ

They are the ones who trade guidance for misguidance. But this trade is profitless, and they are not ˹rightly˺ guided.

Those are the hypocrites who sold themselves in a losing bargain, so they took disbelief and abandoned faith, so they gained nothing, rather they lost guidance. And this is the clear loss.

Hypocrites have exchanged guidance for misguidance, a losing bargain that demonstrates their clear loss and lack of true guidance.

Verse 17

مَثَلُهُمْ كَمَثَلِ الَّذِي اسْتَوْقَدَ نَارًا فَلَمَّا أَضَاءَتْ مَا حَوْلَهُ ذَهَبَ اللَّهُ بِنُورِهِمْ وَتَرَكَهُمْ فِي ظُلُمَاتٍ لَا يُبْصِرُونَ

Their example is that of someone who kindles a fire, but when it lights up all around them, Allah takes away their light, leaving them in complete darkness—unable to see.

The state of the hypocrites who believed - outwardly, not inwardly - in the message of Muhammad, may Allah bless him and grant him peace, then disbelieved, and thus began to stumble in the darkness of their misguidance while they are unaware, with no hope of escaping from it, resembles the state of a group in a dark night, where one of them lit a great fire for warmth and illumination. When the fire blazed and illuminated its surroundings, it went out and became dark, so its companions were in darkness, unable to see anything, nor finding a path or way out.

This verse describes the hypocrites who initially embraced the truth but then rejected it. They are likened to people who light a fire that illuminates their surroundings, only for the light to be taken away, leaving them in complete darkness, unable to see or find their way.

Verse 18

صُمٌّ بُكْمٌ عُمْيٌ فَهُمْ لَا يَرْجِعُونَ

They are ˹wilfully˺ deaf, dumb, and blind, so they will never return ˹to the Right Path˺.

They are deaf to hearing the truth with contemplation, mute to speaking it, blind to seeing the light of guidance; therefore, they cannot return to the faith they left, replacing it with misguidance.

The hypocrites are metaphorically described as deaf to the truth, mute in proclaiming it, and blind to guidance. They are unwilling to return to the right path because of their stubbornness and inner corruption.

Verse 19

أَوْ كَصَيِّبٍ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ فِيهِ ظُلُمَاتٌ وَرَعْدٌ وَبَرْقٌ يَجْعَلُونَ أَصَابِعَهُمْ فِي آذَانِهِمْ مِنَ الصَّوَاعِقِ حَذَرَ الْمَوْتِ ۚ وَاللَّهُ مُحِيطٌ بِالْكَافِرِينَ

Or ˹those caught in˺ a rainstorm from the sky with darkness, thunder, and lightning. They press their fingers into their ears at the sound of every thunder-clap for fear of death. And Allah encompasses the disbelievers ˹by His might˺.

Or the state resembles another group of hypocrites, to whom the truth appears sometimes, and they doubt it at other times, like a group walking in the open, when a heavy rain falls upon them, accompanied by layers of darkness, with the crashing thunder, the flashing lightning, and the scorching thunderbolts, which make them, out of intense horror, place their fingers in their ears for fear of destruction. And Allah Almighty encompasses the disbelievers; they cannot escape Him nor render Him helpless.

This verse presents another analogy for the unstable state of the hypocrites. They are like people caught in a violent storm, with darkness, thunder, and lightning causing them immense fear and uncertainty. They try to avoid the truth because they are afraid of facing consequences.

Verse 20

يَكَادُ الْبَرْقُ يَخْطَفُ أَبْصَارَهُمْ ۖ كُلَّمَا أَضَاءَ لَهُمْ مَشَوْا فِيهِ وَإِذَا أَظْلَمَ عَلَيْهِمْ قَامُوا ۚ وَلَوْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ لَذَهَبَ بِسَمْعِهِمْ وَأَبْصَارِهِمْ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ

It is as if the lightning were about to snatch away their sight. Whenever lightning strikes, they walk in its light, but when darkness covers them, they stand still. Had Allah willed, He could have taken away their hearing and sight. Surely Allah is Most Capable of everything.

The lightning - from its intense brilliance - almost snatches away their sight, yet whenever it illuminates for them, they walk in its light, and when it is gone, the path becomes dark for them, and they stop in their places. Were it not for Allah's respite for them, He would have taken away their hearing and sight, and He is able to do that at any time. Indeed, He is over all things competent.

The lightning in the storm is described as almost taking away their sight. When the lightning flashes, they walk, but when darkness returns, they stop, representing the hypocrites' wavering faith. It also signifies Allah's power to take away their senses anytime.

Verse 21

يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ اعْبُدُوا رَبَّكُمُ الَّذِي خَلَقَكُمْ وَالَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَتَّقُونَ

O humanity! Worship your Lord, Who created you and those before you, so that you may become mindful ˹of Him˺.

A call from Allah to all of humanity: to worship Allah, who nurtured you with His favors, fear Him, and do not disobey His religion; for He brought you into existence from nothingness, and He brought into existence those who came before you, so that you may be among the righteous whom Allah is pleased with and who are pleased with Him.

This verse is a call to all humanity to worship their Lord, who created them and their ancestors. It urges people to be mindful of Allah's blessings and commands.

Verse 22

الَّذِي جَعَلَ لَكُمُ الْأَرْضَ فِرَاشًا وَالسَّمَاءَ بِنَاءً وَأَنْزَلَ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ مَاءً فَأَخْرَجَ بِهِ مِنَ الثَّمَرَاتِ رِزْقًا لَكُمْ ۖ فَلَا تَجْعَلُوا لِلَّهِ أَنْدَادًا وَأَنْتُمْ تَعْلَمُونَ

˹He is the One˺ Who has made the earth a place of settlement for you and the sky a canopy; and sends down rain from the sky, causing fruits to grow as a provision for you. So do not knowingly set up equals to Allah ˹in worship˺.

Your Lord, who made the earth a carpet for you so that your life on it is easy, and the sky a firmly constructed building, and sent down rain from the clouds and brought forth for you by it fruits of various colors and types of plants as provision for you, so do not assign to Allah equals in worship, while you know that He is unique in creation and provision, and deserving of worship.

Allah is the One who made the earth habitable and the sky a protective canopy. He sends down rain for sustenance. Therefore, no one should be associated with Allah in worship because He is the sole Creator and Provider.

Verse 23

وَإِنْ كُنْتُمْ فِي رَيْبٍ مِمَّا نَزَّلْنَا عَلَىٰ عَبْدِنَا فَأْتُوا بِسُورَةٍ مِنْ مِثْلِهِ وَادْعُوا شُهَدَاءَكُمْ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ صَادِقِينَ

And if you are in doubt about what We have revealed to Our servant, then produce a sûrah like it and call your helpers other than Allah, if what you say is true.

And if you - O disbelieving opponents - are in doubt about the Quran which We have revealed to Our servant Muhammad, may Allah bless him and grant him peace, and you claim that it is not from Allah, then bring a chapter similar to a chapter from the Quran, and call upon whoever you can of your helpers, if you are truthful in your claim.

This verse challenges those who doubt the Quran's divine origin. If they believe it is not from Allah, they are asked to produce a chapter similar to it, calling upon all their helpers if necessary. This is a challenge that has never been met.

Verse 24

فَإِنْ لَمْ تَفْعَلُوا وَلَنْ تَفْعَلُوا فَاتَّقُوا النَّارَ الَّتِي وَقُودُهَا النَّاسُ وَالْحِجَارَةُ ۖ أُعِدَّتْ لِلْكَافِرِينَ

But if you are unable to do so—and you will never be able to do so—then fear the Fire fuelled with people and stones, which is prepared for the disbelievers.

Then if you are unable now - and you will be unable in the future, without a doubt - then fear the Fire by believing in the Prophet, may Allah bless him and grant him peace, and obeying Allah Almighty. This Fire whose fuel is people and stones, is prepared for the disbelievers in Allah and His messengers.

Since they will never be able to meet the challenge in the previous verse, they are warned to fear the Fire, which is fueled by people and stones and prepared for those who disbelieve. This is a reminder that rejecting faith leads to severe consequences.

Verse 25

وَبَشِّرِ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ أَنَّ لَهُمْ جَنَّاتٍ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهَا الْأَنْهَارُ ۖ كُلَّمَا رُزِقُوا مِنْهَا مِنْ ثَمَرَةٍ رِزْقًا ۙ قَالُوا هَٰذَا الَّذِي رُزِقْنَا مِنْ قَبْلُ ۖ وَأُتُوا بِهِ مُتَشَابِهًا ۖ وَلَهُمْ فِيهَا أَزْوَاجٌ مُطَهَّرَةٌ ۖ وَهُمْ فِيهَا خَالِدُونَ

Give good news ˹O Prophet˺ to those who believe and do good that they will have Gardens under which rivers flow. Whenever provided with fruit, they will say, “This is what we were given before,” for they will be served fruit that looks similar ˹but tastes different˺. They will have pure spouses, and they will be there forever.

And inform - O Messenger - the people of faith and good deeds with news that fills them with joy, that they will have in the Hereafter wonderful gardens, with rivers flowing beneath their high palaces and shady trees. Every time Allah provides them with a type of delicious fruit, they will say: Allah has provided us with this type before. But when they taste it, they find it something new in its taste and pleasure, even if it is similar to its previous one in color, appearance, and name. And they will have in Paradise spouses purified from all kinds of physical impurity, such as urine and menstruation, and moral impurity, such as lying and bad character. And they will abide in Paradise and its bliss forever, they will not die in it nor will they be removed from it.

This verse gives glad tidings to believers who do good, promising them gardens with flowing rivers in Paradise. They will enjoy fruits that appear familiar but taste new and pure spouses, living there forever.

Verse 26

إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يَسْتَحْيِي أَنْ يَضْرِبَ مَثَلًا مَا بَعُوضَةً فَمَا فَوْقَهَا ۚ فَأَمَّا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا فَيَعْلَمُونَ أَنَّهُ الْحَقُّ مِنْ رَبِّهِمْ ۖ وَأَمَّا الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا فَيَقُولُونَ مَاذَا أَرَادَ اللَّهُ بِهَٰذَا مَثَلًا ۘ يُضِلُّ بِهِ كَثِيرًا وَيَهْدِي بِهِ كَثِيرًا ۚ وَمَا يُضِلُّ بِهِ إِلَّا الْفَاسِقِينَ

Surely Allah does not shy away from using the parable of a mosquito or what is even smaller. As for the believers, they know that it is the truth from their Lord. And as for the disbelievers, they argue, “What does Allah mean by such a parable?” Through this ˹test˺, He leaves many to stray, and guides many. And He leaves none to stray except the rebellious—

Indeed, Allah Almighty is not ashamed of the truth to mention anything, whether small or large, even if it is an analogy with the smallest thing, such as a mosquito, a fly, and the like, which Allah has set as an example of the impotence of everything that is worshipped besides Allah. As for the believers, they know the wisdom of Allah in using the small and large of His creation as examples. As for the disbelievers, they scoff and say: What does Allah mean by setting an example with these insignificant insects? Allah answers them that the purpose is to test and distinguish the believer from the disbeliever. Therefore, Allah misguides many people from the truth by this example because of their mockery, and guides others to more faith and guidance. And Allah Almighty does not wrong anyone, because He does not turn away from the truth except those who disobey Him.

Allah uses parables, even of small things like a mosquito, to teach. Believers understand these as truth from Allah, while disbelievers question their meaning. Through these parables, Allah guides some and lets others stray based on their own choices and rebelliousness.

Verse 27

الَّذِينَ يَنْقُضُونَ عَهْدَ اللَّهِ مِنْ بَعْدِ مِيثَاقِهِ وَيَقْطَعُونَ مَا أَمَرَ اللَّهُ بِهِ أَنْ يُوصَلَ وَيُفْسِدُونَ فِي الْأَرْضِ ۚ أُولَٰئِكَ هُمُ الْخَاسِرُونَ

those who violate Allah’s covenant after it has been affirmed, break whatever ˹ties˺ Allah has ordered to be maintained, and spread corruption in the land. It is they who are the ˹true˺ losers.

Those who break the covenant of Allah that He took upon them of monotheism and obedience, and He has affirmed it by sending messengers and revealing books, and they violate the religion of Allah such as severing ties of kinship and spreading corruption on earth, those are the losers in this world and the hereafter.

This verse describes those who break their covenant with Allah, sever ties, and cause corruption. These are the true losers in both this life and the hereafter.

Verse 28

كَيْفَ تَكْفُرُونَ بِاللَّهِ وَكُنْتُمْ أَمْوَاتًا فَأَحْيَاكُمْ ۖ ثُمَّ يُمِيتُكُمْ ثُمَّ يُحْيِيكُمْ ثُمَّ إِلَيْهِ تُرْجَعُونَ

How can you deny Allah? You were lifeless and He gave you life, then He will cause you to die and again bring you to life, and then to Him you will ˹all˺ be returned.

How can you deny - O polytheists - the Oneness of Allah Almighty, and associate others with Him in worship, with the conclusive proof of it within yourselves? You were dead, and He brought you into existence and breathed life into you, then He will cause you to die after the end of your appointed terms, then He will resurrect you alive on the Day of Resurrection, then to Him you will return for reckoning and recompense.

This verse is a reminder of Allah's power and creation. It questions how one can deny Allah when He brought them to life, will cause them to die, and then resurrect them for judgment.

Verse 29

هُوَ الَّذِي خَلَقَ لَكُمْ مَا فِي الْأَرْضِ جَمِيعًا ثُمَّ اسْتَوَىٰ إِلَى السَّمَاءِ فَسَوَّاهُنَّ سَبْعَ سَمَاوَاتٍ ۚ وَهُوَ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عَلِيمٌ

He is the One Who created everything in the earth for you. Then He turned towards the heaven, forming it into seven heavens. And He has ˹perfect˺ knowledge of all things.

Allah alone is the One who created for you all that is on earth of blessings from which you benefit, then He turned to the creation of the heavens, and He made them seven heavens, and He is Knowing of all things. His knowledge - Glory be to Him - encompasses all that He has created.

Allah created all things on earth for humanity and then turned to creating the seven heavens. This verse highlights Allah's comprehensive knowledge and control over all of creation.

Verse 30

وَإِذْ قَالَ رَبُّكَ لِلْمَلَائِكَةِ إِنِّي جَاعِلٌ فِي الْأَرْضِ خَلِيفَةً ۖ قَالُوا أَتَجْعَلُ فِيهَا مَنْ يُفْسِدُ فِيهَا وَيَسْفِكُ الدِّمَاءَ وَنَحْنُ نُسَبِّحُ بِحَمْدِكَ وَنُقَدِّسُ لَكَ ۖ قَالَ إِنِّي أَعْلَمُ مَا لَا تَعْلَمُونَ

˹Remember˺ when your Lord said to the angels, “I am going to place a successive ˹human˺ authority on earth.” They asked ˹Allah˺, “Will You place in it someone who will spread corruption there and shed blood while we glorify Your praises and proclaim Your holiness?” Allah responded, “I know what you do not know.”

And remember - O Messenger - when your Lord said to the angels: “Indeed, I will make upon the earth a people who will succeed one another to cultivate it.” They said: “Our Lord, teach us and guide us, what is the wisdom in creating these, considering that their nature is to cause corruption on earth and shed blood unjustly and aggressively, while we are obedient to Your command, exalting You with the praise and glory that befits You, and magnifying You with all attributes of perfection and majesty?” Allah said to them: “Indeed, I know that which you do not know of the profound wisdom in their creation.”

Allah informs the angels of His plan to create humans as His representatives on Earth. The angels question this due to their potential for corruption, but Allah asserts His superior knowledge.

Verse 31

وَعَلَّمَ آدَمَ الْأَسْمَاءَ كُلَّهَا ثُمَّ عَرَضَهُمْ عَلَى الْمَلَائِكَةِ فَقَالَ أَنْبِئُونِي بِأَسْمَاءِ هَٰؤُلَاءِ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ صَادِقِينَ

He taught Adam the names of all things, then He presented them to the angels and said, “Tell Me the names of these, if what you say is true?”

And to show the superiority of Adam, peace be upon him, Allah taught him the names of all things. Then He presented their names to the angels, saying to them, “Inform Me of the names of these entities, if you are truthful that you are more worthy of being successors on earth than them.”

To demonstrate Adam's superiority, Allah taught him the names of all things, a knowledge the angels did not possess.

Verse 32

قَالُوا سُبْحَانَكَ لَا عِلْمَ لَنَا إِلَّا مَا عَلَّمْتَنَا ۖ إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ الْعَلِيمُ الْحَكِيمُ

They replied, “Glory be to You! We have no knowledge except what You have taught us. You are truly the All-Knowing, All-Wise.”

The angels said, “Glory to You, our Lord, we have no knowledge except what You have taught us. Indeed, You alone are the All-Knowing of Your creation's affairs, the All-Wise in Your management.”

The angels acknowledge their limited knowledge, glorifying Allah and recognizing Him as the All-Knowing and All-Wise.

Verse 33

قَالَ يَا آدَمُ أَنْبِئْهُمْ بِأَسْمَائِهِمْ ۖ فَلَمَّا أَنْبَأَهُمْ بِأَسْمَائِهِمْ قَالَ أَلَمْ أَقُلْ لَكُمْ إِنِّي أَعْلَمُ غَيْبَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ وَأَعْلَمُ مَا تُبْدُونَ وَمَا كُنْتُمْ تَكْتُمُونَ

Allah said, “O Adam! Inform them of their names.” Then when Adam did, Allah said, “Did I not tell you that I know the secrets of the heavens and the earth, and I know what you reveal and what you conceal?”

Allah said, “O Adam, inform them of the names of these things, which they were unable to know.” So when Adam informed them of these names, Allah said to the angels, “I have told you that I know what is hidden from you in the heavens and the earth, and I know what you reveal and what you conceal.”

Allah instructs Adam to reveal the names to the angels. This proves Adam's knowledge and Allah's encompassing awareness of the seen and unseen.

Verse 34

وَإِذْ قُلْنَا لِلْمَلَائِكَةِ اسْجُدُوا لِآدَمَ فَسَجَدُوا إِلَّا إِبْلِيسَ أَبَىٰ وَاسْتَكْبَرَ وَكَانَ مِنَ الْكَافِرِينَ

And ˹remember˺ when We said to the angels, “Prostrate before Adam,” so they all did—but not Iblîs, who refused and acted arrogantly, becoming unfaithful.

And remind - O Messenger - the people of Allah’s honoring of Adam when He, glory be to Him, said to the angels, “Prostrate to Adam as an honor for him and as a manifestation of his superiority.” So they all obeyed except Iblis, who refused to prostrate out of arrogance and envy, thus becoming one of those who disbelieve in Allah and disobey His command.

Allah commanded the angels to prostrate before Adam as a sign of respect. All obeyed except Iblis (Satan), who refused out of arrogance, thus disobeying Allah.

Verse 35

وَقُلْنَا يَا آدَمُ اسْكُنْ أَنْتَ وَزَوْجُكَ الْجَنَّةَ وَكُلَا مِنْهَا رَغَدًا حَيْثُ شِئْتُمَا وَلَا تَقْرَبَا هَٰذِهِ الشَّجَرَةَ فَتَكُونَا مِنَ الظَّالِمِينَ

We cautioned, “O Adam! Live with your wife in Paradise and eat as freely as you please, but do not approach this tree, or else you will be wrongdoers.”

And Allah said, “O Adam, dwell, you and your wife Hawa, in Paradise, and enjoy its fruits with blessed and abundant enjoyment in any place you wish therein. But do not approach this tree, lest you fall into disobedience and become among those who transgress the command of Allah.”

Allah permitted Adam and his wife to dwell in Paradise and enjoy its blessings, except for one specific tree, warning them against disobedience.

Verse 36

فَأَزَلَّهُمَا الشَّيْطَانُ عَنْهَا فَأَخْرَجَهُمَا مِمَّا كَانَا فِيهِ ۖ وَقُلْنَا اهْبِطُوا بَعْضُكُمْ لِبَعْضٍ عَدُوٌّ ۖ وَلَكُمْ فِي الْأَرْضِ مُسْتَقَرٌّ وَمَتَاعٌ إِلَىٰ حِينٍ

But Satan deceived them—leading to their fall from the ˹blissful˺ state they were in, and We said, “Descend from the heavens ˹to the earth˺ as enemies to each other. You will find in the earth a residence and provision for your appointed stay.”

So Satan caused them to fall into sin: by whispering to them until they ate from the tree, thus causing their expulsion from Paradise and its bliss. And Allah said to them, “Descend to the earth, enemies to one another - that is, Adam, Hawa, and Satan - and on the earth you will have settlement, habitation, and benefit from what is in it until the end of your terms.”

Satan deceived Adam and his wife, leading to their expulsion from Paradise. They were sent to Earth, where they would live as enemies, with their life span and provisions determined.

Verse 37

فَتَلَقَّىٰ آدَمُ مِنْ رَبِّهِ كَلِمَاتٍ فَتَابَ عَلَيْهِ ۚ إِنَّهُ هُوَ التَّوَّابُ الرَّحِيمُ

Then Adam was inspired with words ˹of prayer˺ by his Lord, so He accepted his repentance. Surely He is the Accepter of Repentance, Most Merciful.

Then Adam received with acceptance words that Allah inspired him with as repentance and seeking forgiveness, which are His words: {Our Lord, we have wronged ourselves, and if You do not forgive us and have mercy on us, we will surely be among the losers. (7:23)} So Allah turned to him in forgiveness and forgave his sin. Indeed, He, the Exalted, is the Oft-Returning in forgiveness to those of His servants who repent, the Merciful towards them.

Adam repented to Allah with sincere words he was inspired with, and Allah accepted his repentance. Allah is the ultimate accepter of repentance and the most merciful.

Verse 38

قُلْنَا اهْبِطُوا مِنْهَا جَمِيعًا ۖ فَإِمَّا يَأْتِيَنَّكُمْ مِنِّي هُدًى فَمَنْ تَبِعَ هُدَايَ فَلَا خَوْفٌ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا هُمْ يَحْزَنُونَ

We said, “Descend all of you! Then when guidance comes to you from Me, whoever follows it, there will be no fear for them, nor will they grieve.

Allah said to them: Descend from Paradise all of you, and there will come to you and your successive offspring what guides you to the truth. So whoever acts upon it, there will be no fear for them concerning what they will encounter in the Hereafter, nor will they grieve for what they have missed of worldly matters.

Allah instructs humanity to descend from Paradise, promising guidance. Those who follow this guidance will have no fear or grief in the Hereafter.

Verse 39

وَالَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا وَكَذَّبُوا بِآيَاتِنَا أُولَٰئِكَ أَصْحَابُ النَّارِ ۖ هُمْ فِيهَا خَالِدُونَ

But those who disbelieve and deny Our signs will be the residents of the Fire. They will be there forever.”

And those who disbelieved and denied Our recited verses and the proofs of Our Oneness, those are the ones who will abide in the Fire; they will remain therein eternally, never to depart from it.

Those who disbelieve and deny Allah's signs will be inhabitants of the Fire eternally.

Verse 40

يَا بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ اذْكُرُوا نِعْمَتِيَ الَّتِي أَنْعَمْتُ عَلَيْكُمْ وَأَوْفُوا بِعَهْدِي أُوفِ بِعَهْدِكُمْ وَإِيَّايَ فَارْهَبُونِ

O children of Israel! Remember My favours upon you. Fulfil your covenant and I will fulfil Mine, and stand in awe of Me ˹alone˺.

O Children of Jacob, remember My abundant blessings upon you, and be grateful to Me, and fulfill My covenant with you: that you believe in all My books and messengers, and act upon My laws. If you do that, I will fulfill for you what I have promised you of mercy in this world, and salvation in the Hereafter. And Me - alone - fear, and beware of My retribution if you break the covenant and disbelieve in Me.

Allah reminds the Children of Israel of His favors and calls them to fulfill their covenant with Him, promising blessings in return and warning them to fear Him alone.

Verse 41

وَآمِنُوا بِمَا أَنْزَلْتُ مُصَدِّقًا لِمَا مَعَكُمْ وَلَا تَكُونُوا أَوَّلَ كَافِرٍ بِهِ ۖ وَلَا تَشْتَرُوا بِآيَاتِي ثَمَنًا قَلِيلًا وَإِيَّايَ فَاتَّقُونِ

Believe in My revelations which confirm your Scriptures. Do not be the first to deny them or trade them for a fleeting gain. And be mindful of Me.

And believe - O Children of Israel - in the Quran which I have sent down upon Muhammad, the Prophet and Messenger of Allah, which is in agreement with what you know of the correct Torah, and do not be the first group among the People of the Book to disbelieve in it, and do not exchange My verses for a paltry price of the fleeting worldly possessions, and Me alone, obey Me and abandon disobeying Me.

The Children of Israel are urged to believe in the Quran, which confirms their scriptures, and not to reject it for worldly gains.

Verse 42

وَلَا تَلْبِسُوا الْحَقَّ بِالْبَاطِلِ وَتَكْتُمُوا الْحَقَّ وَأَنْتُمْ تَعْلَمُونَ

Do not mix truth with falsehood or hide the truth knowingly.

And do not mix the truth that I have clarified for you with the falsehood that you have fabricated, and beware of concealing the clear truth of the description of the Prophet and Messenger of Allah, Muhammad, peace be upon him, which is in your books, and you find it written with you, in what you know of the books in your hands.

This verse warns against mixing truth with falsehood and knowingly concealing the truth.

Verse 43

وَأَقِيمُوا الصَّلَاةَ وَآتُوا الزَّكَاةَ وَارْكَعُوا مَعَ الرَّاكِعِينَ

Establish prayer, pay alms-tax, and bow down with those who bow down.

And enter into the religion of Islam: by establishing prayer properly, as the Prophet and Messenger of Allah, Muhammad, peace be upon him, came with it, and give the obligatory charity in the prescribed manner, and be with those who bow down in submission from his nation, peace be upon him.

People are urged to establish prayer, pay the obligatory charity, and join the believers in submission to Allah.

Verse 44

أَتَأْمُرُونَ النَّاسَ بِالْبِرِّ وَتَنْسَوْنَ أَنْفُسَكُمْ وَأَنْتُمْ تَتْلُونَ الْكِتَابَ ۚ أَفَلَا تَعْقِلُونَ

Do you preach righteousness and fail to practice it yourselves, although you read the Scripture? Do you not understand?

How vile is your state and the state of your scholars when you command people to do good, and you abandon yourselves, and do not command yourselves to do the great good, which is Islam, and you recite the Torah, which contains the descriptions of Muhammad, peace be upon him, and the obligation to believe in him!! Do you not use your minds correctly?

This verse questions the hypocrisy of those who preach righteousness but do not practice it themselves, despite knowing the scriptures.

Verse 45

وَاسْتَعِينُوا بِالصَّبْرِ وَالصَّلَاةِ ۚ وَإِنَّهَا لَكَبِيرَةٌ إِلَّا عَلَى الْخَاشِعِينَ

And seek help through patience and prayer. Indeed, it is a burden except for the humble—

And seek help in all your matters through patience in all its forms, and through prayer. And indeed, it is difficult except for the humbly submissive.

People are encouraged to seek help through patience and prayer, which are a burden except for those who are humbly submissive to Allah.

Verse 46

الَّذِينَ يَظُنُّونَ أَنَّهُمْ مُلَاقُو رَبِّهِمْ وَأَنَّهُمْ إِلَيْهِ رَاجِعُونَ

those who are certain that they will meet their Lord and to Him they will return.

Those who fear Allah and hope for what is with Him, and are certain that they will meet their Lord, Exalted is He, after death, and that they will return to Him on the Day of Resurrection for reckoning and recompense.

This verse describes the characteristics of the humbly submissive as those who are certain they will meet their Lord and return to Him.

Verse 47

يَا بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ اذْكُرُوا نِعْمَتِيَ الَّتِي أَنْعَمْتُ عَلَيْكُمْ وَأَنِّي فَضَّلْتُكُمْ عَلَى الْعَالَمِينَ

O Children of Israel! Remember ˹all˺ the favours I granted you and how I honoured you above the others.

O Children of Jacob, remember My abundant blessings upon you, and be grateful to Me for them, and remember that I preferred you over the worlds of your time with the abundance of prophets and the revealed books such as the Torah and the Gospel.

Allah reminds the Children of Israel of the favors He has bestowed upon them, including their preference over others during their time.

Verse 48

وَاتَّقُوا يَوْمًا لَا تَجْزِي نَفْسٌ عَنْ نَفْسٍ شَيْئًا وَلَا يُقْبَلُ مِنْهَا شَفَاعَةٌ وَلَا يُؤْخَذُ مِنْهَا عَدْلٌ وَلَا هُمْ يُنْصَرُونَ

Guard yourselves against the Day on which no soul will be of help to another. No intercession will be accepted, no ransom taken, and no help will be given.

And fear the Day of Resurrection, the day when no one will avail anyone else in the least, and Allah will not accept intercession for the disbelievers, nor will He accept ransom from them, even if it were the wealth of the whole earth, and no one will have the power on that day to step forward to support them and save them from the punishment.

This verse warns about the Day of Judgment, where no one can help another, and neither intercession nor ransom will be accepted for disbelievers.

Verse 49

وَإِذْ نَجَّيْنَاكُمْ مِنْ آلِ فِرْعَوْنَ يَسُومُونَكُمْ سُوءَ الْعَذَابِ يُذَبِّحُونَ أَبْنَاءَكُمْ وَيَسْتَحْيُونَ نِسَاءَكُمْ ۚ وَفِي ذَٰلِكُمْ بَلَاءٌ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ عَظِيمٌ

˹Remember˺ how We delivered you from the people of Pharaoh, who afflicted you with dreadful torment, slaughtering your sons and keeping your women. That was a severe test from your Lord.

And remember Our favor upon you when We saved you from the oppression of Pharaoh and his followers, while they were inflicting on you the worst of torment, slaughtering your sons and leaving your women for servitude and humiliation. And in that was a trial for you from your Lord, and in your deliverance from it was a great blessing, deserving of thanks to Allah Almighty in all your eras and generations.

This verse reminds the Israelites of their deliverance from Pharaoh's oppression, highlighting the severe torment they endured, including the killing of their sons and enslavement of their women. This was a great test from God.

Verse 50

وَإِذْ فَرَقْنَا بِكُمُ الْبَحْرَ فَأَنْجَيْنَاكُمْ وَأَغْرَقْنَا آلَ فِرْعَوْنَ وَأَنْتُمْ تَنْظُرُونَ

And ˹remember˺ when We parted the sea, rescued you, and drowned Pharaoh’s people before your very eyes.

And remember Our favor upon you, when We parted the sea for your sake, and made therein dry paths, so you crossed, and We saved you from Pharaoh and his soldiers, and from perishing in the water. When Pharaoh and his soldiers entered your paths, We destroyed them in the water before your very eyes.

The parting of the sea is recalled as a miraculous event, where God saved the Israelites and drowned Pharaoh's army. This emphasizes God's power and His favor upon the Israelites.

Verse 51

وَإِذْ وَاعَدْنَا مُوسَىٰ أَرْبَعِينَ لَيْلَةً ثُمَّ اتَّخَذْتُمُ الْعِجْلَ مِنْ بَعْدِهِ وَأَنْتُمْ ظَالِمُونَ

And ˹remember˺ when We appointed forty nights for Moses, then you worshipped the calf in his absence, acting wrongfully.

And remember Our favor upon you: when We made an appointment with Moses for forty nights to send down the Torah as guidance and light for you, and you took advantage of his absence during this short period, and made the calf that you made with your own hands an object of worship besides Allah – and this is the most heinous disbelief in Allah – and you were wrongdoers by taking the calf as a god.

This verse refers to the time when Moses was in seclusion for forty nights, and the Israelites worshipped the calf in his absence. This act was a great wrongdoing and an act of disbelief.

Verse 52

ثُمَّ عَفَوْنَا عَنْكُمْ مِنْ بَعْدِ ذَٰلِكَ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَشْكُرُونَ

Even then We ˹still˺ forgave you so perhaps you would be grateful.

Then We overlooked this abominable act, and accepted your repentance after the return of Moses; hoping that you would thank Allah for His blessings and favors, and not persist in disbelief and transgression.

Despite the serious sin of worshipping the calf, God forgave the Israelites, emphasizing His mercy and giving them another chance to be grateful.

Verse 53

وَإِذْ آتَيْنَا مُوسَى الْكِتَابَ وَالْفُرْقَانَ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَهْتَدُونَ

And ˹remember˺ when We gave Moses the Scripture—the standard ˹to distinguish between right and wrong˺ that perhaps you would be ˹rightly˺ guided.

And remember Our favor upon you when We gave Moses the Book that distinguishes between right and wrong - which is the Torah - so that you may be guided from error.

God gave Moses the Scripture (Torah) as a standard to distinguish between right and wrong, so that the Israelites would be guided. This highlights the importance of divine guidance.

Verse 54

وَإِذْ قَالَ مُوسَىٰ لِقَوْمِهِ يَا قَوْمِ إِنَّكُمْ ظَلَمْتُمْ أَنْفُسَكُمْ بِاتِّخَاذِكُمُ الْعِجْلَ فَتُوبُوا إِلَىٰ بَارِئِكُمْ فَاقْتُلُوا أَنْفُسَكُمْ ذَٰلِكُمْ خَيْرٌ لَكُمْ عِنْدَ بَارِئِكُمْ فَتَابَ عَلَيْكُمْ ۚ إِنَّهُ هُوَ التَّوَّابُ الرَّحِيمُ

And ˹remember˺ when Moses said to his people, “O my people! Surely you have wronged yourselves by worshipping the calf, so turn in repentance to your Creator and execute ˹the calf-worshippers among˺ yourselves. That is best for you in the sight of your Creator.” Then He accepted your repentance. Surely He is the Accepter of Repentance, Most Merciful.

And remember Our favor upon you when Moses said to his people: You have wronged yourselves by taking the calf as a god, so repent to your Creator: by killing some of you others, and this is better for you with your Creator than eternal dwelling in the Fire. So you obeyed, and Allah bestowed upon you acceptance of your repentance. Indeed, He is the Acceptor of repentance for those who repent of His servants, the Merciful to them.

Moses instructed his people to repent after worshipping the calf, and the repentance included self-execution of the idolaters. God accepted their repentance and showed His mercy.

Verse 55

وَإِذْ قُلْتُمْ يَا مُوسَىٰ لَنْ نُؤْمِنَ لَكَ حَتَّىٰ نَرَى اللَّهَ جَهْرَةً فَأَخَذَتْكُمُ الصَّاعِقَةُ وَأَنْتُمْ تَنْظُرُونَ

And ˹remember˺ when you said, “O Moses! We will never believe you until we see Allah with our own eyes,” so a thunderbolt struck you while you were looking on.

And remember when you said, O Moses, we will not believe you that the words we hear from you are the words of Allah, until we see Allah with our own eyes, so a fire descended from the sky that you saw with your own eyes, and it killed you because of your sins, and your audacity towards Allah Almighty.

The Israelites audaciously demanded to see God with their own eyes, which resulted in a thunderbolt striking them as a consequence of their disbelief and audacity.

Verse 56

ثُمَّ بَعَثْنَاكُمْ مِنْ بَعْدِ مَوْتِكُمْ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَشْكُرُونَ

Then We brought you back to life after your death, so that perhaps you would be grateful.

Then We revived you after your death by the thunderbolt, so that you may give thanks for the favor of Allah upon you. This death was a punishment for them, then Allah resurrected them to fulfill their appointed times.

God then brought them back to life after the thunderbolt, as a reminder of His power over life and death, and so that they might be grateful.

Verse 57

وَظَلَّلْنَا عَلَيْكُمُ الْغَمَامَ وَأَنْزَلْنَا عَلَيْكُمُ الْمَنَّ وَالسَّلْوَىٰ ۖ كُلُوا مِنْ طَيِّبَاتِ مَا رَزَقْنَاكُمْ ۖ وَمَا ظَلَمُونَا وَلَٰكِنْ كَانُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ يَظْلِمُونَ

And ˹remember when˺ We shaded you with clouds and sent down to you manna and quails, ˹saying˺, “Eat from the good things We have provided for you.” The evildoers ˹certainly˺ did not wrong Us, but wronged themselves.

And remember Our favor upon you when you were wandering in the land; as We made the clouds a shade over you from the heat of the sun, and We sent down upon you manna, which is something like gum, tasting like honey, and We sent down upon you quail, which is a bird resembling quail, and We said to you, eat from the good things We have provided you with, and do not violate your religion, but you did not comply. They did not wrong Us by being ungrateful for the blessings, but they were wronging themselves because the consequence of wrongdoing returns to them.

During their wandering, God provided shade with clouds and sent down manna and quails for the Israelites to eat, yet they still disobeyed. They wronged themselves, not God, through their ingratitude.

Verse 58

وَإِذْ قُلْنَا ادْخُلُوا هَٰذِهِ الْقَرْيَةَ فَكُلُوا مِنْهَا حَيْثُ شِئْتُمْ رَغَدًا وَادْخُلُوا الْبَابَ سُجَّدًا وَقُولُوا حِطَّةٌ نَغْفِرْ لَكُمْ خَطَايَاكُمْ ۚ وَسَنَزِيدُ الْمُحْسِنِينَ

And ˹remember˺ when We said, “Enter this city and eat freely from wherever you please; enter the gate with humility, saying, ‘Absolve us.’ We will forgive your sins and multiply the reward for the good-doers.”

And remember Our favor upon you when We said, "Enter this city, 'Jerusalem,' and eat from its good things from wherever you wish, and be submissive to Allah, humbled to Him in your entry, and say: Our Lord, remove our sins from us, We will respond to you and forgive them and conceal them from you, and We will increase the good-doers with good and reward for their deeds."

This verse recalls Allah's command for the Children of Israel to enter a city (Jerusalem), eat freely, and ask for forgiveness with humility. This act of obedience would lead to the forgiveness of their sins and increased reward for the righteous.

Verse 59

فَبَدَّلَ الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا قَوْلًا غَيْرَ الَّذِي قِيلَ لَهُمْ فَأَنْزَلْنَا عَلَى الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا رِجْزًا مِنَ السَّمَاءِ بِمَا كَانُوا يَفْسُقُونَ

But the wrongdoers changed the words they were commanded to say. So We sent down a punishment from the heavens upon them for their rebelliousness.

Then the unjust and misguided from the Children of Israel changed the word of Allah, and distorted the word and the deed all together, when they entered dragging on their backsides and said: A grain in a hair, and they mocked the religion of Allah. So Allah sent down upon them a punishment from the sky; because of their rebellion and their disobedience to Allah.

However, the wrongdoers among them disobeyed by changing the words they were instructed to say. This defiance resulted in divine punishment as a consequence of their rebellion.

Verse 60

وَإِذِ اسْتَسْقَىٰ مُوسَىٰ لِقَوْمِهِ فَقُلْنَا اضْرِبْ بِعَصَاكَ الْحَجَرَ ۖ فَانْفَجَرَتْ مِنْهُ اثْنَتَا عَشْرَةَ عَيْنًا ۖ قَدْ عَلِمَ كُلُّ أُنَاسٍ مَشْرَبَهُمْ ۖ كُلُوا وَاشْرَبُوا مِنْ رِزْقِ اللَّهِ وَلَا تَعْثَوْا فِي الْأَرْضِ مُفْسِدِينَ

And ˹remember˺ when Moses prayed for water for his people, We said, “Strike the rock with your staff.” Then twelve springs gushed out, ˹and˺ each tribe knew its drinking place. ˹We then said,˺ “Eat and drink of Allah’s provisions, and do not go about spreading corruption in the land.”

And remember Our favor upon you - while you were thirsty in the wilderness - when Moses called upon Us - with supplication - to give his people drink, so We said: Strike the stone with your staff, and he struck, and twelve springs burst forth from it, according to the number of tribes, with each tribe being informed of their specific spring so that they would not dispute. And We said to them: Eat and drink from the provision of Allah, and do not seek to cause corruption on the earth.

This verse recounts the miracle of water provision for the Israelites through Moses. When they were thirsty in the wilderness, Moses struck a rock with his staff, and twelve springs gushed forth. The verse advises them to be grateful and avoid causing corruption on earth.

Verse 61

وَإِذْ قُلْتُمْ يَا مُوسَىٰ لَنْ نَصْبِرَ عَلَىٰ طَعَامٍ وَاحِدٍ فَادْعُ لَنَا رَبَّكَ يُخْرِجْ لَنَا مِمَّا تُنْبِتُ الْأَرْضُ مِنْ بَقْلِهَا وَقِثَّائِهَا وَفُومِهَا وَعَدَسِهَا وَبَصَلِهَا ۖ قَالَ أَتَسْتَبْدِلُونَ الَّذِي هُوَ أَدْنَىٰ بِالَّذِي هُوَ خَيْرٌ ۚ اهْبِطُوا مِصْرًا فَإِنَّ لَكُمْ مَا سَأَلْتُمْ ۗ وَضُرِبَتْ عَلَيْهِمُ الذِّلَّةُ وَالْمَسْكَنَةُ وَبَاءُوا بِغَضَبٍ مِنَ اللَّهِ ۗ ذَٰلِكَ بِأَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا يَكْفُرُونَ بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ وَيَقْتُلُونَ النَّبِيِّينَ بِغَيْرِ الْحَقِّ ۗ ذَٰلِكَ بِمَا عَصَوْا وَكَانُوا يَعْتَدُونَ

And ˹remember˺ when you said, “O Moses! We cannot endure the same meal ˹every day˺. So ˹just˺ call upon your Lord on our behalf, He will bring forth for us some of what the earth produces of herbs, cucumbers, garlic, lentils, and onions.” Moses scolded ˹them˺, “Do you exchange what is better for what is worse? ˹You can˺ go down to any village and you will find what you have asked for.” They were stricken with disgrace and misery, and they invited the displeasure of Allah for rejecting Allah’s signs and unjustly killing the prophets. This is ˹a fair reward˺ for their disobedience and violations.

And remember when We sent down upon you sweet food and delicious birds, but you grew ungrateful of the favor, as was your custom, and you were afflicted with distress and boredom, so you said: O Moses, we cannot endure one kind of food that does not change with the days, so pray to your Lord for us to bring forth from the earth's plants food of herbs, cucumbers, grains that are eaten, lentils, and onions. Moses said – disapproving of them –: Do you seek these foods that are of less value, and leave this beneficial provision that Allah has chosen for you? Go down from this wilderness to any city, you will find much of what you desire in the fields and markets. And when they went down, it became clear to them that they prioritize their choice – in every instance – over Allah's choice, and they prefer their desires over what Allah has chosen for them; therefore, they were afflicted with humiliation and poverty of souls, and they went back with anger from Allah; because of their turning away from the religion of Allah, and because they used to disbelieve in the signs of Allah and kill the prophets unjustly and transgressively; and that was due to their disobedience and exceeding the limits of their Lord.

The Children of Israel, despite receiving manna and quail, complained about the lack of variety in their diet. They asked Moses to pray for different foods. Moses rebuked them for preferring lesser provisions over the blessings they had received. They were ultimately afflicted with disgrace and misery for their ingratitude and disobedience.

Verse 62

إِنَّ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَالَّذِينَ هَادُوا وَالنَّصَارَىٰ وَالصَّابِئِينَ مَنْ آمَنَ بِاللَّهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ وَعَمِلَ صَالِحًا فَلَهُمْ أَجْرُهُمْ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ وَلَا خَوْفٌ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا هُمْ يَحْزَنُونَ

Indeed, the believers, Jews, Christians, and Sabians—whoever ˹truly˺ believes in Allah and the Last Day and does good will have their reward with their Lord. And there will be no fear for them, nor will they grieve.

Indeed, those who believe from this nation, who have believed in Allah and His messengers, and acted according to His law, and those who were before the mission of Muhammad, peace be upon him, from the previous nations of Jews, Christians, and Sabians - and they are a people remaining on their innate nature, and no established religion for them to follow - all of these, if they believe in Allah with a correct and sincere belief, and in the Day of Resurrection and recompense, and do deeds pleasing to Allah, then their reward is established for them with their Lord, and there is no fear for them in what they will face in the Hereafter, nor will they grieve over what they have missed in the affairs of this world. As for after the mission of Muhammad, peace be upon him, as the seal of the prophets and messengers to all people, Allah will not accept from anyone any religion other than what he brought, which is Islam.

This verse explains that salvation is based on sincere belief in Allah and the Last Day, coupled with righteous actions. This principle applies to believers and those of other faiths before the advent of Islam. After Prophet Muhammad (PBUH), Islam became the only acceptable path.

Verse 63

وَإِذْ أَخَذْنَا مِيثَاقَكُمْ وَرَفَعْنَا فَوْقَكُمُ الطُّورَ خُذُوا مَا آتَيْنَاكُمْ بِقُوَّةٍ وَاذْكُرُوا مَا فِيهِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَتَّقُونَ

And ˹remember˺ when We took a covenant from you and raised the mountain above you ˹saying˺, “Hold firmly to that ˹Scripture˺ which We have given you and observe its teachings so perhaps you will become mindful ˹of Allah˺.”

And remember - O Children of Israel - when We took a firm covenant from you to believe in Allah and single Him out for worship, and We raised the Mount of Tur above you, and We said to you: Take the Book which We have given you with seriousness and diligence, and preserve it, or else We will drop the mountain upon you, and do not forget the Torah, in word and deed, so that you may fear Me and fear My punishment.

This verse reminds the Children of Israel of the covenant they made with Allah. They were commanded to adhere firmly to the Scripture (Torah) and its teachings, symbolized by the raising of Mount Tur above them, emphasizing the seriousness of their commitment.

Verse 64

ثُمَّ تَوَلَّيْتُمْ مِنْ بَعْدِ ذَٰلِكَ ۖ فَلَوْلَا فَضْلُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكُمْ وَرَحْمَتُهُ لَكُنْتُمْ مِنَ الْخَاسِرِينَ

Yet you turned away afterwards. Had it not been for Allah’s grace and mercy upon you, you would have certainly been of the losers.

Then you disobeyed and rebelled again, after taking the covenant and raising the mountain, as is always your way. Were it not for the favor of Allah upon you and His mercy by accepting repentance, and overlooking your sins, you would have been among the losers in this world and the Hereafter.

This verse highlights the Israelites' disobedience after their covenant with Allah. It notes that their salvation is due to Allah's grace and mercy. Without this divine mercy, they would have faced losses in this world and the Hereafter.

Verse 65

وَلَقَدْ عَلِمْتُمُ الَّذِينَ اعْتَدَوْا مِنْكُمْ فِي السَّبْتِ فَقُلْنَا لَهُمْ كُونُوا قِرَدَةً خَاسِئِينَ

You are already aware of those of you who broke the Sabbath. We said to them, “Be disgraced apes!”

And you have known - O company of Jews - what harm befell your ancestors from the people of the town that disobeyed Allah, concerning what He had taken upon them of honoring the Sabbath, so they schemed to catch fish on the Sabbath, by placing nets and digging ponds, then they caught the fish on Sunday as a trick to what was forbidden. When they did that, Allah transformed them into despised apes.

This verse recounts the story of those who violated the Sabbath. As punishment for their deceitful actions, Allah transformed them into disgraced apes, serving as a warning for others.

Verse 66

فَجَعَلْنَاهَا نَكَالًا لِمَا بَيْنَ يَدَيْهَا وَمَا خَلْفَهَا وَمَوْعِظَةً لِلْمُتَّقِينَ

So We made their fate an example to present and future generations, and a lesson to the God-fearing.

So We made this town an example for those in its vicinity from the towns, conveying to them its news and what befell it, and an example for those who commit such sins after it, and We made it a reminder for the righteous, so that they may know that they are on the truth, and remain firm upon it.

The fate of those who violated the Sabbath serves as a lesson and a deterrent to present and future generations. It's a reminder of the consequences of disobeying Allah’s commands and a reminder for the God-fearing.

Verse 67

وَإِذْ قَالَ مُوسَىٰ لِقَوْمِهِ إِنَّ اللَّهَ يَأْمُرُكُمْ أَنْ تَذْبَحُوا بَقَرَةً ۖ قَالُوا أَتَتَّخِذُنَا هُزُوًا ۖ قَالَ أَعُوذُ بِاللَّهِ أَنْ أَكُونَ مِنَ الْجَاهِلِينَ

And ˹remember˺ when Moses said to his people, “Allah commands you to sacrifice a cow.” They replied, “Are you mocking us?” Moses responded, “I seek refuge in Allah from acting foolishly!”

And remember, O Children of Israel, the crime of your forefathers, and their frequent stubbornness and arguing with Moses, peace be upon him, when he said to them: 'Indeed, Allah commands you to slaughter a cow.' So they said - arrogantly -: 'Do you make us a subject of mockery and trivialization?' So Moses replied to them, saying: 'I seek refuge in Allah from being among the mockers.'

This verse tells of Prophet Musa (Moses) relaying Allah's command to sacrifice a cow. The Children of Israel responded with disbelief and mockery, which Musa rejected, seeking refuge in Allah.

Verse 68

قَالُوا ادْعُ لَنَا رَبَّكَ يُبَيِّنْ لَنَا مَا هِيَ ۚ قَالَ إِنَّهُ يَقُولُ إِنَّهَا بَقَرَةٌ لَا فَارِضٌ وَلَا بِكْرٌ عَوَانٌ بَيْنَ ذَٰلِكَ ۖ فَافْعَلُوا مَا تُؤْمَرُونَ

They said, “Call upon your Lord to clarify for us what type ˹of cow˺ it should be!” He replied, “Allah says, ‘The cow should neither be old nor young but in between. So do as you are commanded!’”

They said: 'Call upon your Lord to make clear to us the description of this cow.' So he answered them: 'Indeed, Allah says to you: Its description is that it should not be an old and senile one, nor a small and young one, but rather, it is of an intermediate age between the two. So hasten to comply with the command of your Lord.'

This verse describes how the Israelites attempted to delay following Allah's order by asking for details about the cow. Allah responded that the cow should be neither old nor young, but an intermediate age.

Verse 69

قَالُوا ادْعُ لَنَا رَبَّكَ يُبَيِّنْ لَنَا مَا لَوْنُهَا ۚ قَالَ إِنَّهُ يَقُولُ إِنَّهَا بَقَرَةٌ صَفْرَاءُ فَاقِعٌ لَوْنُهَا تَسُرُّ النَّاظِرِينَ

They said, “Call upon your Lord to specify for us its colour.” He replied, “Allah says, ‘It should be a bright yellow cow—pleasant to see.’”

They returned to their arguing, saying: 'Call upon your Lord to make clear to us its color.' He said: 'He says: It is a yellow cow, intensely yellow in color, pleasing to those who look at it.'

The Israelites continued to seek more details about the cow, questioning its color. Allah specified that the cow should be a bright yellow, pleasing to look at.

Verse 70

قَالُوا ادْعُ لَنَا رَبَّكَ يُبَيِّنْ لَنَا مَا هِيَ إِنَّ الْبَقَرَ تَشَابَهَ عَلَيْنَا وَإِنَّا إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ لَمُهْتَدُونَ

Again they said, “Call upon your Lord so that He may make clear to us which cow, for all cows look the same to us. Then, Allah willing, we will be guided ˹to the right one˺.”

The Children of Israel said to Moses, "Call upon your Lord for us to clarify for us other characteristics than what has been mentioned before; because the cows—with these characteristics—are many, and it has become confusing for us what to choose? And indeed, we—if Allah wills—will be guided to the cow that is ordered to be slaughtered."

The Israelites asked for more details about the cow to be sacrificed, as they were confused by the initial description. They requested that Allah guide them to the correct cow.

Verse 71

قَالَ إِنَّهُ يَقُولُ إِنَّهَا بَقَرَةٌ لَا ذَلُولٌ تُثِيرُ الْأَرْضَ وَلَا تَسْقِي الْحَرْثَ مُسَلَّمَةٌ لَا شِيَةَ فِيهَا ۚ قَالُوا الْآنَ جِئْتَ بِالْحَقِّ ۚ فَذَبَحُوهَا وَمَا كَادُوا يَفْعَلُونَ

He replied, “Allah says, ‘It should have been used neither to till the soil nor water the fields; wholesome and without blemish.’” They said, “Now you have come with the truth.” Yet they still slaughtered it hesitantly!

Moses said to them, "Allah says, 'It is a cow not trained to work in plowing the land for agriculture, nor prepared to draw water from the well, and free from all defects, and without any mark of color other than the color of its skin.'" They said, "Now you have come with the true description of the cow." So, they were forced to slaughter it after much evasion, and they almost did not do that because of their stubbornness. Thus, they made it difficult, so Allah made it difficult for them.

Moses clarified that the cow should be one that hasn't been used for farming, is healthy, and has no blemishes. Despite this clear description, they hesitated to slaughter the cow.

Verse 72

وَإِذْ قَتَلْتُمْ نَفْسًا فَادَّارَأْتُمْ فِيهَا ۖ وَاللَّهُ مُخْرِجٌ مَا كُنْتُمْ تَكْتُمُونَ

˹This is˺ when a man was killed and you disputed who the killer was, but Allah revealed what you concealed.

And remember when you killed a soul, and you disputed about it, each one pushing away the accusation of murder from himself, and Allah was to bring out what you were concealing of the killing of the slain.

This verse refers to a murder case where the identity of the killer was disputed among the Israelites, but Allah was aware of the truth.

Verse 73

فَقُلْنَا اضْرِبُوهُ بِبَعْضِهَا ۚ كَذَٰلِكَ يُحْيِي اللَّهُ الْمَوْتَىٰ وَيُرِيكُمْ آيَاتِهِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَعْقِلُونَ

So We instructed, “Strike the dead body with a piece of the cow.” This is how ˹easily˺ Allah brings the dead to life, showing you His signs so that you may understand.

So We said, "Strike the slain with a part of this slaughtered cow, and Allah will resurrect him alive, and he will inform you about his killer." So they struck him with part of it, and Allah brought him to life and he informed about his killer. Thus, Allah brings the dead to life on the Day of Resurrection, and shows you—O Children of Israel—His miracles that indicate the perfection of His ability, may He be exalted; so that you may ponder with your minds, and refrain from His disobedience.

Allah instructed that a piece of the sacrificed cow be used to strike the dead man, bringing him back to life to reveal his killer. This showed the power of Allah to resurrect the dead.

Verse 74

ثُمَّ قَسَتْ قُلُوبُكُمْ مِنْ بَعْدِ ذَٰلِكَ فَهِيَ كَالْحِجَارَةِ أَوْ أَشَدُّ قَسْوَةً ۚ وَإِنَّ مِنَ الْحِجَارَةِ لَمَا يَتَفَجَّرُ مِنْهُ الْأَنْهَارُ ۚ وَإِنَّ مِنْهَا لَمَا يَشَّقَّقُ فَيَخْرُجُ مِنْهُ الْمَاءُ ۚ وَإِنَّ مِنْهَا لَمَا يَهْبِطُ مِنْ خَشْيَةِ اللَّهِ ۗ وَمَا اللَّهُ بِغَافِلٍ عَمَّا تَعْمَلُونَ

Even then your hearts became hardened like a rock or even harder, for some rocks gush rivers; others split, spilling water; while others are humbled in awe of Allah. And Allah is never unaware of what you do.

But you did not benefit from that; for after all these extraordinary miracles, your hearts hardened and thickened, so no good penetrated them, and they did not soften in front of the clear signs that I showed you, until your hearts became like deaf stones, or even harder; because among the stones are some that widen and open up until water pours from them, becoming flowing rivers, and among the stones are those that crack and split, and springs and fountains come out of them, and among the stones are those that fall from the tops of the mountains out of fear of Allah, may He be exalted, and glorifying Him. And Allah is not unaware of what you do.

Despite the miracles they witnessed, the hearts of the Israelites hardened. Some rocks are softer than their hearts, as they can split open to form rivers, springs, or crumble in awe of Allah.

Verse 75

أَفَتَطْمَعُونَ أَنْ يُؤْمِنُوا لَكُمْ وَقَدْ كَانَ فَرِيقٌ مِنْهُمْ يَسْمَعُونَ كَلَامَ اللَّهِ ثُمَّ يُحَرِّفُونَهُ مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا عَقَلُوهُ وَهُمْ يَعْلَمُونَ

Do you ˹believers still˺ expect them to be true to you, though a group of them would hear the word of Allah then knowingly corrupt it after understanding it?

O Muslims, have you forgotten the deeds of the Children of Israel, so your souls have become eager that the Jews would believe in your religion? And their scholars used to hear the word of Allah from the Torah, then they would distort it by diverting it to other than its correct meaning after they had understood its reality, or by distorting its words, while they knew that they were deliberately and falsely distorting the words of the Lord of the worlds.

This verse questions whether believers should expect truthfulness from the Israelites, given their history of knowingly distorting the word of Allah after understanding it.

Verse 76

وَإِذَا لَقُوا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا قَالُوا آمَنَّا وَإِذَا خَلَا بَعْضُهُمْ إِلَىٰ بَعْضٍ قَالُوا أَتُحَدِّثُونَهُمْ بِمَا فَتَحَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْكُمْ لِيُحَاجُّوكُمْ بِهِ عِنْدَ رَبِّكُمْ ۚ أَفَلَا تَعْقِلُونَ

When they meet the believers they say, “We believe.” But in private they say ˹to each other˺, “Will you disclose to the believers the knowledge Allah has revealed to you, so that they may use it against you before your Lord? Do you not understand?”

These Jews, when they meet those who have believed, they say with their tongues, “We have believed in your religion and your messenger who is foretold in the Torah.” And when some of these hypocrites among the Jews are alone with others, they say in denial: “Do you tell the believers what Allah has made clear to you in the Torah about Muhammad, so that it may be a proof against you before your Lord on the Day of Resurrection? Do you not understand so that you may beware?”

The Israelites would claim to believe when they met the believers, but in private, they would fear disclosing their knowledge of their scriptures to the believers, lest they use it against them before God.

Verse 77

أَوَلَا يَعْلَمُونَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ يَعْلَمُ مَا يُسِرُّونَ وَمَا يُعْلِنُونَ

Do they not know that Allah is aware of what they conceal and what they reveal?

Do they commit all these crimes, and do they not know that Allah knows all that they conceal and what they reveal?

This verse questions whether people are unaware that Allah knows everything, both hidden and revealed, emphasizing His complete knowledge of all actions and intentions.

Verse 78

وَمِنْهُمْ أُمِّيُّونَ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ الْكِتَابَ إِلَّا أَمَانِيَّ وَإِنْ هُمْ إِلَّا يَظُنُّونَ

And among them are the illiterate who know nothing about the Scripture except lies, and ˹so˺ they ˹wishfully˺ speculate.

And among the Jews are a group who are ignorant of reading and writing, and they do not know the Torah and what it contains of the attributes of the Prophet of Allah and His Messenger Muhammad, may Allah bless him and grant him peace, and what they have of that is nothing but falsehoods and corrupt assumptions.

This verse highlights that some among the Jews are illiterate and are unaware of the true scriptures, relying on falsehoods and speculation instead.

Verse 79

فَوَيْلٌ لِلَّذِينَ يَكْتُبُونَ الْكِتَابَ بِأَيْدِيهِمْ ثُمَّ يَقُولُونَ هَٰذَا مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ لِيَشْتَرُوا بِهِ ثَمَنًا قَلِيلًا ۖ فَوَيْلٌ لَهُمْ مِمَّا كَتَبَتْ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَوَيْلٌ لَهُمْ مِمَّا يَكْسِبُونَ

So woe to those who distort the Scripture with their own hands then say, “This is from Allah”—seeking a fleeting gain! So woe to them for what their hands have written, and woe to them for what they have earned.

So, destruction and severe warning are for the evil rabbis of the Jews who write the scripture with their own hands, then say, 'This is from Allah,' while it contradicts what Allah revealed to His Prophet Moses, peace be upon him, in order to take in return for this the fleeting gains of the world. So, for them is a destructive punishment because of their writing this falsehood with their own hands, and for them is a destructive punishment because of what they take in return of unlawful money, such as bribery and other things.

This verse warns those who distort the scriptures for personal gain. It condemns their actions and the false claims they make about God's word.

Verse 80

وَقَالُوا لَنْ تَمَسَّنَا النَّارُ إِلَّا أَيَّامًا مَعْدُودَةً ۚ قُلْ أَتَّخَذْتُمْ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ عَهْدًا فَلَنْ يُخْلِفَ اللَّهُ عَهْدَهُ ۖ أَمْ تَقُولُونَ عَلَى اللَّهِ مَا لَا تَعْلَمُونَ

˹Some of˺ the Jews claim, “The Fire will not touch us except for a number of days.” Say, ˹O Prophet,˺ “Have you taken a pledge from Allah—for Allah never breaks His word—or are you ˹just˺ saying about Allah what you do not know?”

And the Children of Israel said, “The Fire will not touch us except for a few days.” Say to them, O Messenger, refuting their claim, “Have you taken a covenant from Allah regarding this? For Allah never breaks His covenant. Rather, you are saying about Allah that which you do not know, by fabricating lies.”

This verse refutes the Jews' claim that they will only be in Hell for a short time, asking if they have a covenant from Allah or are simply making false claims.

Verse 81

بَلَىٰ مَنْ كَسَبَ سَيِّئَةً وَأَحَاطَتْ بِهِ خَطِيئَتُهُ فَأُولَٰئِكَ أَصْحَابُ النَّارِ ۖ هُمْ فِيهَا خَالِدُونَ

But no! Those who commit evil and are engrossed in sin will be the residents of the Fire. They will be there forever.

So, the ruling of Allah is established: that whoever commits sins until they drag him into disbelief, and his sins overwhelm him from all sides, and this only occurs to those who associate partners with Allah, then the polytheists and the disbelievers are the ones who will remain in Hellfire, permanently without interruption.

This verse clarifies that those who commit evil and are engulfed by sin will be residents of Hellfire eternally.

Verse 82

وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ أُولَٰئِكَ أَصْحَابُ الْجَنَّةِ ۖ هُمْ فِيهَا خَالِدُونَ

And those who believe and do good will be the residents of Paradise. They will be there forever.

And the established ruling of Allah in contrast to this: that those who sincerely believed in Allah and His messengers, and did righteous deeds in accordance with the law of Allah that He revealed to His messengers, these will remain in Paradise in the Hereafter, permanently without interruption.

This verse contrasts the previous one, stating that those who believe and do good will reside in Paradise forever.

Verse 83

وَإِذْ أَخَذْنَا مِيثَاقَ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ لَا تَعْبُدُونَ إِلَّا اللَّهَ وَبِالْوَالِدَيْنِ إِحْسَانًا وَذِي الْقُرْبَىٰ وَالْيَتَامَىٰ وَالْمَسَاكِينِ وَقُولُوا لِلنَّاسِ حُسْنًا وَأَقِيمُوا الصَّلَاةَ وَآتُوا الزَّكَاةَ ثُمَّ تَوَلَّيْتُمْ إِلَّا قَلِيلًا مِنْكُمْ وَأَنْتُمْ مُعْرِضُونَ

And ˹remember˺ when We took a covenant from the children of Israel ˹stating˺, “Worship none but Allah; be kind to parents, relatives, orphans and the needy; speak kindly to people; establish prayer; and pay alms-tax.” But you ˹Israelites˺ turned away—except for a few of you—and were indifferent.

And remember, O Children of Israel, when We took a confirmed covenant from you: that you should worship Allah alone, without any partners, and that you should treat parents kindly, and relatives, and the orphans, and the needy, and speak to people kind words, while establishing prayer and giving charity, then you turned away and broke the covenant - except a few of you who remained steadfast to it - and you are continuously turning away.

This verse reminds the Children of Israel of the covenant they made with Allah to worship Him alone, be kind, and establish prayer but then they turned away.

Verse 84

وَإِذْ أَخَذْنَا مِيثَاقَكُمْ لَا تَسْفِكُونَ دِمَاءَكُمْ وَلَا تُخْرِجُونَ أَنْفُسَكُمْ مِنْ دِيَارِكُمْ ثُمَّ أَقْرَرْتُمْ وَأَنْتُمْ تَشْهَدُونَ

And ˹remember˺ when We took your covenant that you would neither shed each other’s blood nor expel each other from their homes, you gave your pledge and bore witness.

And remember, O Children of Israel, when We took a firm covenant from you in the Torah: you shall not shed each other's blood, nor expel one another from your homes. Then you acknowledged it, and you were witnesses to it.

This verse reminds the Children of Israel of their covenant with God, which included not harming one another or expelling each other from their homes. They acknowledged this covenant.

Verse 85

ثُمَّ أَنْتُمْ هَٰؤُلَاءِ تَقْتُلُونَ أَنْفُسَكُمْ وَتُخْرِجُونَ فَرِيقًا مِنْكُمْ مِنْ دِيَارِهِمْ تَظَاهَرُونَ عَلَيْهِمْ بِالْإِثْمِ وَالْعُدْوَانِ وَإِنْ يَأْتُوكُمْ أُسَارَىٰ تُفَادُوهُمْ وَهُوَ مُحَرَّمٌ عَلَيْكُمْ إِخْرَاجُهُمْ ۚ أَفَتُؤْمِنُونَ بِبَعْضِ الْكِتَابِ وَتَكْفُرُونَ بِبَعْضٍ ۚ فَمَا جَزَاءُ مَنْ يَفْعَلُ ذَٰلِكَ مِنْكُمْ إِلَّا خِزْيٌ فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا ۖ وَيَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ يُرَدُّونَ إِلَىٰ أَشَدِّ الْعَذَابِ ۗ وَمَا اللَّهُ بِغَافِلٍ عَمَّا تَعْمَلُونَ

But here you are, killing each other and expelling some of your people from their homes, aiding one another in sin and aggression; and when those ˹expelled˺ come to you as captives, you still ransom them—though expelling them was unlawful for you. Do you believe in some of the Scripture and reject the rest? Is there any reward for those who do so among you other than disgrace in this worldly life and being subjected to the harshest punishment on the Day of Judgment? For Allah is never unaware of what you do.

Yet, you are those who kill one another and expel a group of you from their homes, supporting one another against each other with sin and aggression. And if they come to you as captives in the hands of the enemy, you hasten to ransom them, even though it was forbidden for you to expel them from their homes. How evil is what you do when you believe in part of the Torah and disbelieve in part! The recompense for those who do this among you is nothing but disgrace in this worldly life. And on the Day of Resurrection, Allah will return them to the most severe punishment in the Fire. And Allah is not unaware of what you do.

Despite their covenant, the Children of Israel violated it by killing and expelling each other. They even ransomed their captured brethren while simultaneously engaging in aggression, displaying selective adherence to their scriptures and facing disgrace in this life and severe punishment in the Hereafter. This verse highlights their hypocrisy.

Verse 86

أُولَٰئِكَ الَّذِينَ اشْتَرَوُا الْحَيَاةَ الدُّنْيَا بِالْآخِرَةِ ۖ فَلَا يُخَفَّفُ عَنْهُمُ الْعَذَابُ وَلَا هُمْ يُنْصَرُونَ

These are the ones who trade the Hereafter for the life of this world. So their punishment will not be reduced, nor will they be helped.

Those are the ones who have preferred the worldly life over the Hereafter, so the punishment will not be lightened for them, and they will have no helper to save them from the punishment of Allah.

Those who prioritize worldly life over the Hereafter will not have their punishment reduced and will receive no help.

Verse 87

وَلَقَدْ آتَيْنَا مُوسَى الْكِتَابَ وَقَفَّيْنَا مِنْ بَعْدِهِ بِالرُّسُلِ ۖ وَآتَيْنَا عِيسَى ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ الْبَيِّنَاتِ وَأَيَّدْنَاهُ بِرُوحِ الْقُدُسِ ۗ أَفَكُلَّمَا جَاءَكُمْ رَسُولٌ بِمَا لَا تَهْوَىٰ أَنْفُسُكُمُ اسْتَكْبَرْتُمْ فَفَرِيقًا كَذَّبْتُمْ وَفَرِيقًا تَقْتُلُونَ

Indeed, We gave Moses the Book and sent after him successive messengers. And We gave Jesus, son of Mary, clear proofs and supported him with the holy spirit. Why is it that every time a messenger comes to you ˹Israelites˺ with something you do not like, you become arrogant, rejecting some and killing others?

And We certainly gave Moses the Torah, and We followed him with messengers from the Children of Israel, and We gave Jesus, the son of Mary, clear miracles and strengthened him with the Holy Spirit (Gabriel). Is it that every time a messenger came to you with that which your souls did not desire, you grew arrogant? And a group you denied, and a group you killed?

God sent Moses with the Torah, followed by other messengers, and gave Jesus clear miracles and the Holy Spirit (Gabriel). Yet, the Israelites were arrogant, rejecting some messengers and even killing others, highlighting their resistance to divine guidance.

Verse 88

وَقَالُوا قُلُوبُنَا غُلْفٌ ۚ بَلْ لَعَنَهُمُ اللَّهُ بِكُفْرِهِمْ فَقَلِيلًا مَا يُؤْمِنُونَ

They say, “Our hearts are unreceptive!” In fact, Allah has condemned them for their disbelief. They have but little faith.

And the Children of Israel said to the Prophet of Allah and His Messenger Muhammad, peace be upon him: “Our hearts are covered, your words cannot penetrate them.” But the matter is not as they claim, rather, their hearts are cursed, sealed, and they are expelled from the mercy of Allah because of their denial, so they do not believe except a little belief that does not benefit them.

The Israelites claimed their hearts were unreceptive, but in reality, their disbelief led to their condemnation and expulsion from Allah's mercy, indicating their lack of genuine faith.

Verse 89

وَلَمَّا جَاءَهُمْ كِتَابٌ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ مُصَدِّقٌ لِمَا مَعَهُمْ وَكَانُوا مِنْ قَبْلُ يَسْتَفْتِحُونَ عَلَى الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا فَلَمَّا جَاءَهُمْ مَا عَرَفُوا كَفَرُوا بِهِ ۚ فَلَعْنَةُ اللَّهِ عَلَى الْكَافِرِينَ

Although they used to pray for victory ˹by means of the Prophet˺ over the polytheists, when there came to them a Book from Allah which they recognized, confirming the Scripture they had ˹in their hands˺, they rejected it. So may Allah’s condemnation be upon the disbelievers.

And when the Quran came to them from Allah, confirming what was with them of the Torah, they denied it, and denied the prophethood of Muhammad, may Allah bless him and grant him peace. And they were before his mission seeking victory through him over the polytheists of the Arabs, and saying: The advent of the Prophet of the end of time is near, and we will follow him and fight with him against you. But when the Messenger came to them, whose attributes and truthfulness they knew, they disbelieved in him and called him a liar. So the curse of Allah is upon everyone who disbelieves in the Prophet of Allah and His Messenger Muhammad, may Allah bless him and grant him peace, and his book that Allah revealed to him.

This verse criticizes those who, despite previously seeking the Prophet's arrival for victory, rejected him and the Quran when they came. This rejection, despite recognizing its truth, invites Allah's condemnation.

Verse 90

بِئْسَمَا اشْتَرَوْا بِهِ أَنْفُسَهُمْ أَنْ يَكْفُرُوا بِمَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ بَغْيًا أَنْ يُنَزِّلَ اللَّهُ مِنْ فَضْلِهِ عَلَىٰ مَنْ يَشَاءُ مِنْ عِبَادِهِ ۖ فَبَاءُوا بِغَضَبٍ عَلَىٰ غَضَبٍ ۚ وَلِلْكَافِرِينَ عَذَابٌ مُهِينٌ
