Miserable is the price they have sold their souls for—denying Allah’s revelation and resenting Allah for granting His grace to whoever He wills of His servants! They have earned wrath upon wrath. And such disbelievers will suffer a humiliating punishment.

Evil is what the Children of Israel have chosen for themselves; when they exchanged disbelief for faith out of injustice and envy for Allah's sending down of His bounty, the Quran, upon the Prophet of Allah and His Messenger Muhammad, may Allah bless him and grant him peace. So they returned with wrath from Allah upon them because of their denial of the Prophet Muhammad, may Allah bless him and grant him peace, after His wrath upon them because of their distortion of the Torah. And for those who deny the prophethood of Muhammad, may Allah bless him and grant him peace, is a humiliating and disgraceful punishment.

This verse describes the terrible bargain of trading faith for disbelief out of envy, leading to multiple layers of Allah's wrath and a humiliating punishment. It highlights the negative consequences of denying Allah's grace.

Verse 91

وَإِذَا قِيلَ لَهُمْ آمِنُوا بِمَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ قَالُوا نُؤْمِنُ بِمَا أُنْزِلَ عَلَيْنَا وَيَكْفُرُونَ بِمَا وَرَاءَهُ وَهُوَ الْحَقُّ مُصَدِّقًا لِمَا مَعَهُمْ ۗ قُلْ فَلِمَ تَقْتُلُونَ أَنْبِيَاءَ اللَّهِ مِنْ قَبْلُ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ مُؤْمِنِينَ

When it is said to them: “Believe in what Allah has revealed,” they reply, “We only believe in what was sent down to us,” and they deny what came afterwards, though it is the truth confirming their own Scriptures! Ask ˹them, O Prophet˺, “Why then did you kill Allah’s prophets before, if you are ˹truly˺ believers?”

And when some Muslims say to the Jews, "Believe in what Allah has revealed of the Quran," they say, "We believe in what Allah revealed to our prophets," and they deny what Allah revealed after that, which is the truth confirming what they have. If they truly believed in their books, they would have believed in the Quran that confirms them. Say to them, O Muhammad, if you are believers in what Allah has revealed to you, then why did you kill the prophets of Allah before?

This verse questions the hypocritical stance of those who claim to believe only in previous scriptures while rejecting the Quran, even though it confirms their own. Their past actions of killing prophets further expose their lack of true belief.

Verse 92

وَلَقَدْ جَاءَكُمْ مُوسَىٰ بِالْبَيِّنَاتِ ثُمَّ اتَّخَذْتُمُ الْعِجْلَ مِنْ بَعْدِهِ وَأَنْتُمْ ظَالِمُونَ

Indeed, Moses came to you with clear proofs, then you worshipped the calf in his absence, acting wrongfully.

And indeed, the Prophet of Allah, Moses, came to you with clear miracles indicating his truthfulness, such as the flood, the locusts, the lice, the frogs, and other things that Allah mentioned in the Great Quran. Yet, you took the calf as an object of worship, after Moses had gone to the appointed time with his Lord, while you were transgressing the limits of Allah.

This verse reminds of the clear signs that Prophet Moses brought and how, despite that, the people worshipped the calf in his absence, committing a grave sin.

Verse 93

وَإِذْ أَخَذْنَا مِيثَاقَكُمْ وَرَفَعْنَا فَوْقَكُمُ الطُّورَ خُذُوا مَا آتَيْنَاكُمْ بِقُوَّةٍ وَاسْمَعُوا ۖ قَالُوا سَمِعْنَا وَعَصَيْنَا وَأُشْرِبُوا فِي قُلُوبِهِمُ الْعِجْلَ بِكُفْرِهِمْ ۚ قُلْ بِئْسَمَا يَأْمُرُكُمْ بِهِ إِيمَانُكُمْ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ مُؤْمِنِينَ

And when We took your covenant and raised the mountain above you ˹saying˺, “Hold firmly to that ˹Scripture˺ which We have given you and obey,” they answered, “We hear and disobey.” The love of the calf was rooted in their hearts because of their disbelief. Say, ˹O Prophet,˺ “How evil is what your ˹so-called˺ belief prompts you to do, if you ˹actually˺ believe ˹in the Torah˺!”

And remember when We took a confirmed covenant from you to accept what Moses brought you of the Torah, and you broke the covenant, so We raised Mount Tur above your heads, and We said to you, 'Take what We have given you with determination, and hear and obey, or We will drop the mountain on you.' So you said, 'We have heard your word and disobeyed your command,' because the worship of the calf had mixed with your hearts due to your persistence in disbelief. Say to them, O Messenger, evil is what your faith commands you of disbelief and misguidance, if you are believers in what Allah has revealed to you.

This verse recounts the covenant taken and the people's disobedience, showcasing their deep-rooted disbelief. Their claim of faith in the Torah is questioned, considering their actions.

Verse 94

قُلْ إِنْ كَانَتْ لَكُمُ الدَّارُ الْآخِرَةُ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ خَالِصَةً مِنْ دُونِ النَّاسِ فَتَمَنَّوُا الْمَوْتَ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ صَادِقِينَ

Say, ˹O Prophet,˺ “If the ˹eternal˺ Home of the Hereafter with Allah is exclusively for you ˹Israelites˺ out of all humanity, then wish for death if what you say is true!”

Say - O Messenger - to the Jews who claim that Paradise is exclusive to them, because they claim that they are the allies of Allah to the exclusion of other people, and that they are His children and beloved ones: If that is the case, then invoke death upon the liars among you or others, if you are truthful in your claim.

This verse challenges the Jews who claim to be the only people destined for Paradise. They are asked to wish for death if their claim is true, as a way to demonstrate their certainty.

Verse 95

وَلَنْ يَتَمَنَّوْهُ أَبَدًا بِمَا قَدَّمَتْ أَيْدِيهِمْ ۗ وَاللَّهُ عَلِيمٌ بِالظَّالِمِينَ

But they will never wish for that because of what their hands have done. And Allah has ˹perfect˺ knowledge of the wrongdoers.

And they will never do that, because they know the truthfulness of the Prophet Muhammad, may Allah bless him and grant him peace, and their lies and fabrications, and because of the disbelief and disobedience they have committed, which leads to their deprivation of Paradise and entry into Hellfire. And Allah is Knowing of the wrongdoers among His servants, and He will recompense them for that.

The Jews will not wish for death because they are aware of their misdeeds and that it will lead to punishment. Allah knows the wrongdoers and will hold them accountable.

Verse 96

وَلَتَجِدَنَّهُمْ أَحْرَصَ النَّاسِ عَلَىٰ حَيَاةٍ وَمِنَ الَّذِينَ أَشْرَكُوا ۚ يَوَدُّ أَحَدُهُمْ لَوْ يُعَمَّرُ أَلْفَ سَنَةٍ وَمَا هُوَ بِمُزَحْزِحِهِ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ أَنْ يُعَمَّرَ ۗ وَاللَّهُ بَصِيرٌ بِمَا يَعْمَلُونَ

You will surely find them clinging to life more eagerly than any other people, even more than polytheists. Each one of them wishes to live a thousand years. But even if they were to live that long, it would not save them from the punishment. And Allah is All-Seeing of what they do.

And you will surely know, O Messenger, that the Jews are the most eager of people for a long life, no matter what this life is of humiliation and degradation; indeed, their desire for a long life exceeds the desires of the polytheists. A Jew wishes to live a thousand years, and this long life, if obtained, does not distance him from the punishment of Allah. And Allah is not unaware of anything of their deeds, and He will recompense them for them with what they deserve of torment.

The Jews are described as having an extreme attachment to life, even more than polytheists, and desire a long life regardless of its quality. This desire won't save them from divine punishment as Allah is fully aware of their actions.

Verse 97

قُلْ مَنْ كَانَ عَدُوًّا لِجِبْرِيلَ فَإِنَّهُ نَزَّلَهُ عَلَىٰ قَلْبِكَ بِإِذْنِ اللَّهِ مُصَدِّقًا لِمَا بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ وَهُدًى وَبُشْرَىٰ لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ

Say, ˹O Prophet,˺ “Whoever is an enemy of Gabriel should know that he revealed this ˹Quran˺ to your heart by Allah’s Will, confirming what came before it—a guide and good news for the believers.”

Say - O Messenger - to the Jews when they said: Gabriel is our enemy among the angels: Whoever is an enemy to Gabriel, then he has brought down the Qur'an upon your heart by the permission of Allah, confirming what preceded it of the books of Allah, guiding to the truth, and giving good tidings to those who believe in it with all good in this world and the hereafter.

This verse addresses those who are enemies of Angel Gabriel, stating that Gabriel brought the Quran to the Prophet Muhammad by Allah's will. The Quran confirms previous scriptures and is a guide and good news for believers.

Verse 98

مَنْ كَانَ عَدُوًّا لِلَّهِ وَمَلَائِكَتِهِ وَرُسُلِهِ وَجِبْرِيلَ وَمِيكَالَ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ عَدُوٌّ لِلْكَافِرِينَ

Whoever is an enemy of Allah, His angels, His messengers, Gabriel, and Michael, then ˹let them know that˺ Allah is certainly the enemy of the disbelievers.

Whoever is an enemy to Allah and His angels, and His messengers from among the angels or humans, especially the two angels Gabriel and Michael, because the Jews claimed that Gabriel is their enemy and Michael is their ally, then Allah informs them that whoever is an enemy to one of them is an enemy to the other, and an enemy to Allah as well, for indeed Allah is an enemy to those who reject what was revealed to His Messenger Muhammad, may Allah bless him and grant him peace.

Whoever is an enemy to Allah, His angels, His messengers, or specifically to Gabriel and Michael, is considered an enemy of Allah as well. Allah is an enemy to those who disbelieve.

Verse 99

وَلَقَدْ أَنْزَلْنَا إِلَيْكَ آيَاتٍ بَيِّنَاتٍ ۖ وَمَا يَكْفُرُ بِهَا إِلَّا الْفَاسِقُونَ

Indeed, We have sent down to you ˹O Prophet˺ clear revelations. ˹But˺ none will deny them except the rebellious.

And We have indeed sent down to you, O Messenger, clear signs that indicate that you are a Messenger from Allah truly and rightfully, and none denies these signs except those who depart from the religion of Allah.

Clear revelations have been sent down, and only those who are rebellious will deny them. This highlights the obstinacy of those who reject the truth even when it is clear.

Verse 100

أَوَكُلَّمَا عَاهَدُوا عَهْدًا نَبَذَهُ فَرِيقٌ مِنْهُمْ ۚ بَلْ أَكْثَرُهُمْ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ

Why is it that every time they make a covenant, a group of them casts it aside? In fact, most of them do not believe.

How bad is the state of the Children of Israel in their breaking of covenants! Whenever they made a covenant, a group of them rejected that covenant and broke it; you see them concluding a covenant today and breaking it tomorrow; indeed, most of them do not believe in what the Prophet of Allah and His Messenger Muhammad, may Allah bless him and grant him peace, came with.

This verse questions the habit of the Children of Israel in breaking their covenants repeatedly. It indicates their lack of faith in the message of Prophet Muhammad.

Verse 101

وَلَمَّا جَاءَهُمْ رَسُولٌ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ مُصَدِّقٌ لِمَا مَعَهُمْ نَبَذَ فَرِيقٌ مِنَ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ كِتَابَ اللَّهِ وَرَاءَ ظُهُورِهِمْ كَأَنَّهُمْ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ

Now, when a messenger from Allah has come to them—confirming their own Scriptures—some of the People of the Book cast the Book of Allah behind their backs as if they did not know.

And when Muhammad, the Messenger of Allah, may Allah bless him and grant him peace, came to them with the Qur'an, which agrees with what they had of the Torah, a group of them cast away the Book of Allah and put it behind their backs, like the ignorant who do not know its reality.

When a messenger (Muhammad) came with a scripture (Quran) confirming their own, some from the People of the Book discarded it. They acted as if they were ignorant, even though it confirmed their scriptures.

Verse 102

وَاتَّبَعُوا مَا تَتْلُو الشَّيَاطِينُ عَلَىٰ مُلْكِ سُلَيْمَانَ ۖ وَمَا كَفَرَ سُلَيْمَانُ وَلَٰكِنَّ الشَّيَاطِينَ كَفَرُوا يُعَلِّمُونَ النَّاسَ السِّحْرَ وَمَا أُنْزِلَ عَلَى الْمَلَكَيْنِ بِبَابِلَ هَارُوتَ وَمَارُوتَ ۚ وَمَا يُعَلِّمَانِ مِنْ أَحَدٍ حَتَّىٰ يَقُولَا إِنَّمَا نَحْنُ فِتْنَةٌ فَلَا تَكْفُرْ ۖ فَيَتَعَلَّمُونَ مِنْهُمَا مَا يُفَرِّقُونَ بِهِ بَيْنَ الْمَرْءِ وَزَوْجِهِ ۚ وَمَا هُمْ بِضَارِّينَ بِهِ مِنْ أَحَدٍ إِلَّا بِإِذْنِ اللَّهِ ۚ وَيَتَعَلَّمُونَ مَا يَضُرُّهُمْ وَلَا يَنْفَعُهُمْ ۚ وَلَقَدْ عَلِمُوا لَمَنِ اشْتَرَاهُ مَا لَهُ فِي الْآخِرَةِ مِنْ خَلَاقٍ ۚ وَلَبِئْسَ مَا شَرَوْا بِهِ أَنْفُسَهُمْ ۚ لَوْ كَانُوا يَعْلَمُونَ

They ˹instead˺ followed the magic promoted by the devils during the reign of Solomon. Never did Solomon disbelieve, rather the devils disbelieved. They taught magic to the people, along with what had been revealed to the two angels, Hârût and Mârût, in Babylon. The two angels never taught anyone without saying, “We are only a test ˹for you˺, so do not abandon ˹your˺ faith.” Yet people learned ˹magic˺ that caused a rift ˹even˺ between husband and wife; although their magic could not harm anyone except by Allah’s Will. They learned what harmed them and did not benefit them—although they already knew that whoever buys into magic would have no share in the Hereafter. Miserable indeed was the price for which they sold their souls, if only they knew!

And the Jews followed what the devils gave out in the reign of Solomon. It was not Solomon who disbelieved, but the devils disbelieved, teaching people magic and thus disbelieving in Allah. And the Jews also followed the magic that was revealed to the two angels, Harut and Marut, in Babylon, Iraq, as a test and trial from Allah for His servants. The two angels would not teach anyone until they advised them and warned them against learning magic, saying: 'Do not disbelieve by learning magic and obeying the devils.' So people would learn from the two angels that which they could use to cause hatred between husband and wife until they separated. And the magicians cannot harm anyone except by the permission and decree of Allah. And the magicians learn only evil that harms them and does not benefit them, and the devils have transmitted it to the Jews, so it became widespread among them until they preferred it over the Book of Allah. And the Jews have known that whoever chooses magic and abandons the truth has no share of good in the Hereafter. And evil is that for which they have sold themselves with magic and disbelief in exchange for faith and following the Messenger, if only they had knowledge that yields action based on what they were admonished with.

This verse discusses how some people followed magic taught by devils instead of the divine guidance of Solomon. The devils, not Solomon, disbelieved by teaching magic. It highlights a test through two angels, Harut and Marut, who warned against magic. Despite warnings, people learned magic that could cause harm, even between spouses, but only with Allah's permission. Ultimately, choosing magic leads to loss in the Hereafter.

Verse 103

وَلَوْ أَنَّهُمْ آمَنُوا وَاتَّقَوْا لَمَثُوبَةٌ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ خَيْرٌ ۖ لَوْ كَانُوا يَعْلَمُونَ

If only they were faithful and mindful ˹of Allah˺, there would have been a better reward from Allah, if only they knew!

And if the Jews had believed and feared Allah, they would have been certain that the reward of Allah is better for them than magic and what they have earned with it, if they only knew what is obtained through faith and piety of reward and recompense, they would have truly believed.

This verse emphasizes that if people had faith and feared Allah, they would have known that Allah's reward is much better than any worldly gains from magic. It underscores the importance of piety and faith in achieving true and lasting benefits.

Verse 104

يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تَقُولُوا رَاعِنَا وَقُولُوا انْظُرْنَا وَاسْمَعُوا ۗ وَلِلْكَافِرِينَ عَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌ

O believers! Do not say, “Râ’ina.” [Herd us!] But say, “Unẓurna,” [Tend to us!] and listen ˹attentively˺. And the disbelievers will suffer a painful punishment.

O you who have believed, do not say to the Messenger Muhammad, may Allah bless him and grant him peace: 'Ra'ina,' which means: 'Give ear to us,' so understand from us and make us understand; because the Jews used to say it to the Prophet, may Allah bless him and grant him peace, twisting their tongues with it, intending to insult him and attribute him to foolishness. Rather, say - O believers - instead of that: 'Unzurna,' meaning 'look at us and take care of us,' which conveys the same desired meaning, and listen to what is recited to you from the Book of your Lord and understand it. And for the disbelievers is a painful torment.

This verse directs believers to use respectful language when addressing the Prophet. Instead of using "Ra'ina" which could be twisted, they are told to use "Unzurna". It also highlights the importance of attentively listening to the divine message and warns of a painful punishment for disbelievers.

Verse 105

مَا يَوَدُّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ وَلَا الْمُشْرِكِينَ أَنْ يُنَزَّلَ عَلَيْكُمْ مِنْ خَيْرٍ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ ۗ وَاللَّهُ يَخْتَصُّ بِرَحْمَتِهِ مَنْ يَشَاءُ ۚ وَاللَّهُ ذُو الْفَضْلِ الْعَظِيمِ

The disbelievers from the People of the Book and the polytheists would not want you to receive any blessing from your Lord, but Allah selects whoever He wills for His mercy. And Allah is the Lord of infinite bounty.

The disbelievers from the People of the Book and the polytheists do not like that any good from your Lord should be sent down upon you, be it a Quran, or knowledge, or victory, or glad tidings. And Allah selects for His mercy whom He wills from His servants with prophethood and messengership. And Allah is the Possessor of vast, abundant bestowal.

This verse reveals that disbelievers from the People of the Book (Jews and Christians) and polytheists do not wish good upon the believers. It affirms that Allah chooses whomever He wills for His mercy and that He is the Possessor of infinite bounty.

Verse 106

مَا نَنْسَخْ مِنْ آيَةٍ أَوْ نُنْسِهَا نَأْتِ بِخَيْرٍ مِنْهَا أَوْ مِثْلِهَا ۗ أَلَمْ تَعْلَمْ أَنَّ اللَّهَ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ

If We ever abrogate a verse or cause it to be forgotten, We replace it with a better or similar one. Do you not know that Allah is Most Capable of everything?

We do not abrogate a verse or cause it to be forgotten from the hearts and minds without bringing one better than it or similar to it in terms of obligation and reward, and for each is wisdom. Do you not know -O Prophet- you and your nation that Allah is Capable and nothing is impossible for Him?

This verse explains that Allah can replace any verse with a better one or one similar in value. This highlights Allah's absolute power and wisdom.

Verse 107

أَلَمْ تَعْلَمْ أَنَّ اللَّهَ لَهُ مُلْكُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ ۗ وَمَا لَكُمْ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ مِنْ وَلِيٍّ وَلَا نَصِيرٍ

Do you not know that the kingdom of the heavens and the earth belongs ˹only˺ to Allah, and you have no guardian or helper besides Allah?

Do you not know -O Prophet- you and your nation that Allah, the Exalted, is the Owner and Controller of the heavens and the earth? He does what He wills, and He judges as He pleases, and He commands His servants and forbids them as He wills, and obedience and acceptance are upon them. And let those who disobey know that there is no guardian for them besides Allah, nor any helper to prevent them from the punishment of Allah.

This verse reminds us that Allah is the sole owner and controller of the heavens and the earth. It emphasizes that no one can offer protection or help besides Allah.

Verse 108

أَمْ تُرِيدُونَ أَنْ تَسْأَلُوا رَسُولَكُمْ كَمَا سُئِلَ مُوسَىٰ مِنْ قَبْلُ ۗ وَمَنْ يَتَبَدَّلِ الْكُفْرَ بِالْإِيمَانِ فَقَدْ ضَلَّ سَوَاءَ السَّبِيلِ

Or do you ˹believers˺ intend to ask of your Messenger as Moses was asked before? But whoever trades belief for disbelief has truly strayed from the Right Way.

Rather, do you want -O people- to ask your Messenger Muhammad, peace and blessings be upon him, for things out of stubbornness and obstinacy, as was requested of Moses? Know that whoever chooses disbelief and abandons faith has departed from the straight path of Allah to ignorance and misguidance.

This verse cautions believers against asking too many questions out of stubbornness, like the Children of Israel did with Moses. It warns that choosing disbelief over faith is a clear deviation from the right path.

Verse 109

وَدَّ كَثِيرٌ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ لَوْ يَرُدُّونَكُمْ مِنْ بَعْدِ إِيمَانِكُمْ كُفَّارًا حَسَدًا مِنْ عِنْدِ أَنْفُسِهِمْ مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا تَبَيَّنَ لَهُمُ الْحَقُّ ۖ فَاعْفُوا وَاصْفَحُوا حَتَّىٰ يَأْتِيَ اللَّهُ بِأَمْرِهِ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ

Many among the People of the Book wish they could turn you ˹believers˺ back to disbelief because of their envy, after the truth has been made clear to them. Pardon and bear with them until Allah delivers His decision. Surely Allah is Most Capable of everything.

Many of the People of the Book wished to turn you back after your belief, as disbelievers as you used to worship idols before, because of the hatred that filled their hearts after the truth of the prophet of Allah and His Messenger Muhammad, peace and blessings be upon him, had become clear to them in what he brought. So, overlook what was their fault and mistake and pardon their ignorance, until Allah brings His judgment upon them with fighting (which has come and occurred), and He will punish them for their evil deeds. Indeed, Allah is Capable of all things, nothing is impossible for Him.

This verse reveals that some People of the Book wish to turn believers away from Islam out of envy. It instructs believers to pardon them until Allah's judgment is delivered.

Verse 110

وَأَقِيمُوا الصَّلَاةَ وَآتُوا الزَّكَاةَ ۚ وَمَا تُقَدِّمُوا لِأَنْفُسِكُمْ مِنْ خَيْرٍ تَجِدُوهُ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ بَصِيرٌ

Establish prayer, and pay alms-tax. Whatever good you send forth for yourselves, you will ˹certainly˺ find ˹its reward˺ with Allah. Surely Allah is All-Seeing of what you do.

And engage -O believers- in performing prayer correctly, and giving the prescribed alms (Zakat). And know that every good you put forward for yourselves, you will find its reward with Allah in the Hereafter. Indeed, He is All-Seeing of all your deeds, and He will recompense you for them.

This verse urges believers to establish prayer and give Zakat (alms-tax). It also assures them that their good deeds will be rewarded by Allah.

Verse 111

وَقَالُوا لَنْ يَدْخُلَ الْجَنَّةَ إِلَّا مَنْ كَانَ هُودًا أَوْ نَصَارَىٰ ۗ تِلْكَ أَمَانِيُّهُمْ ۗ قُلْ هَاتُوا بُرْهَانَكُمْ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ صَادِقِينَ

The Jews and Christians each claim that none will enter Paradise except those of their own faith. These are their desires. Reply, ˹O Prophet,˺ “Show ˹me˺ your proof if what you say is true.”

Each of the Jews and Christians claimed that Paradise is exclusive to their sect and no one else will enter it. These are their corrupt delusions. Say to them -O Messenger-: Bring your proof of the validity of your claims, if you are truthful in your claims.

This verse exposes the false claims of Jews and Christians who each say that only their own will enter Paradise. It challenges them to prove such claims.

Verse 112

بَلَىٰ مَنْ أَسْلَمَ وَجْهَهُ لِلَّهِ وَهُوَ مُحْسِنٌ فَلَهُ أَجْرُهُ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِ وَلَا خَوْفٌ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا هُمْ يَحْزَنُونَ

But no! Whoever submits themselves to Allah and does good will have their reward with their Lord. And there will be no fear for them, nor will they grieve.

The matter is not as they claimed that Paradise is exclusive to one sect over another, but rather, whoever sincerely devotes themselves to Allah alone, without any partners, and follows the Messenger Muhammad, peace and blessings be upon him, in all his sayings and actions, then for him is the reward of his deeds with his Lord in the Hereafter, which is entering Paradise, and they will have no fear for what they are to face of the Hereafter, nor will they grieve over what they missed of worldly gains.

This verse clarifies that anyone who submits to Allah and does good deeds will be rewarded by Allah in Paradise, without fear or grief.

Verse 113

وَقَالَتِ الْيَهُودُ لَيْسَتِ النَّصَارَىٰ عَلَىٰ شَيْءٍ وَقَالَتِ النَّصَارَىٰ لَيْسَتِ الْيَهُودُ عَلَىٰ شَيْءٍ وَهُمْ يَتْلُونَ الْكِتَابَ ۗ كَذَٰلِكَ قَالَ الَّذِينَ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ مِثْلَ قَوْلِهِمْ ۚ فَاللَّهُ يَحْكُمُ بَيْنَهُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ فِيمَا كَانُوا فِيهِ يَخْتَلِفُونَ

The Jews say, “The Christians have nothing to stand on” and the Christians say, “The Jews have nothing to stand on,” although both recite the Scriptures. And those ˹pagans˺ who have no knowledge say the same ˹about people of faith˺. Surely Allah will judge between them on the Day of Judgment regarding their dispute.

The Jews said: 'The Christians have no basis in the correct religion,' and likewise the Christians said about the Jews, while they read the Torah and the Gospel, both of which contain the obligation of believing in all the prophets. Similarly, those who do not know from the polytheists of the Arabs and others said the same, meaning they said to everyone with a religion: 'You are not on anything (of truth),' so Allah will judge between them on the Day of Resurrection concerning what they differed about in matters of religion, and will recompense each according to his deeds.

This verse highlights the conflicts between religious groups, with each claiming exclusivity. It emphasizes that despite having scriptures, they deny each other’s validity. Ultimately, Allah will judge between them on the Day of Judgment.

Verse 114

وَمَنْ أَظْلَمُ مِمَّنْ مَنَعَ مَسَاجِدَ اللَّهِ أَنْ يُذْكَرَ فِيهَا اسْمُهُ وَسَعَىٰ فِي خَرَابِهَا ۚ أُولَٰئِكَ مَا كَانَ لَهُمْ أَنْ يَدْخُلُوهَا إِلَّا خَائِفِينَ ۚ لَهُمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا خِزْيٌ وَلَهُمْ فِي الْآخِرَةِ عَذَابٌ عَظِيمٌ

Who does more wrong than those who prevent Allah’s Name from being mentioned in His places of worship and strive to destroy them? Such people have no right to enter these places except with fear. For them there is disgrace in this world, and they will suffer a tremendous punishment in the Hereafter.

And who is more unjust than those who prevent the remembrance of Allah in mosques, from establishing prayer, and reciting the Quran, and the like, and strive to ruin them by demolition or closure, or by preventing the believers from them? Those are the unjust ones; it was not for them to enter the mosques except in fear and apprehension of punishment. For them is disgrace and ignominy in this world, and for them in the Hereafter is a severe punishment.

This verse condemns those who prevent the remembrance of Allah in mosques and strive to destroy them. They are warned of disgrace in this life and severe punishment in the Hereafter.

Verse 115

وَلِلَّهِ الْمَشْرِقُ وَالْمَغْرِبُ ۚ فَأَيْنَمَا تُوَلُّوا فَثَمَّ وَجْهُ اللَّهِ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ وَاسِعٌ عَلِيمٌ

To Allah belong the east and the west, so wherever you turn you are facing ˹towards˺ Allah. Surely Allah is All-Encompassing, All-Knowing.

To Allah belongs the east and the west. So wherever you [may] turn, there is the Face of Allah. Indeed, Allah is all-Encompassing and Knowing. You are seeking His face wherever you turn in prayer by the command of Allah; you have not exited from His dominion and obedience. Indeed, Allah is vast in mercy to His servants, knowing of their actions; nothing of it is hidden from Him.

This verse states that all directions belong to Allah, so wherever one turns in prayer, they are facing Him. It emphasizes Allah's all-encompassing presence and knowledge.

Verse 116

وَقَالُوا اتَّخَذَ اللَّهُ وَلَدًا ۗ سُبْحَانَهُ ۖ بَلْ لَهُ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ ۖ كُلٌّ لَهُ قَانِتُونَ

They say, “Allah has offspring.” Glory be to Him! In fact, to Him belongs whatever is in the heavens and the earth—all are subject to His Will.

And the Jews, the Christians, and the polytheists said, 'Allah has taken a son.' Exalted is Allah -Glorified is He- above this false statement. Rather, everyone in the heavens and the earth is His possession and His servants, and they are all submissive to Him, subjected under His control.

This verse refutes the claim that Allah has offspring, stating that everything in the heavens and earth belongs to Him and is subject to His will. Allah is exalted above such claims.

Verse 117

بَدِيعُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ ۖ وَإِذَا قَضَىٰ أَمْرًا فَإِنَّمَا يَقُولُ لَهُ كُنْ فَيَكُونُ

˹He is˺ the Originator of the heavens and the earth! When He decrees a matter, He simply tells it, “Be!” And it is!

And Allah is the Creator of the heavens and the earth, without any prior example. And when He decrees a matter and intends its existence, He only says to it, 'Be,' and it is.

This verse emphasizes Allah as the Originator of the heavens and the earth. When Allah decrees something, He simply says “Be,” and it comes into existence. This shows His absolute power and authority.

Verse 118

وَقَالَ الَّذِينَ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ لَوْلَا يُكَلِّمُنَا اللَّهُ أَوْ تَأْتِينَا آيَةٌ ۗ كَذَٰلِكَ قَالَ الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ مِثْلَ قَوْلِهِمْ ۘ تَشَابَهَتْ قُلُوبُهُمْ ۗ قَدْ بَيَّنَّا الْآيَاتِ لِقَوْمٍ يُوقِنُونَ

Those who have no knowledge say, “If only Allah would speak to us or a sign would come to us!” The same was said by those who came before. Their hearts are all alike. Indeed, We have made the signs clear for people of sure faith.

And the ignorant among the People of the Book and others said to the Prophet of Allah and His Messenger Muhammad, may Allah bless him and grant him peace, by way of stubbornness: 'Why does Allah not speak to us directly to inform us that you are His Messenger, or bring us a miracle from Allah that indicates your truthfulness?' And such a statement was said by the nations before to their messengers out of stubbornness and defiance; due to the similarity of the hearts of the predecessors and the successors in disbelief and misguidance. We have clarified the verses for those who believe with firm conviction; because they are believers in Allah, and follow what He has legislated for them.

This verse addresses the demands of the ignorant for direct signs from Allah. It notes that previous generations also made similar demands. However, Allah has already clarified signs for those who truly believe.

Verse 119

إِنَّا أَرْسَلْنَاكَ بِالْحَقِّ بَشِيرًا وَنَذِيرًا ۖ وَلَا تُسْأَلُ عَنْ أَصْحَابِ الْجَحِيمِ

We have surely sent you with the truth ˹O Prophet˺ as a deliverer of good news and a warner. And you will not be accountable for the residents of the Hellfire.

Indeed, We have sent you -O Messenger- with the true religion, supported by proofs and miracles, so convey it to the people, while giving good tidings to the believers of the good of this world and the Hereafter, and warning the stubborn with what awaits them from the punishment of Allah, and you are not -after the conveyance- responsible for the disbelief of whoever disbelieves in you; for they will enter the Fire on the Day of Resurrection, and will not come out of it.

This verse states that the Prophet was sent with truth as a deliverer of good news and a warner. It clarifies that he is not accountable for those who reject faith, as they will face the consequences of their disbelief.

Verse 120

وَلَنْ تَرْضَىٰ عَنْكَ الْيَهُودُ وَلَا النَّصَارَىٰ حَتَّىٰ تَتَّبِعَ مِلَّتَهُمْ ۗ قُلْ إِنَّ هُدَى اللَّهِ هُوَ الْهُدَىٰ ۗ وَلَئِنِ اتَّبَعْتَ أَهْوَاءَهُمْ بَعْدَ الَّذِي جَاءَكَ مِنَ الْعِلْمِ ۙ مَا لَكَ مِنَ اللَّهِ مِنْ وَلِيٍّ وَلَا نَصِيرٍ

Never will the Jews or Christians be pleased with you, until you follow their faith. Say, “Allah’s guidance is the only ˹true˺ guidance.” And if you were to follow their desires after ˹all˺ the knowledge that has come to you, there would be none to protect or help you against Allah.

The Jews and the Christians will never be pleased with you, O Messenger, until you abandon your religion and follow their religion. Say to them: Indeed, the religion of Islam is the true religion. And if you were to follow their desires after what has come to you of revelation, you would have no protector or helper with Allah. This is directed to the nation in general, even if it is addressed to the Prophet, peace be upon him.

This verse highlights that Jews and Christians will not be satisfied until Muslims abandon their faith. It emphasizes that true guidance comes from Allah, and following other desires would leave one without protection.

Verse 121

الَّذِينَ آتَيْنَاهُمُ الْكِتَابَ يَتْلُونَهُ حَقَّ تِلَاوَتِهِ أُولَٰئِكَ يُؤْمِنُونَ بِهِ ۗ وَمَنْ يَكْفُرْ بِهِ فَأُولَٰئِكَ هُمُ الْخَاسِرُونَ

Those We have given the Book follow it as it should be followed. It is they who ˹truly˺ believe in it. As for those who reject it, it is they who are the losers.

Those to whom We have given the Book, from among the Jews and the Christians, read it with proper recitation, and follow it as it should be followed, and believe in what came in it of faith in the messengers of Allah, and among them is their seal, our Prophet and Messenger Muhammad, peace be upon him, and they do not distort or alter what came in it. These are the ones who believe in the Prophet Muhammad, peace be upon him, and in what was revealed to him. As for those who altered part of the Book and concealed part of it, these are disbelievers in the Prophet of Allah Muhammad, peace be upon him, and in what was revealed to him. And whoever disbelieves in him, then those are the most severe losers with Allah.

This verse describes those who follow the divine book properly, believing in its teachings and messengers, including Prophet Muhammad (peace be upon him). Those who reject it are deemed losers.

Verse 122

يَا بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ اذْكُرُوا نِعْمَتِيَ الَّتِي أَنْعَمْتُ عَلَيْكُمْ وَأَنِّي فَضَّلْتُكُمْ عَلَى الْعَالَمِينَ

O Children of Israel! Remember My favours upon you and how I honoured you above the others.

O descendants of Jacob, remember My many favors upon you, and that I favored you over the worlds of your time by the abundance of your prophets and what was revealed to them of the books.

This verse reminds the Children of Israel of the favors granted to them by Allah, emphasizing their distinction through the prophets and scriptures they received.

Verse 123

وَاتَّقُوا يَوْمًا لَا تَجْزِي نَفْسٌ عَنْ نَفْسٍ شَيْئًا وَلَا يُقْبَلُ مِنْهَا عَدْلٌ وَلَا تَنْفَعُهَا شَفَاعَةٌ وَلَا هُمْ يُنْصَرُونَ

And guard yourselves against the Day when no soul will be of any help to another. No ransom will be taken, no intercession accepted, and no help will be given.

And fear the terrors of the Day of Reckoning when no soul will avail another soul at all, nor will Allah accept from it any ransom to save it from the punishment, nor will any intercession benefit it, nor will anyone help it.

This verse warns about the Day of Judgment, where no one can help another, and neither ransom nor intercession will be accepted, underscoring the importance of accountability.

Verse 124

وَإِذِ ابْتَلَىٰ إِبْرَاهِيمَ رَبُّهُ بِكَلِمَاتٍ فَأَتَمَّهُنَّ ۖ قَالَ إِنِّي جَاعِلُكَ لِلنَّاسِ إِمَامًا ۖ قَالَ وَمِنْ ذُرِّيَّتِي ۖ قَالَ لَا يَنَالُ عَهْدِي الظَّالِمِينَ

˹Remember˺ when Abraham was tested by his Lord with ˹certain˺ commandments, which he fulfilled. Allah said, “I will certainly make you into a role model for the people.” Abraham asked, “What about my offspring?” Allah replied, “My covenant is not extended to the wrongdoers.”

And remember, O Prophet, when Allah tested Abraham with what He legislated for him of obligations, and he fulfilled them and carried them out in the best manner. Allah said to him: Indeed, I will make you a model for the people. Abraham said: My Lord, make some of my descendants leaders, as a favor from You. Allah, the Glorified, answered him that the leadership in religion will not be attained by the wrongdoers.

This verse narrates how Abraham fulfilled Allah's commandments and was made a role model. It also clarifies that divine leadership is not granted to wrongdoers.

Verse 125

وَإِذْ جَعَلْنَا الْبَيْتَ مَثَابَةً لِلنَّاسِ وَأَمْنًا وَاتَّخِذُوا مِنْ مَقَامِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ مُصَلًّى ۖ وَعَهِدْنَا إِلَىٰ إِبْرَاهِيمَ وَإِسْمَاعِيلَ أَنْ طَهِّرَا بَيْتِيَ لِلطَّائِفِينَ وَالْعَاكِفِينَ وَالرُّكَّعِ السُّجُودِ

And ˹remember˺ when We made the Sacred House a centre and a sanctuary for the people ˹saying˺, “˹You may˺ take the standing-place of Abraham as a site of prayer.” And We entrusted Abraham and Ishmael to purify My House for those who circle it, who meditate in it, and who bow and prostrate themselves ˹in prayer˺.

And remember, O Prophet, when We made the Kaaba a resort for the people, to which they come, then return to their families, then return to it, and a gathering place for them in the Hajj, the Umrah, the circumambulation, and the prayer, and a safe haven for them, where no enemy attacks them. And We said: Take the standing place of Abraham as a place for prayer, which is the stone on which Abraham stood when he built the Kaaba. And We revealed to Abraham and his son Ishmael: Purify My House from all filth and impurity, for those who worship in it by circumambulating the Kaaba, or secluding themselves in the mosque, and praying in it.

This verse recalls when the Kaaba was established as a center and sanctuary for people. The standing place of Abraham is designated as a place of prayer and Muslims are reminded to purify the House of Allah.

Verse 126

وَإِذْ قَالَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ رَبِّ اجْعَلْ هَٰذَا بَلَدًا آمِنًا وَارْزُقْ أَهْلَهُ مِنَ الثَّمَرَاتِ مَنْ آمَنَ مِنْهُمْ بِاللَّهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ ۖ قَالَ وَمَنْ كَفَرَ فَأُمَتِّعُهُ قَلِيلًا ثُمَّ أَضْطَرُّهُ إِلَىٰ عَذَابِ النَّارِ ۖ وَبِئْسَ الْمَصِيرُ

And ˹remember˺ when Abraham said, “My Lord, make this city ˹of Mecca˺ secure and provide fruits to its people—those among them who believe in Allah and the Last Day.” He answered, “As for those who disbelieve, I will let them enjoy themselves for a little while, then I will condemn them to the torment of the Fire. What an evil destination!”

And remember, O Prophet, when Abraham said in supplication: My Lord, make "Mecca" a safe city from fear, and provide its people with various kinds of fruits, and dedicate this provision to those who believe in Allah and the Last Day. Allah said: And whoever disbelieves among them, then I will provide for him in this world and let him enjoy a little, then I will force him reluctantly to the punishment of the Fire. And how wretched a destination and place of abode is this fate.

This verse describes Abraham's prayer for Mecca to be secure and its people to be provided for, particularly the believers. It also mentions that disbelievers will be given temporary enjoyment but face severe punishment in the afterlife.

Verse 127

وَإِذْ يَرْفَعُ إِبْرَاهِيمُ الْقَوَاعِدَ مِنَ الْبَيْتِ وَإِسْمَاعِيلُ رَبَّنَا تَقَبَّلْ مِنَّا ۖ إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ السَّمِيعُ الْعَلِيمُ

And ˹remember˺ when Abraham raised the foundation of the House with Ishmael, ˹both praying,˺ “Our Lord! Accept ˹this˺ from us. You are indeed the All-Hearing, All-Knowing.

And remember - O Prophet - when Abraham and Ishmael raised the foundations of the Kaaba, and they were calling upon Allah in humility: Our Lord, accept from us our righteous deeds and our supplication. Indeed, You are the All-Hearing of Your servants’ statements, the All-Knowing of their conditions.

This verse recalls when Abraham and Ishmael were raising the foundation of the Kaaba, praying for Allah to accept their work. They acknowledged that Allah is All-Hearing and All-Knowing.

Verse 128

رَبَّنَا وَاجْعَلْنَا مُسْلِمَيْنِ لَكَ وَمِنْ ذُرِّيَّتِنَا أُمَّةً مُسْلِمَةً لَكَ وَأَرِنَا مَنَاسِكَنَا وَتُبْ عَلَيْنَا ۖ إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ التَّوَّابُ الرَّحِيمُ

Our Lord! Make us both ˹fully˺ submit to You and from our descendants a nation that will submit to you. Show us our rituals, and turn to us in grace. You are truly the Accepter of Repentance, Most Merciful.

Our Lord, and make us steadfast upon Islam, submissive to Your commands, and make from our descendants a nation submissive to You, in faith, and make us see the landmarks of our worship to You, and forgive our sins. Indeed, You are the Ever-Accepting of Repentance, the Most Merciful to Your servants.

Abraham and Ishmael ask Allah to make them and their descendants submit to Him, to show them the ways of worship, and to accept their repentance. They acknowledge Allah as the Accepter of Repentance and the Most Merciful.

Verse 129

رَبَّنَا وَابْعَثْ فِيهِمْ رَسُولًا مِنْهُمْ يَتْلُو عَلَيْهِمْ آيَاتِكَ وَيُعَلِّمُهُمُ الْكِتَابَ وَالْحِكْمَةَ وَيُزَكِّيهِمْ ۚ إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ الْعَزِيزُ الْحَكِيمُ

Our Lord! Raise from among them a messenger who will recite to them Your revelations, teach them the Book and wisdom, and purify them. Indeed, You ˹alone˺ are the Almighty, All-Wise.”

Our Lord, and send forth in this nation a messenger from the descendants of Ishmael who will recite to them Your verses and teach them the Quran and the Sunnah, and purify them from polytheism and bad morals. Indeed, You are the Almighty, Whom nothing can prevent, the Wise, who places things in their proper places.

They pray for a messenger to come from among them, who will recite Allah's verses, teach the Quran and wisdom, and purify the people. They recognize Allah as the Almighty and All-Wise.

Verse 130

وَمَنْ يَرْغَبُ عَنْ مِلَّةِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ إِلَّا مَنْ سَفِهَ نَفْسَهُ ۚ وَلَقَدِ اصْطَفَيْنَاهُ فِي الدُّنْيَا ۖ وَإِنَّهُ فِي الْآخِرَةِ لَمِنَ الصَّالِحِينَ

And who would reject the faith of Abraham except a fool! We certainly chose him in this life, and in the Hereafter he will surely be among the righteous.

And no one turns away from the religion of Abraham - which is Islam - except one who is foolish and ignorant. And We have chosen Abraham in this world as a prophet and messenger, and indeed he, in the Hereafter, will be among the righteous who have the highest ranks.

This verse states that only a fool would reject Abraham's faith. Allah chose Abraham in this world, and in the Hereafter he will be among the righteous.

Verse 131

إِذْ قَالَ لَهُ رَبُّهُ أَسْلِمْ ۖ قَالَ أَسْلَمْتُ لِرَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ

When his Lord ordered him, “Submit ˹to My Will˺,” he responded, “I submit to the Lord of all worlds.”

And the reason for this choice is his hastening to Islam without hesitation, when his Lord said to him: Devote yourself to Allah in submission to Him. So, Abraham responded and said: I have submitted to the Lord of the Worlds in sincerity, monotheism, love and turning to Him.

This verse highlights Abraham's immediate submission to Allah's command, declaring his devotion to the Lord of all worlds.

Verse 132

وَوَصَّىٰ بِهَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بَنِيهِ وَيَعْقُوبُ يَا بَنِيَّ إِنَّ اللَّهَ اصْطَفَىٰ لَكُمُ الدِّينَ فَلَا تَمُوتُنَّ إِلَّا وَأَنْتُمْ مُسْلِمُونَ

This was the advice of Abraham—as well as Jacob—to his children, ˹saying˺, “Indeed, Allah has chosen for you this faith; so do not die except in ˹a state of full˺ submission.”

And Abraham and Jacob urged their sons to be steadfast upon Islam, saying: O our sons, indeed Allah has chosen for you this religion - which is the religion of Islam that Muhammad, peace and blessings be upon him, brought - so do not depart from it during your lives, and let not death come to you except while you are upon it.

Abraham and Jacob advised their children to remain steadfast in Islam and not to die except in a state of submission to Allah.

Verse 133

أَمْ كُنْتُمْ شُهَدَاءَ إِذْ حَضَرَ يَعْقُوبَ الْمَوْتُ إِذْ قَالَ لِبَنِيهِ مَا تَعْبُدُونَ مِنْ بَعْدِي قَالُوا نَعْبُدُ إِلَٰهَكَ وَإِلَٰهَ آبَائِكَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ وَإِسْمَاعِيلَ وَإِسْحَاقَ إِلَٰهًا وَاحِدًا وَنَحْنُ لَهُ مُسْلِمُونَ

Or did you witness when death came to Jacob? He asked his children, “Who will you worship after my passing?” They replied, “We will ˹continue to˺ worship your God, the God of your forefathers—Abraham, Ishmael, and Isaac—the One God. And to Him we ˹all˺ submit.”

Were you, O Jews, witnesses when death came to Jacob, when he gathered his sons and asked them what they would worship after his death? They said: We will worship your God and the God of your fathers, Abraham, Ishmael, and Isaac, one God, and to Him we are submissive and humble.

This verse mentions Jacob asking his children who they will worship after him. They affirmed that they will worship Allah, the God of Abraham, Ishmael, and Isaac, submitting to Him alone.

Verse 134

تِلْكَ أُمَّةٌ قَدْ خَلَتْ ۖ لَهَا مَا كَسَبَتْ وَلَكُمْ مَا كَسَبْتُمْ ۖ وَلَا تُسْأَلُونَ عَمَّا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ

That was a community that had already gone before. For them is what they earned and for you is what you have earned. And you will not be accountable for what they have done.

That was a nation of your forefathers that has passed away. They had their deeds, and you will have your deeds. You will not be questioned about their actions, and they will not be questioned about your actions. And everyone will be recompensed for what he did; no one will be punished for the sin of another, and no one will benefit except from his faith and righteousness.

This verse clarifies that past communities are accountable for their own deeds, and each person is responsible for their actions and will be judged accordingly.

Verse 135

وَقَالُوا كُونُوا هُودًا أَوْ نَصَارَىٰ تَهْتَدُوا ۗ قُلْ بَلْ مِلَّةَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ حَنِيفًا ۖ وَمَا كَانَ مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ

The Jews and Christians each say, “Follow our faith to be ˹rightly˺ guided.” Say, ˹O Prophet,˺ “No! We follow the faith of Abraham, the upright—who was not a polytheist.”

The Jews said to the community of Muhammad, may Allah bless him and grant him peace: "Enter into the religion of Judaism and you will find guidance." And the Christians said the same to them. Say to them - O Messenger -: Rather, guidance is that we all follow the religion of Abraham, who turned away from every false religion to the religion of truth, and he was not one of those who associated partners with Allah the Almighty.

This verse addresses the claims of Jews and Christians that their faith is the only path to guidance. It asserts that true guidance lies in following the way of Abraham, a man of pure monotheism, who did not associate partners with Allah.

Verse 136

قُولُوا آمَنَّا بِاللَّهِ وَمَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْنَا وَمَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَىٰ إِبْرَاهِيمَ وَإِسْمَاعِيلَ وَإِسْحَاقَ وَيَعْقُوبَ وَالْأَسْبَاطِ وَمَا أُوتِيَ مُوسَىٰ وَعِيسَىٰ وَمَا أُوتِيَ النَّبِيُّونَ مِنْ رَبِّهِمْ لَا نُفَرِّقُ بَيْنَ أَحَدٍ مِنْهُمْ وَنَحْنُ لَهُ مُسْلِمُونَ

Say, ˹O believers,˺ “We believe in Allah and what has been revealed to us; and what was revealed to Abraham, Ishmael, Isaac, Jacob, and his descendants; and what was given to Moses, Jesus, and other prophets from their Lord. We make no distinction between any of them. And to Allah we all submit.”

Say - O believers - to these Jews and Christians: We have believed in Allah, the One God, the One who is rightfully worshipped, and in what has been revealed to us from the Quran which Allah revealed to His Prophet and Messenger Muhammad, may Allah bless him and grant him peace, and what was revealed from the scriptures to Abraham and his two sons, Ishmael and Isaac, and to Jacob and the Tribes - who are the prophets from the offspring of Jacob who were in the twelve tribes of the Children of Israel - and what was given to Moses from the Torah, and to Jesus from the Gospel, and what was given to all the prophets from the revelation of their Lord. We do not differentiate between any of them in belief, and we are submissive to Allah in obedience and worship.

This verse calls on believers to affirm their belief in Allah, the Quran, and all prophets, including Abraham, Ishmael, Isaac, Jacob, Moses, and Jesus, without making any distinction between them. It emphasizes submission to Allah alone.

Verse 137

فَإِنْ آمَنُوا بِمِثْلِ مَا آمَنْتُمْ بِهِ فَقَدِ اهْتَدَوْا ۖ وَإِنْ تَوَلَّوْا فَإِنَّمَا هُمْ فِي شِقَاقٍ ۖ فَسَيَكْفِيكَهُمُ اللَّهُ ۚ وَهُوَ السَّمِيعُ الْعَلِيمُ

So if they believe in what you believe, then they will indeed be ˹rightly˺ guided. But if they turn away, they are simply opposed ˹to the truth˺. But Allah will spare you their evil. For He is the All-Hearing, All-Knowing.

So, if the disbelievers from the Jews and Christians and others believe in the like of what you believe in, which the Messenger came with, then they have been guided to the truth. But if they turn away, then they are in great dissension. So, Allah will suffice you, O Messenger, against their evil and will grant you victory over them. And He is the All-Hearing of your words, the All-Knowing of your circumstances.

This verse states that if others believe in what the believers believe, then they are rightly guided. If they turn away, they are in opposition to the truth. Allah will protect believers from any harm or opposition they face.

Verse 138

صِبْغَةَ اللَّهِ ۖ وَمَنْ أَحْسَنُ مِنَ اللَّهِ صِبْغَةً ۖ وَنَحْنُ لَهُ عَابِدُونَ

This is the ˹natural˺ Way of Allah. And who is better than Allah in ordaining a way? And we worship ˹none but˺ Him.

Adhere to the religion of Allah upon which He has created you, for there is nothing better than the nature of Allah upon which He has created mankind. So adhere to it and say, "We are submissive and obedient to our Lord in our following of the religion of Abraham."

This verse emphasizes the natural path of Allah, stating that there is no better way than the one that Allah has set. It encourages adherence to the faith of Abraham and submission to Allah alone.

Verse 139

قُلْ أَتُحَاجُّونَنَا فِي اللَّهِ وَهُوَ رَبُّنَا وَرَبُّكُمْ وَلَنَا أَعْمَالُنَا وَلَكُمْ أَعْمَالُكُمْ وَنَحْنُ لَهُ مُخْلِصُونَ

Say, “Would you dispute with us about Allah, while He is our Lord and your Lord? We are accountable for our deeds and you for yours. And we are devoted to Him ˹alone˺.

Say - O Messenger, to the People of the Book -: Do you argue with us about the Oneness of Allah and devotion to Him, while He is the Lord of all the worlds, not specific to one people over another? To us are our deeds, and to you are your deeds, and we are devoted to Allah in worship and obedience, we do not associate anything with Him, nor do we worship anyone other than Him.

This verse challenges those who dispute with believers about Allah. It clarifies that Allah is the Lord of all, and that all will be accountable for their own deeds. It affirms the devotion of believers to Allah alone.

Verse 140

أَمْ تَقُولُونَ إِنَّ إِبْرَاهِيمَ وَإِسْمَاعِيلَ وَإِسْحَاقَ وَيَعْقُوبَ وَالْأَسْبَاطَ كَانُوا هُودًا أَوْ نَصَارَىٰ ۗ قُلْ أَأَنْتُمْ أَعْلَمُ أَمِ اللَّهُ ۗ وَمَنْ أَظْلَمُ مِمَّنْ كَتَمَ شَهَادَةً عِنْدَهُ مِنَ اللَّهِ ۗ وَمَا اللَّهُ بِغَافِلٍ عَمَّا تَعْمَلُونَ

Or do you claim that Abraham, Ishmael, Isaac, Jacob, and his descendants were all Jews or Christians?” Say, “Who is more knowledgeable: you or Allah?” Who does more wrong than those who hide the testimony they received from Allah? And Allah is never unaware of what you do.

Or do you say, arguing about Allah: That Abraham, Ishmael, Isaac, Jacob, and the Tribes - who are the prophets who were in the twelve tribes of the Children of Israel from the descendants of Jacob - were upon the religion of Judaism or Christianity? And this is a lie; for they were sent and died before the Torah and the Gospel were revealed. Say to them - O Messenger -: Are you more knowledgeable about their religion or Allah the Almighty? And He has informed in the Quran that they were monotheists and Muslims. And there is no one more unjust than you when you conceal a testimony that is established with you from Allah the Almighty, and claim the opposite, fabricating lies about Allah. And Allah is not unaware of any of your actions, but He is the One who enumerates them and will recompense you for them.

This verse questions the claim that Abraham and his descendants were Jews or Christians, clarifying that they lived before Judaism and Christianity. It accuses those who hide the truth they received from Allah of wrongdoing and reminds that Allah is aware of their actions.

Verse 141

تِلْكَ أُمَّةٌ قَدْ خَلَتْ ۖ لَهَا مَا كَسَبَتْ وَلَكُمْ مَا كَسَبْتُمْ ۖ وَلَا تُسْأَلُونَ عَمَّا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ

That was a community that had already gone before. For them is what they earned and for you is what you have earned. And you will not be accountable for what they have done.

That was a community that has passed away, to them is what they earned and to you is what you earned. And you will not be asked about their actions, and they will not be asked about your actions. And in the verse, there is a cutting off of attachment to the creation, and not being deceived by association with them, and that the lesson is in believing in Allah and worshipping Him alone, and following His messengers, and that whoever disbelieves in one of the messengers has disbelieved in all the messengers.

This verse emphasizes the individual accountability of each community, stating that each group will be responsible for their own deeds. It teaches that one's relationship with Allah is personal and not based on heritage.

Verse 142

سَيَقُولُ السُّفَهَاءُ مِنَ النَّاسِ مَا وَلَّاهُمْ عَنْ قِبْلَتِهِمُ الَّتِي كَانُوا عَلَيْهَا ۚ قُلْ لِلَّهِ الْمَشْرِقُ وَالْمَغْرِبُ ۚ يَهْدِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ إِلَىٰ صِرَاطٍ مُسْتَقِيمٍ

The foolish among the people will ask, “Why did they turn away from the direction of prayer they used to face?” Say, ˹O Prophet,˺ “The east and west belong ˹only˺ to Allah. He guides whoever He wills to the Straight Path.”

The ignorant and weak-minded among the Jews and their ilk will say, in mockery and objection: 'What has turned these Muslims away from their qiblah which they used to face in prayer at the beginning of Islam (which is "Bayt al-Maqdis")?' Say to them - O Messenger -: 'To Allah belong the east and the west and what is between them, so no direction is outside of His dominion. He guides whom He wills of His servants to the straight path of guidance.' And in this is an indication that the whole matter belongs to Allah, in complying with His commands, so wherever He directs us, we turn.

This verse addresses the criticism of those who questioned the change of the prayer direction (Qibla) from Jerusalem to Mecca. It emphasizes that all directions belong to Allah and He guides whom He wills to the right path.

Verse 143

وَكَذَٰلِكَ جَعَلْنَاكُمْ أُمَّةً وَسَطًا لِتَكُونُوا شُهَدَاءَ عَلَى النَّاسِ وَيَكُونَ الرَّسُولُ عَلَيْكُمْ شَهِيدًا ۗ وَمَا جَعَلْنَا الْقِبْلَةَ الَّتِي كُنْتَ عَلَيْهَا إِلَّا لِنَعْلَمَ مَنْ يَتَّبِعُ الرَّسُولَ مِمَّنْ يَنْقَلِبُ عَلَىٰ عَقِبَيْهِ ۚ وَإِنْ كَانَتْ لَكَبِيرَةً إِلَّا عَلَى الَّذِينَ هَدَى اللَّهُ ۗ وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ لِيُضِيعَ إِيمَانَكُمْ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ بِالنَّاسِ لَرَءُوفٌ رَحِيمٌ

And so We have made you ˹believers˺ an upright community so that you may be witnesses over humanity and that the Messenger may be a witness over you. We assigned your former direction of prayer only to distinguish those who would remain faithful to the Messenger from those who would lose faith. It was certainly a difficult test except for those ˹rightly˺ guided by Allah. And Allah would never discount your ˹previous acts of˺ faith. Surely Allah is Ever Gracious and Most Merciful to humanity.

And as We have guided you - O Muslims - to the correct path in religion, We have made you a chosen and just nation, so that you may be witnesses over the nations on the Day of Judgment that their messengers delivered the messages of their Lord, and the Messenger will be a witness over you on the Day of Judgment that he delivered the message of his Lord to you. And We did not make - O Messenger - the qiblah of "Bayt al-Maqdis" which you were on, then We turned you away from it to the Kaaba in "Mecca", except to make manifest what We knew in eternity; knowledge related to reward and punishment, to distinguish who follows and obeys you and faces with you wherever you turn, and who is weak in faith, thus turning back, an apostate from his religion due to his doubt and hypocrisy. And indeed, this matter, which is the turning of the Muslim in his prayer from facing Bayt al-Maqdis to facing the Kaaba, is indeed heavy and difficult, except for those whom Allah has guided and favored with faith and piety. And Allah would not waste your faith in Him and your following of His Messenger, and invalidate your prayers towards the previous qiblah. Indeed, He is, glory be to Him, Most Kind and Merciful to people.

Muslims are described as a just and balanced community, chosen to be witnesses for humanity. The change of the Qibla was a test to distinguish the true believers from those who were weak in faith. Allah's grace and mercy are highlighted.

Verse 144

قَدْ نَرَىٰ تَقَلُّبَ وَجْهِكَ فِي السَّمَاءِ ۖ فَلَنُوَلِّيَنَّكَ قِبْلَةً تَرْضَاهَا ۚ فَوَلِّ وَجْهَكَ شَطْرَ الْمَسْجِدِ الْحَرَامِ ۚ وَحَيْثُ مَا كُنْتُمْ فَوَلُّوا وُجُوهَكُمْ شَطْرَهُ ۗ وَإِنَّ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ لَيَعْلَمُونَ أَنَّهُ الْحَقُّ مِنْ رَبِّهِمْ ۗ وَمَا اللَّهُ بِغَافِلٍ عَمَّا يَعْمَلُونَ

Indeed, We see you ˹O Prophet˺ turning your face towards heaven. Now We will make you turn towards a direction ˹of prayer˺ that will please you. So turn your face towards the Sacred Mosque ˹in Mecca˺—wherever you are, turn your faces towards it. Those who were given the Scripture certainly know this to be the truth from their Lord. And Allah is never unaware of what they do.

We have certainly seen the turning of your face - O Messenger - towards the sky, time after time, awaiting the revelation to descend upon you concerning the qiblah, so We will turn you from "Bayt al-Maqdis" to a qiblah that you love and are pleased with, which is the direction of the Sacred Mosque in "Mecca", so turn your face towards it. And wherever you are - O Muslims - and you want to pray, then turn towards the Sacred Mosque. And those whom Allah has given knowledge of the Book, from the Jews and Christians, certainly know that your turning to the Kaaba is the truth established in their books. And Allah is not unaware of what these objectors and doubters do, and He will recompense them for that.

This verse confirms that the Prophet's (peace be upon him) desire for the Qibla to be changed to the Sacred Mosque (Kaaba) in Mecca was fulfilled by Allah. Muslims are commanded to face the Kaaba in prayer, and it is confirmed that the People of the Book knew this to be the truth.

Verse 145

وَلَئِنْ أَتَيْتَ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ بِكُلِّ آيَةٍ مَا تَبِعُوا قِبْلَتَكَ ۚ وَمَا أَنْتَ بِتَابِعٍ قِبْلَتَهُمْ ۚ وَمَا بَعْضُهُمْ بِتَابِعٍ قِبْلَةَ بَعْضٍ ۚ وَلَئِنِ اتَّبَعْتَ أَهْوَاءَهُمْ مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا جَاءَكَ مِنَ الْعِلْمِ ۙ إِنَّكَ إِذًا لَمِنَ الظَّالِمِينَ

Even if you were to bring every proof to the People of the Book, they would not accept your direction ˹of prayer˺, nor would you accept theirs; nor would any of them accept the direction ˹of prayer˺ of another. And if you were to follow their desires after ˹all˺ the knowledge that has come to you, then you would certainly be one of the wrongdoers.

And if you were to bring - O Messenger - those who were given the Torah and the Gospel every proof and evidence that your turning to the Kaaba in prayer is the truth from Allah, they would not follow your qiblah out of stubbornness and arrogance, and you would not be a follower of their qiblah again, and some of them do not follow the qiblah of others. And if you were to follow their desires regarding the qiblah and other matters after what has come to you of knowledge that you are on the truth and they are on falsehood, then at that time, you would surely be among the wrongdoers to themselves. And this is an address to the entire nation, and it is a threat and a warning to whoever follows the desires of those who oppose the Sharia of Islam.

Even with all evidence, the People of the Book would not accept the new Qibla. Muslims are warned not to follow their desires and to remain steadfast in the truth that has been revealed to them; deviating would be wrong.

Verse 146

الَّذِينَ آتَيْنَاهُمُ الْكِتَابَ يَعْرِفُونَهُ كَمَا يَعْرِفُونَ أَبْنَاءَهُمْ ۖ وَإِنَّ فَرِيقًا مِنْهُمْ لَيَكْتُمُونَ الْحَقَّ وَهُمْ يَعْلَمُونَ

Those We have given the Scripture recognize this ˹Prophet˺ as they recognize their own children. Yet a group of them hides the truth knowingly.

Those whom We gave the Torah and the Gospel, from the rabbis of the Jews and the scholars of the Christians, know that Muhammad, may Allah's peace and blessings be upon him, is the Messenger of Allah, by his descriptions mentioned in their books, just as they know their own sons. And indeed, a group of them conceal the truth while they know its authenticity and the confirmation of its descriptions.

This verse states that those who received previous scriptures recognize Prophet Muhammad as they recognize their own children. Yet, some of them knowingly hide the truth about his prophethood.

Verse 147

الْحَقُّ مِنْ رَبِّكَ ۖ فَلَا تَكُونَنَّ مِنَ الْمُمْتَرِينَ

˹This is˺ the truth from your Lord, so do not ever be one of those who doubt.

What has been revealed to you, O Prophet, is the truth from your Lord, so do not be among those who doubt it. And this, even if it is addressed to the Messenger, may Allah's peace and blessings be upon him, it is directed to the nation.

The Quran is the ultimate truth from Allah. Believers should not doubt its divine nature and authenticity.

Verse 148

وَلِكُلٍّ وِجْهَةٌ هُوَ مُوَلِّيهَا ۖ فَاسْتَبِقُوا الْخَيْرَاتِ ۚ أَيْنَ مَا تَكُونُوا يَأْتِ بِكُمُ اللَّهُ جَمِيعًا ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ

Everyone turns to their own direction ˹of prayer˺. So compete with one another in doing good. Wherever you are, Allah will bring you all together ˹for judgment˺. Surely Allah is Most Capable of everything.

For every nation, there is a direction to which each of them turns in their prayer, so hasten, O believers, competing to do the righteous deeds that Allah has prescribed for you in the religion of Islam. And Allah will gather you all on the Day of Resurrection from wherever you may be. Indeed, Allah is over all things competent.

Each community has its direction of prayer, but Muslims are urged to compete in doing good deeds. Ultimately, Allah will gather everyone for judgment.

Verse 149

وَمِنْ حَيْثُ خَرَجْتَ فَوَلِّ وَجْهَكَ شَطْرَ الْمَسْجِدِ الْحَرَامِ ۖ وَإِنَّهُ لَلْحَقُّ مِنْ رَبِّكَ ۗ وَمَا اللَّهُ بِغَافِلٍ عَمَّا تَعْمَلُونَ

Wherever you are ˹O Prophet˺, turn your face towards the Sacred Mosque. This is certainly the truth from your Lord. And Allah is never unaware of what you ˹all˺ do.

And from wherever you depart, O Prophet, traveling, and you want to pray, then turn your face toward the Sacred Mosque. And indeed, your turning towards it is the established truth from your Lord. And Allah is not unaware of what you do, and He will recompense you for that.

Prophet Muhammad is commanded to turn his face towards the Sacred Mosque (Kaaba) during prayer, affirming that this is the truth from Allah.

Verse 150

وَمِنْ حَيْثُ خَرَجْتَ فَوَلِّ وَجْهَكَ شَطْرَ الْمَسْجِدِ الْحَرَامِ ۚ وَحَيْثُ مَا كُنْتُمْ فَوَلُّوا وُجُوهَكُمْ شَطْرَهُ لِئَلَّا يَكُونَ لِلنَّاسِ عَلَيْكُمْ حُجَّةٌ إِلَّا الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا مِنْهُمْ فَلَا تَخْشَوْهُمْ وَاخْشَوْنِي وَلِأُتِمَّ نِعْمَتِي عَلَيْكُمْ وَلَعَلَّكُمْ تَهْتَدُونَ

Wherever you are ˹O Prophet˺, turn your face towards the Sacred Mosque. And wherever you ˹believers˺ are, face towards it, so that people will have no argument against you, except the wrongdoers among them. Do not fear them; fear Me, so that I may ˹continue to˺ perfect My favour upon you and so you may be ˹rightly˺ guided.

And from wherever you depart, O Prophet, turn towards the Sacred Mosque, and wherever you are, O Muslims, in any region of the earth, turn your faces towards the Sacred Mosque, so that the people who oppose you will have no argument against you with disputes and debates, after this turning toward it, except for those among them who are unjust and obstinate, so they will remain in their arguments. So do not fear them and fear Me by obeying My command and avoiding My prohibitions, and so that I may perfect My favor upon you by choosing the most complete of laws for you, and perhaps you may be guided to the truth and what is correct.

Muslims are commanded to face the Sacred Mosque during prayer, so that people will have no argument against them except the wrongdoers. Muslims should fear Allah and follow his guidance.

Verse 151

كَمَا أَرْسَلْنَا فِيكُمْ رَسُولًا مِنْكُمْ يَتْلُو عَلَيْكُمْ آيَاتِنَا وَيُزَكِّيكُمْ وَيُعَلِّمُكُمُ الْكِتَابَ وَالْحِكْمَةَ وَيُعَلِّمُكُمْ مَا لَمْ تَكُونُوا تَعْلَمُونَ

Since We have sent you a messenger from among yourselves—reciting to you Our revelations, purifying you, teaching you the Book and wisdom, and teaching you what you never knew—

Just as We have bestowed upon you the favor of facing the Kaaba, We have sent among you a messenger from among yourselves who recites to you the verses that make clear the truth from falsehood, and purifies you from the impurity of polytheism and bad morals, and teaches you the Book and the Sunnah and the laws of the Sharia, and teaches you from the news of the prophets and the stories of the previous nations that which you did not know.

Allah sent a messenger from among the believers to recite the Quran, purify them, and teach them the Book and wisdom, things that they never knew before.

Verse 152

فَاذْكُرُونِي أَذْكُرْكُمْ وَاشْكُرُوا لِي وَلَا تَكْفُرُونِ

remember Me; I will remember you. And thank Me, and never be ungrateful.

Allah Almighty commanded the believers to remember Him, and promised the best reward for it, which is praise in the highest assembly for those who remember Him, and single Me out, O believers, with gratitude in word and deed and do not deny My favors upon you.

This verse emphasizes the importance of remembering Allah and being grateful to Him for His blessings and favors.

Verse 153

يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا اسْتَعِينُوا بِالصَّبْرِ وَالصَّلَاةِ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ مَعَ الصَّابِرِينَ

O believers! Seek comfort in patience and prayer. Allah is truly with those who are patient.

O you who believe, seek help from Allah in all your affairs: through patience in times of tribulation and calamity, and abandoning sins and misdeeds, and patience in acts of obedience and piety, and prayer through which the soul finds peace, and it prevents indecency and wrongdoing. Indeed, Allah is with the patient through His help, guidance and facilitation. And in the verse is: The affirmation of Allah's special being with the believers, which necessitates what has been mentioned previously; as for the general being, which necessitates knowledge and encompassing, it is for all of creation.

Believers are encouraged to seek help from Allah through patience and prayer, for He is with those who are patient.

Verse 154

وَلَا تَقُولُوا لِمَنْ يُقْتَلُ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ أَمْوَاتٌ ۚ بَلْ أَحْيَاءٌ وَلَٰكِنْ لَا تَشْعُرُونَ

Never say that those martyred in the cause of Allah are dead—in fact, they are alive! But you do not perceive it.

And do not say - O believers - about those who are killed striving in the way of Allah: 'They are dead.' Rather, they are alive with a special life in their graves, the nature of which is known only to Allah - the Exalted - but you do not perceive it. And in this is evidence of the bliss of the grave.

This verse clarifies that martyrs in the cause of Allah are not dead but are alive in a way we cannot comprehend. This highlights the honor and reward for those who sacrifice for their faith.

Verse 155

وَلَنَبْلُوَنَّكُمْ بِشَيْءٍ مِنَ الْخَوْفِ وَالْجُوعِ وَنَقْصٍ مِنَ الْأَمْوَالِ وَالْأَنْفُسِ وَالثَّمَرَاتِ ۗ وَبَشِّرِ الصَّابِرِينَ

We will certainly test you with a touch of fear and famine and loss of property, life, and crops. Give good news to those who patiently endure—

And We will surely test you with something of fear and hunger and a loss of wealth through difficulty in obtaining it, or its loss, and lives: by death or martyrdom in the way of Allah, and a loss of the fruits of palm trees, grapes, and grains, by the scarcity of their yield or their spoilage. And give glad tidings - O Prophet - to the patient ones for this and the like, with what will make them happy and pleased with the good consequences in this world and the Hereafter.

This verse states that Allah will test believers through various hardships like fear, hunger, and loss. It encourages patience during these trials, promising good news for those who endure.

Verse 156

الَّذِينَ إِذَا أَصَابَتْهُمْ مُصِيبَةٌ قَالُوا إِنَّا لِلَّهِ وَإِنَّا إِلَيْهِ رَاجِعُونَ

who, when faced with a disaster, say, “Surely to Allah we belong and to Him we will ˹all˺ return.”

One of the characteristics of these patient ones is that when they are afflicted with something they dislike, they say: 'Indeed, we are owned slaves of Allah, managed by His command and disposition; He does with us what He wills, and indeed, we are returning to Him by death, then by the resurrection for reckoning and recompense.'

This verse describes the reaction of patient believers when afflicted; they acknowledge their belonging to Allah and their eventual return to Him, accepting His decree.

Verse 157

أُولَٰئِكَ عَلَيْهِمْ صَلَوَاتٌ مِنْ رَبِّهِمْ وَرَحْمَةٌ ۖ وَأُولَٰئِكَ هُمُ الْمُهْتَدُونَ

They are the ones who will receive Allah’s blessings and mercy. And it is they who are ˹rightly˺ guided.

Those are the patient ones for whom there is praise from their Lord and great mercy from Him, and those are the rightly guided.

This verse highlights the rewards for those who are patient in the face of adversity: they will receive Allah's blessings, mercy and guidance.

Verse 158

إِنَّ الصَّفَا وَالْمَرْوَةَ مِنْ شَعَائِرِ اللَّهِ ۖ فَمَنْ حَجَّ الْبَيْتَ أَوِ اعْتَمَرَ فَلَا جُنَاحَ عَلَيْهِ أَنْ يَطَّوَّفَ بِهِمَا ۚ وَمَنْ تَطَوَّعَ خَيْرًا فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ شَاكِرٌ عَلِيمٌ

Indeed, ˹the hills of˺ Ṣafa and Marwah are among the symbols of Allah. So whoever performs the pilgrimage or minor pilgrimage, let them walk between ˹the two hills˺. And whoever does good willingly, Allah is truly Appreciative, All-Knowing.

Indeed, as-Safa and al-Marwa - and they are two small mountains near the Kaaba on the eastern side - are among the manifest landmarks of the religion of Allah, where Allah has commanded His servants to strive between them. So whoever intends the Kaaba for pilgrimage or Umrah, there is no sin or blame upon him in that he strives between them; rather, it is obligatory upon him to do so. And whoever does good deeds voluntarily, sincerely for Allah, then indeed Allah is Appreciative, rewarding the little with much, Knowing of His servants' deeds, so He does not waste them, nor does He shortchange anyone the weight of an atom.

This verse explains that Safa and Marwah are symbols of Allah, making the Sa'i (walking between them) a necessary act during Hajj and Umrah, while encouraging voluntary good deeds, noting Allah's appreciation and knowledge.

Verse 159

إِنَّ الَّذِينَ يَكْتُمُونَ مَا أَنْزَلْنَا مِنَ الْبَيِّنَاتِ وَالْهُدَىٰ مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا بَيَّنَّاهُ لِلنَّاسِ فِي الْكِتَابِ ۙ أُولَٰئِكَ يَلْعَنُهُمُ اللَّهُ وَيَلْعَنُهُمُ اللَّاعِنُونَ

Those who hide the clear proofs and guidance that We have revealed—after We made it clear for humanity in the Book—will be condemned by Allah and ˹all˺ those who condemn.

Indeed, those who conceal what We have sent down of the clear verses indicating the prophethood of Muhammad, peace and blessings be upon him, and what he brought, and they are the Jewish scholars and the Christian scholars, and others who conceal what Allah has revealed after We made it clear to people in the Torah and the Gospel, those Allah expels from His mercy, and all of creation invokes curses upon them.

This verse condemns those who hide the clear proofs and guidance of Allah revealed in scripture, particularly after it has been made clear to humanity. These people are subject to curses by Allah and all creation.

Verse 160

إِلَّا الَّذِينَ تَابُوا وَأَصْلَحُوا وَبَيَّنُوا فَأُولَٰئِكَ أَتُوبُ عَلَيْهِمْ ۚ وَأَنَا التَّوَّابُ الرَّحِيمُ

As for those who repent, mend their ways, and let the truth be known, they are the ones to whom I will turn ˹in forgiveness˺, for I am the Accepter of Repentance, Most Merciful.

Except those who return, seeking forgiveness from Allah for their sins, and amend what they have corrupted, and make clear what they have concealed, those, I accept their repentance and recompense them with forgiveness, and I am the Accepter of Repentance for those who repent from My servants, the Merciful to them; as I have guided them to repentance and accepted it from them.

This verse offers hope for those who repent from concealing the truth, mend their ways, and make clear what they concealed. Allah promises forgiveness for those who return to Him in sincerity.

Verse 161

إِنَّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا وَمَاتُوا وَهُمْ كُفَّارٌ أُولَٰئِكَ عَلَيْهِمْ لَعْنَةُ اللَّهِ وَالْمَلَائِكَةِ وَالنَّاسِ أَجْمَعِينَ

Surely those who disbelieve and die as disbelievers are condemned by Allah, the angels, and all of humanity.

Indeed, those who deny faith and conceal the truth, and continue upon that until they die, those are upon them the curse of Allah and the angels and all people in being expelled from His mercy.

This verse states that those who die as disbelievers face the condemnation of Allah, the angels, and all of humanity, signifying a severe consequence for their denial of faith.

Verse 162

خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا ۖ لَا يُخَفَّفُ عَنْهُمُ الْعَذَابُ وَلَا هُمْ يُنْظَرُونَ

They will be in Hell forever. Their punishment will not be lightened, nor will they be delayed ˹from it˺.

Abiding in the curse and the Fire, the punishment will not be lightened for them, nor will they be granted respite with an excuse to offer.

This verse clarifies that the disbelievers will abide in Hell forever, where their punishment will not be lightened or delayed, emphasizing the permanence of their suffering.

Verse 163

وَإِلَٰهُكُمْ إِلَٰهٌ وَاحِدٌ ۖ لَا إِلَٰهَ إِلَّا هُوَ الرَّحْمَٰنُ الرَّحِيمُ

Your God is ˹only˺ One God. There is no god ˹worthy of worship˺ except Him—the Most Compassionate, Most Merciful.

And your God - O people - is one God, unique in His essence, names, attributes, actions, and in the servitude of His creation to Him. There is no deity worthy of worship except Him, the Most Gracious, described with mercy in His essence and actions for all of creation, the Most Merciful to the believers.

This verse emphasizes the Oneness of Allah (*Tawheed*), declaring that there is no deity worthy of worship except Him. *Ar-Rahman* (The Most Compassionate) and *Ar-Rahim* (The Most Merciful) highlight Allah's mercy toward all and especially the believers.

Verse 164

إِنَّ فِي خَلْقِ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ وَاخْتِلَافِ اللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ وَالْفُلْكِ الَّتِي تَجْرِي فِي الْبَحْرِ بِمَا يَنْفَعُ النَّاسَ وَمَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ مِنْ مَاءٍ فَأَحْيَا بِهِ الْأَرْضَ بَعْدَ مَوْتِهَا وَبَثَّ فِيهَا مِنْ كُلِّ دَابَّةٍ وَتَصْرِيفِ الرِّيَاحِ وَالسَّحَابِ الْمُسَخَّرِ بَيْنَ السَّمَاءِ وَالْأَرْضِ لَآيَاتٍ لِقَوْمٍ يَعْقِلُونَ

Indeed, in the creation of the heavens and the earth; the alternation of the day and the night; the ships that sail the sea for the benefit of humanity; the rain sent down by Allah from the skies, reviving the earth after its death; the scattering of all kinds of creatures throughout; the shifting of the winds; and the clouds drifting between the heavens and the earth—˹in all of this˺ are surely signs for people of understanding.

Indeed, in the creation of the heavens with their height and vastness, and the earth with its mountains, plains, and seas, and in the alternation of night and day with their length and shortness, darkness and light, and their succession where each replaces the other, and in the ships that sail the seas, carrying what benefits people, and what Allah sends down from the sky of rainwater, reviving the earth, so it becomes green and beautiful after being dry and barren, and what Allah has spread on it of every creature that crawls on the face of the earth, and what He has bestowed upon you of turning and directing the winds, and the clouds controlled between the sky and the earth - indeed in all the previous signs are indications of the oneness of Allah, and His great blessings, for a people who understand the locations of the arguments, and comprehend His proofs, may He be glorified, of His oneness, and His deserving worship alone.

This verse points to signs of Allah's power and wisdom in creation: the heavens, earth, day/night cycle, ships, rain, living creatures, winds, and clouds. These are all reminders for people of understanding to recognize Allah's oneness and blessings.

Verse 165

وَمِنَ النَّاسِ مَنْ يَتَّخِذُ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ أَنْدَادًا يُحِبُّونَهُمْ كَحُبِّ اللَّهِ ۖ وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا أَشَدُّ حُبًّا لِلَّهِ ۗ وَلَوْ يَرَى الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا إِذْ يَرَوْنَ الْعَذَابَ أَنَّ الْقُوَّةَ لِلَّهِ جَمِيعًا وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ شَدِيدُ الْعَذَابِ

Still there are some who take others as Allah’s equal—they love them as they should love Allah—but the ˹true˺ believers love Allah even more. If only the wrongdoers could see the ˹horrible˺ punishment ˹awaiting them˺, they would certainly realize that all power belongs to Allah and that Allah is indeed severe in punishment.

And despite these conclusive proofs, a group of people take besides Allah idols, statues, and allies, making them rivals to Allah Almighty, and giving them of love, veneration, and obedience what is not befitting except for Allah alone. And the believers are greater in love for Allah than the love of these disbelievers for Allah and their deities; because the believers have dedicated all their love to Allah, and those have associated others in love. And if those who wronged themselves with polytheism in the worldly life knew, when they witness the torment of the Hereafter, that Allah is the Unique in all power, and that Allah is severe in punishment, they would not have taken besides Allah deities to worship them besides Him, and to seek nearness to Him through them.

This verse contrasts true believers, whose love for Allah is absolute, with those who wrongly associate others with Him. It warns that on the Day of Judgment, the wrongdoers will realize that all power belongs to Allah alone and will face severe punishment.

Verse 166

إِذْ تَبَرَّأَ الَّذِينَ اتُّبِعُوا مِنَ الَّذِينَ اتَّبَعُوا وَرَأَوُا الْعَذَابَ وَتَقَطَّعَتْ بِهِمُ الْأَسْبَابُ

˹Consider the Day˺ when those who misled others will disown their followers—when they face the torment—and the bonds that united them will be cut off.

When they witness the punishment of the Hereafter, the leaders who were followed will disown those who followed them in polytheism, and all the ties that bound them in the world will be severed: from kinship, following, religion, and so on.

On the Day of Judgment, leaders who misled others will disown their followers, severing all worldly ties. This emphasizes the isolation and regret of those who rejected the truth.

Verse 167

وَقَالَ الَّذِينَ اتَّبَعُوا لَوْ أَنَّ لَنَا كَرَّةً فَنَتَبَرَّأَ مِنْهُمْ كَمَا تَبَرَّءُوا مِنَّا ۗ كَذَٰلِكَ يُرِيهِمُ اللَّهُ أَعْمَالَهُمْ حَسَرَاتٍ عَلَيْهِمْ ۖ وَمَا هُمْ بِخَارِجِينَ مِنَ النَّارِ

The ˹misled˺ followers will cry, “If only we could have a second chance, we would disown them as they disowned us.” And so Allah will make them remorseful of their misdeeds. And they will never ˹be able to˺ leave the Fire.
