And the followers will say: 'If only we could return to the world, then we would disavow these leaders, just as they have disavowed us.' And just as Allah shows them the severity of His punishment on the Day of Resurrection, He will show them their vain deeds as regrets upon them, and they will never leave the Fire.

The followers of misguidance will wish for a chance to disown their leaders as they were disowned. They will be filled with remorse for their deeds, facing eternal punishment in the Fire.

Verse 168

يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ كُلُوا مِمَّا فِي الْأَرْضِ حَلَالًا طَيِّبًا وَلَا تَتَّبِعُوا خُطُوَاتِ الشَّيْطَانِ ۚ إِنَّهُ لَكُمْ عَدُوٌّ مُبِينٌ

O humanity! Eat from what is lawful and good on the earth and do not follow Satan’s footsteps. He is truly your sworn enemy.

O people, eat from the provision of Allah that He has made lawful for you in the earth, which is pure and not impure, beneficial and not harmful, and do not follow the ways of Satan in making lawful and unlawful, and innovations and disobedience. Indeed, he is a clear enemy to you.

This verse calls on humanity to eat from the good and lawful provisions on Earth. It warns against following Satan, who is a sworn enemy, and not to follow his ways.

Verse 169

إِنَّمَا يَأْمُرُكُمْ بِالسُّوءِ وَالْفَحْشَاءِ وَأَنْ تَقُولُوا عَلَى اللَّهِ مَا لَا تَعْلَمُونَ

He only incites you to commit evil and indecency, and to claim against Allah what you do not know.

Satan only commands you with every evil shameful deed that harms you, and with every sin of extreme ugliness, and that you fabricate lies against Allah by prohibiting the lawful and other things without knowledge.

Satan incites evil, indecency, and fabricating lies against Allah. This verse emphasizes the importance of resisting Satan's temptations and adhering to truth and righteousness.

Verse 170

وَإِذَا قِيلَ لَهُمُ اتَّبِعُوا مَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ قَالُوا بَلْ نَتَّبِعُ مَا أَلْفَيْنَا عَلَيْهِ آبَاءَنَا ۗ أَوَلَوْ كَانَ آبَاؤُهُمْ لَا يَعْقِلُونَ شَيْئًا وَلَا يَهْتَدُونَ

When it is said to them, “Follow what Allah has revealed,” they reply, “No! We ˹only˺ follow what we found our forefathers practicing.” ˹Would they still do so,˺ even if their forefathers had ˹absolutely˺ no understanding or guidance?

And when the believers advise those who are misguided, saying: Follow what Allah has sent down of the Quran and guidance, they insist on imitating their polytheistic forefathers, saying: We do not follow your religion, but we follow that which we found our fathers upon. Do they follow their fathers even if they do not understand anything about Allah, nor do they perceive guidance?

This verse criticizes those who blindly follow their ancestors' traditions instead of the guidance revealed by Allah, even if their forefathers lacked understanding or guidance.

Verse 171

وَمَثَلُ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا كَمَثَلِ الَّذِي يَنْعِقُ بِمَا لَا يَسْمَعُ إِلَّا دُعَاءً وَنِدَاءً ۚ صُمٌّ بُكْمٌ عُمْيٌ فَهُمْ لَا يَعْقِلُونَ

The example of the disbelievers ˹not responding to the Messenger’s warning˺ is like a flock not comprehending the calls and cries of the shepherd. ˹They are wilfully˺ deaf, dumb and blind so they have no understanding.

And the description of those who disbelieve and their inviter to guidance and faith is like the description of the shepherd who shouts at the livestock and rebukes them, and they do not understand the meanings of his words, but only hear the call and the sound's echo. These disbelievers are deaf, having closed their ears to the truth; dumb, having silenced their tongues from speaking it; blind, their eyes do not see its clear proofs. So they do not use their minds in what benefits them.

This verse compares disbelievers to a flock that does not understand the shepherd's call. They are described as deaf, dumb, and blind to the truth, highlighting their willful ignorance.

Verse 172

يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا كُلُوا مِنْ طَيِّبَاتِ مَا رَزَقْنَاكُمْ وَاشْكُرُوا لِلَّهِ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ إِيَّاهُ تَعْبُدُونَ

O believers! Eat from the good things We have provided for you. And give thanks to Allah if you ˹truly˺ worship Him ˹alone˺.

O you who believe, eat from the delicious, lawful foods that We have provided for you, and do not be like the disbelievers who forbid good things and make lawful evil things. And give thanks to Allah for His great blessings upon you with your hearts, tongues, and limbs, if you are truly obedient to His command, hearing and obeying Him, worshipping Him alone without any partners.

Believers are instructed to eat from the good and lawful provisions Allah has provided and to express gratitude to Him if they truly worship Him alone.

Verse 173

إِنَّمَا حَرَّمَ عَلَيْكُمُ الْمَيْتَةَ وَالدَّمَ وَلَحْمَ الْخِنْزِيرِ وَمَا أُهِلَّ بِهِ لِغَيْرِ اللَّهِ ۖ فَمَنِ اضْطُرَّ غَيْرَ بَاغٍ وَلَا عَادٍ فَلَا إِثْمَ عَلَيْهِ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ

He has only forbidden you ˹to eat˺ carrion, blood, swine, and what is slaughtered in the name of any other than Allah. But if someone is compelled by necessity—neither driven by desire nor exceeding immediate need—they will not be sinful. Surely Allah is All-Forgiving, Most Merciful.

Allah has only forbidden you what harms you, such as carrion which has not been slaughtered according to Islamic law, flowing blood, pork, and sacrifices that have been slaughtered for other than Allah. And from Allah's favor upon you and His facilitation is that He has permitted you to eat these forbidden things in case of necessity. So whoever is compelled by necessity to eat something from them, not being unjust in eating beyond his need, nor transgressing the limits of Allah in what is permitted to him, then there is no sin upon him in that. Indeed, Allah is Forgiving to His servants, Merciful to them.

This verse specifies what is forbidden (carrion, blood, swine, and what is sacrificed to other than Allah) but permits consumption of these out of necessity, emphasizing Allah's forgiveness and mercy.

Verse 174

إِنَّ الَّذِينَ يَكْتُمُونَ مَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ مِنَ الْكِتَابِ وَيَشْتَرُونَ بِهِ ثَمَنًا قَلِيلًا ۙ أُولَٰئِكَ مَا يَأْكُلُونَ فِي بُطُونِهِمْ إِلَّا النَّارَ وَلَا يُكَلِّمُهُمُ اللَّهُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَلَا يُزَكِّيهِمْ وَلَهُمْ عَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌ

Indeed, those who hide Allah’s revelations, trading them for a fleeting gain consume nothing but fire into their bellies. Allah will neither speak to them on the Day of Judgment, nor will He purify them. And they will suffer a painful punishment.

Indeed, those who conceal what Allah has sent down in His books of the description of Muhammad, peace and blessings be upon him, and other than that of the truth, and are keen to take a small price from the worldly life in exchange for this concealment, these people do not eat in return for concealing the truth except for the fire of Hell blazing in their bellies, and Allah will not speak to them on the Day of Resurrection due to His anger and wrath upon them, nor will He purify them from the filth of their sins and disbelief, and they will have a painful punishment.

Those who conceal Allah's revelations for worldly gain will be punished with fire and will be denied Allah's mercy and purification on the Day of Judgment.

Verse 175

أُولَٰئِكَ الَّذِينَ اشْتَرَوُا الضَّلَالَةَ بِالْهُدَىٰ وَالْعَذَابَ بِالْمَغْفِرَةِ ۚ فَمَا أَصْبَرَهُمْ عَلَى النَّارِ

They are the ones who trade guidance for misguidance and forgiveness for punishment. How persistent are they in pursuit of the Fire!

Those who are characterized by these attributes have exchanged misguidance for guidance and Allah's punishment for His forgiveness, so how daring they are to the Fire by doing the deeds of the people of the Fire!! Allah is amazed by their boldness to do so, so be amazed - O people - by their audacity and their patience in the Fire and their stay in it. And this is in order to disdain them and to belittle their matter.

This verse highlights the grave consequences for those who exchange guidance for misguidance and Allah’s forgiveness for punishment, expressing astonishment at their pursuit of hellfire.

Verse 176

ذَٰلِكَ بِأَنَّ اللَّهَ نَزَّلَ الْكِتَابَ بِالْحَقِّ ۗ وَإِنَّ الَّذِينَ اخْتَلَفُوا فِي الْكِتَابِ لَفِي شِقَاقٍ بَعِيدٍ

That is because Allah has revealed the Book in truth. And surely those who differ regarding it are totally engrossed in opposition.

That punishment which they deserved was because Allah Almighty revealed His books to His messengers containing the clear truth, and they disbelieved in it. And indeed, those who differed about the Book, believing in some of it and disbelieving in some of it, are in a dispute and a departure far from righteousness and truth.

The reason for the severe punishment is that Allah revealed the truth through His books, and those who dispute or disbelieve in parts of it are far astray from the truth.

Verse 177

لَيْسَ الْبِرَّ أَنْ تُوَلُّوا وُجُوهَكُمْ قِبَلَ الْمَشْرِقِ وَالْمَغْرِبِ وَلَٰكِنَّ الْبِرَّ مَنْ آمَنَ بِاللَّهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ وَالْمَلَائِكَةِ وَالْكِتَابِ وَالنَّبِيِّينَ وَآتَى الْمَالَ عَلَىٰ حُبِّهِ ذَوِي الْقُرْبَىٰ وَالْيَتَامَىٰ وَالْمَسَاكِينَ وَابْنَ السَّبِيلِ وَالسَّائِلِينَ وَفِي الرِّقَابِ وَأَقَامَ الصَّلَاةَ وَآتَى الزَّكَاةَ وَالْمُوفُونَ بِعَهْدِهِمْ إِذَا عَاهَدُوا ۖ وَالصَّابِرِينَ فِي الْبَأْسَاءِ وَالضَّرَّاءِ وَحِينَ الْبَأْسِ ۗ أُولَٰئِكَ الَّذِينَ صَدَقُوا ۖ وَأُولَٰئِكَ هُمُ الْمُتَّقُونَ

Righteousness is not in turning your faces towards the east or the west. Rather, the righteous are those who believe in Allah, the Last Day, the angels, the Books, and the prophets; who give charity out of their cherished wealth to relatives, orphans, the poor, ˹needy˺ travellers, beggars, and for freeing captives; who establish prayer, pay alms-tax, and keep the pledges they make; and who are patient in times of suffering, adversity, and in ˹the heat of˺ battle. It is they who are true ˹in faith˺, and it is they who are mindful ˹of Allah˺.

Righteousness in the sight of Allah - the Most High - is not in turning one's face in prayer toward the east or the west, unless it is according to the command and law of Allah. Rather, true righteousness lies in the faith of one who believes in Allah, affirming Him as the sole deity with no partner, and believes in the Day of Resurrection and Judgment, and in all the angels, and in all the revealed books, and in all the prophets without distinction, and gives wealth – despite his love for it – to relatives, and needy orphans whose fathers died before reaching puberty, and the poor who are burdened by poverty, and needy travelers who are far from their families and wealth, and the beggars who are forced to beg due to their dire need, and spends in freeing slaves and captives, and establishes prayer, and pays the obligatory Zakat, and those who fulfill their covenants, and those who are patient in times of poverty, sickness, and during intense fighting. Those who are described with these attributes are the ones who are truthful in their faith, and those are the ones who have feared the punishment of Allah and avoided His disobedience.

True righteousness is not merely about rituals; it's about faith in Allah, the Last Day, angels, scriptures, and prophets. It involves giving to the needy, performing prayers, paying charity, keeping promises, and being patient in hardship. These are the attributes of the truthful and God-conscious believers.

Verse 178

يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا كُتِبَ عَلَيْكُمُ الْقِصَاصُ فِي الْقَتْلَى ۖ الْحُرُّ بِالْحُرِّ وَالْعَبْدُ بِالْعَبْدِ وَالْأُنْثَىٰ بِالْأُنْثَىٰ ۚ فَمَنْ عُفِيَ لَهُ مِنْ أَخِيهِ شَيْءٌ فَاتِّبَاعٌ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ وَأَدَاءٌ إِلَيْهِ بِإِحْسَانٍ ۗ ذَٰلِكَ تَخْفِيفٌ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ وَرَحْمَةٌ ۗ فَمَنِ اعْتَدَىٰ بَعْدَ ذَٰلِكَ فَلَهُ عَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌ

O believers! ˹The law of˺ retaliation is set for you in cases of murder—a free man for a free man, a slave for a slave, and a female for a female. But if the offender is pardoned by the victim’s guardian, then blood-money should be decided fairly and payment should be made courteously. This is a concession and a mercy from your Lord. But whoever transgresses after that will suffer a painful punishment.

O you who have believed in Allah and His Messenger and acted according to His law, Allah has prescribed for you legal retribution for the intentional killing: the killer is to be killed, under the condition of equality and likeness: a free person is killed for a free person, a slave for a slave, and a female for a female. But whoever is forgiven by the heir of the murdered person by foregoing retaliation and accepting the blood money – which is a specific amount of money that the offender pays in exchange for being forgiven – then both parties must adhere to good conduct; the heir should demand the blood money without violence, and the killer should pay him his due with kindness, without delay or reduction. Such forgiveness with accepting blood money is a relief and mercy from your Lord for you, due to the ease and benefit it provides. But whoever kills the killer after forgiveness and receiving the blood money, then he will have a painful punishment, either by being killed in retaliation in this world, or in the Fire in the Hereafter.

This verse outlines the law of retaliation in cases of murder, where a life is taken for a life. However, it also allows for forgiveness and the acceptance of blood money. This is presented as a mercy from Allah, but transgressing these limits incurs severe punishment.

Verse 179

وَلَكُمْ فِي الْقِصَاصِ حَيَاةٌ يَا أُولِي الْأَلْبَابِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَتَّقُونَ

There is ˹security of˺ life for you in ˹the law of˺ retaliation, O people of reason, so that you may become mindful ˹of Allah˺.

And there is life for you in the law of retribution and its implementation - O people of sound intellect - in the hope of fearing Allah and being conscious of Him by obeying Him always.

The law of retaliation is meant to provide security and preserve life. It serves as a deterrent and a means for the community to remain mindful of Allah and act justly.

Verse 180

كُتِبَ عَلَيْكُمْ إِذَا حَضَرَ أَحَدَكُمُ الْمَوْتُ إِنْ تَرَكَ خَيْرًا الْوَصِيَّةُ لِلْوَالِدَيْنِ وَالْأَقْرَبِينَ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ ۖ حَقًّا عَلَى الْمُتَّقِينَ

It is prescribed that when death approaches any of you—if they leave something of value—a will should be made in favour of parents and immediate family with fairness. ˹This is˺ an obligation on those who are mindful ˹of Allah˺.

Allah has ordained for you, when death approaches one of you and he leaves behind wealth, to make a will for his parents and close relatives, observing justice; not leaving the poor and bequeathing to the rich, and not exceeding one third of the estate. And that is a fixed right to be acted upon by the people of piety who fear Allah. And this was before the revelation of the verses of inheritance, in which Allah specified the share of each heir.

When death approaches, a person is obligated to make a fair will for their parents and close relatives if they possess wealth. This is a duty for those who are conscious of Allah, meant to ensure fairness and avoid disputes.

Verse 181

فَمَنْ بَدَّلَهُ بَعْدَمَا سَمِعَهُ فَإِنَّمَا إِثْمُهُ عَلَى الَّذِينَ يُبَدِّلُونَهُ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ سَمِيعٌ عَلِيمٌ

But whoever changes the will after hearing it, the blame will only be on those who made the change. Indeed, Allah is All-Hearing, All-Knowing.

Then whoever changes the will of the deceased after hearing it from him before his death, then the sin is only upon those who change and alter it. Indeed, Allah is All-Hearing of your wills and statements, All-Knowing of what your hearts conceal of inclination to truth and justice or injustice and unfairness, and He will recompense you for that.

If someone changes the will after it has been made, the responsibility for that wrongdoing falls on them alone. Allah is aware of all actions and intentions and will hold them to account.

Verse 182

فَمَنْ خَافَ مِنْ مُوصٍ جَنَفًا أَوْ إِثْمًا فَأَصْلَحَ بَيْنَهُمْ فَلَا إِثْمَ عَلَيْهِ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ

Whoever suspects an error or an injustice in the will and brings about a ˹fair˺ settlement among the parties will not be sinful. Surely Allah is All-Forgiving, Most Merciful.

So, whoever knows from a testator an inclination to injustice in his will, by way of error or intent, and advises the testator at the time of the will with what is more just, and if he does not achieve that, then he reconciles between the parties by changing the will to be in accordance with the Sharia, then there is no sin upon him in this reconciliation. Indeed, Allah is Forgiving to His servants, Merciful to them.

This verse addresses the situation where someone suspects injustice in a will. It permits and encourages reconciliation to ensure fairness. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful, thus allowing for adjustment of the will if errors or injustice are suspected.

Verse 183

يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا كُتِبَ عَلَيْكُمُ الصِّيَامُ كَمَا كُتِبَ عَلَى الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَتَّقُونَ

O believers! Fasting is prescribed for you—as it was for those before you—so perhaps you will become mindful ˹of Allah˺.

O you who have believed in Allah and His Messenger and acted according to His law, Allah has prescribed for you fasting as He prescribed it for the nations before you, so that you may fear your Lord, and make between you and disobedience a protection by obeying Him and worshipping Him alone.

Fasting is prescribed for believers, similar to previous nations, as a means to attain mindfulness of Allah. This verse highlights that fasting is a form of worship intended to increase piety.

Verse 184

أَيَّامًا مَعْدُودَاتٍ ۚ فَمَنْ كَانَ مِنْكُمْ مَرِيضًا أَوْ عَلَىٰ سَفَرٍ فَعِدَّةٌ مِنْ أَيَّامٍ أُخَرَ ۚ وَعَلَى الَّذِينَ يُطِيقُونَهُ فِدْيَةٌ طَعَامُ مِسْكِينٍ ۖ فَمَنْ تَطَوَّعَ خَيْرًا فَهُوَ خَيْرٌ لَهُ ۚ وَأَنْ تَصُومُوا خَيْرٌ لَكُمْ ۖ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ تَعْلَمُونَ

˹Fast a˺ prescribed number of days. But whoever of you is ill or on a journey, then ˹let them fast˺ an equal number of days ˹after Ramaḍân˺. For those who can only fast with extreme difficulty, compensation can be made by feeding a needy person ˹for every day not fasted˺. But whoever volunteers to give more, it is better for them. And to fast is better for you, if only you knew.

Allah has prescribed for you fasting for a specified number of days, which are the days of the month of Ramadan. So whoever among you is ill and fasting is difficult for him, or is on a journey, then he may break his fast, and he must fast a number of other days equal to the ones he broke. And upon those who can barely endure fasting and it is extremely difficult for them, like an old man and a sick person who has no hope of recovery, there is a ransom for every day they break, which is the feeding of a poor person. Whoever increases in the amount of ransom as a voluntary act, then it is better for him, and your fasting is better for you - despite bearing the hardship - than giving the ransom, if you know the great virtue of fasting with Allah.

Fasting is for a specific number of days. If someone is ill or traveling, they can make up those days later. Those who find fasting extremely difficult can compensate by feeding a poor person. However, fasting is still better if one can do it.

Verse 185

شَهْرُ رَمَضَانَ الَّذِي أُنْزِلَ فِيهِ الْقُرْآنُ هُدًى لِلنَّاسِ وَبَيِّنَاتٍ مِنَ الْهُدَىٰ وَالْفُرْقَانِ ۚ فَمَنْ شَهِدَ مِنْكُمُ الشَّهْرَ فَلْيَصُمْهُ ۖ وَمَنْ كَانَ مَرِيضًا أَوْ عَلَىٰ سَفَرٍ فَعِدَّةٌ مِنْ أَيَّامٍ أُخَرَ ۗ يُرِيدُ اللَّهُ بِكُمُ الْيُسْرَ وَلَا يُرِيدُ بِكُمُ الْعُسْرَ وَلِتُكْمِلُوا الْعِدَّةَ وَلِتُكَبِّرُوا اللَّهَ عَلَىٰ مَا هَدَاكُمْ وَلَعَلَّكُمْ تَشْكُرُونَ

Ramaḍân is the month in which the Quran was revealed as a guide for humanity with clear proofs of guidance and the standard ˹to distinguish between right and wrong˺. So whoever is present this month, let them fast. But whoever is ill or on a journey, then ˹let them fast˺ an equal number of days ˹after Ramaḍân˺. Allah intends ease for you, not hardship, so that you may complete the prescribed period and proclaim the greatness of Allah for guiding you, and perhaps you will be grateful.

The month of Ramadan in which Allah began to send down the Quran on the Night of Decree, as a guidance for people to the truth, in it are clear proofs of Allah’s guidance, and of the distinction between truth and falsehood. So whoever among you is present in the month and is healthy and not traveling, then he should fast its day. And the sick and the traveler are allowed to break the fast, then they make up those days. Allah desires for you ease in His laws, and He does not desire for you difficulty, and so that you may complete the number of fasting days, a month, and so that you may conclude the fasting by magnifying Allah on the day of Eid al-Fitr, and so that you may glorify Him for His guidance, and so that you may thank Him for what He has bestowed upon you of guidance, success, and ease.

The Quran was revealed in the month of Ramadan, a guide for humanity. Those who are present during this month must fast, while those who are sick or traveling can make up for it later. Allah intends ease, so believers should complete the fast, magnify Allah, and be grateful.

Verse 186

وَإِذَا سَأَلَكَ عِبَادِي عَنِّي فَإِنِّي قَرِيبٌ ۖ أُجِيبُ دَعْوَةَ الدَّاعِ إِذَا دَعَانِ ۖ فَلْيَسْتَجِيبُوا لِي وَلْيُؤْمِنُوا بِي لَعَلَّهُمْ يَرْشُدُونَ

When My servants ask you ˹O Prophet˺ about Me: I am truly near. I respond to one’s prayer when they call upon Me. So let them respond ˹with obedience˺ to Me and believe in Me, perhaps they will be guided ˹to the Right Way˺.

And when My servants ask you, [O Muhammad], concerning Me - indeed I am near. I respond to the invocation of the supplicant when he calls upon Me. So let them obey Me and believe in Me that they may be [rightly] guided to the benefits of their religion and their world. And in this verse is an affirmation from Him, Glory be to Him, about His nearness to His servants, the nearness that befits His Majesty.

When believers ask about Allah, He is near. He responds to prayers when called upon. Thus, believers should obey and have faith so they may be guided correctly. This verse affirms Allah's nearness to His servants.

Verse 187

أُحِلَّ لَكُمْ لَيْلَةَ الصِّيَامِ الرَّفَثُ إِلَىٰ نِسَائِكُمْ ۚ هُنَّ لِبَاسٌ لَكُمْ وَأَنْتُمْ لِبَاسٌ لَهُنَّ ۗ عَلِمَ اللَّهُ أَنَّكُمْ كُنْتُمْ تَخْتَانُونَ أَنْفُسَكُمْ فَتَابَ عَلَيْكُمْ وَعَفَا عَنْكُمْ ۖ فَالْآنَ بَاشِرُوهُنَّ وَابْتَغُوا مَا كَتَبَ اللَّهُ لَكُمْ ۚ وَكُلُوا وَاشْرَبُوا حَتَّىٰ يَتَبَيَّنَ لَكُمُ الْخَيْطُ الْأَبْيَضُ مِنَ الْخَيْطِ الْأَسْوَدِ مِنَ الْفَجْرِ ۖ ثُمَّ أَتِمُّوا الصِّيَامَ إِلَى اللَّيْلِ ۚ وَلَا تُبَاشِرُوهُنَّ وَأَنْتُمْ عَاكِفُونَ فِي الْمَسَاجِدِ ۗ تِلْكَ حُدُودُ اللَّهِ فَلَا تَقْرَبُوهَا ۗ كَذَٰلِكَ يُبَيِّنُ اللَّهُ آيَاتِهِ لِلنَّاسِ لَعَلَّهُمْ يَتَّقُونَ

It has been made permissible for you to be intimate with your wives during the nights preceding the fast. Your spouses are a garment for you as you are for them. Allah knows that you were deceiving yourselves. So He has accepted your repentance and pardoned you. So now you may be intimate with them and seek what Allah has prescribed for you. ˹You may˺ eat and drink until you see the light of dawn breaking the darkness of night, then complete the fast until nightfall. Do not be intimate with your spouses while you are meditating in the mosques. These are the limits set by Allah, so do not exceed them. This is how Allah makes His revelations clear to people, so they may become mindful ˹of Him˺.

Allah has permitted you to have relations with your wives during the nights of Ramadan. They are a covering and protection for you, and you are a covering and protection for them. Allah knows that you used to betray yourselves by violating what Allah had forbidden you from having relations with women after Isha during the nights of fasting - and that was in the beginning of Islam - so Allah has turned to you in forgiveness and made the matter easier for you. So now, have relations with them and seek what Allah has destined for you of children. And eat and drink until the white thread of dawn becomes distinct from the black thread of night at the appearance of true dawn. Then complete the fast until night by abstaining from the things that break it until sunset. And do not have relations with your wives or do anything that leads to relations if you are observing I'tikaf in the mosques, because this invalidates the I'tikaf (which is staying in the mosque for a specified period with the intention of drawing closer to Allah). These are the ordinances that Allah has prescribed for you, which are His limits distinguishing between the lawful and the unlawful, so do not approach them lest you fall into the unlawful. With such clear explanations, Allah makes clear His verses and ordinances to people so that they may fear Him.

This verse permits intimacy with spouses during the nights of Ramadan. It also clarifies the rules of fasting, allowing eating and drinking until dawn and abstaining from them until sunset. It prohibits intimacy during I'tikaf (seclusion) in mosques and emphasizes following Allah's limits to be mindful of Him.

Verse 188

وَلَا تَأْكُلُوا أَمْوَالَكُمْ بَيْنَكُمْ بِالْبَاطِلِ وَتُدْلُوا بِهَا إِلَى الْحُكَّامِ لِتَأْكُلُوا فَرِيقًا مِنْ أَمْوَالِ النَّاسِ بِالْإِثْمِ وَأَنْتُمْ تَعْلَمُونَ

Do not consume one another’s wealth unjustly, nor deliberately bribe authorities in order to devour a portion of others’ property, knowing that it is a sin.

And do not consume one another’s wealth unjustly, such as by false oaths, usurpation, theft, bribery, usury, and the like. And do not present false arguments to the rulers so that you may consume the wealth of a group of people unjustly, while you know it is forbidden for you.

This verse prohibits consuming others' wealth unjustly through means like false oaths, theft, bribery, or usury. It also forbids using influence or power to unlawfully acquire wealth, emphasizing that such actions are sinful and known to be so.

Verse 189

يَسْأَلُونَكَ عَنِ الْأَهِلَّةِ ۖ قُلْ هِيَ مَوَاقِيتُ لِلنَّاسِ وَالْحَجِّ ۗ وَلَيْسَ الْبِرُّ بِأَنْ تَأْتُوا الْبُيُوتَ مِنْ ظُهُورِهَا وَلَٰكِنَّ الْبِرَّ مَنِ اتَّقَىٰ ۗ وَأْتُوا الْبُيُوتَ مِنْ أَبْوَابِهَا ۚ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ لَعَلَّكُمْ تُفْلِحُونَ

They ask you ˹O Prophet˺ about the phases of the moon. Say, “They are a means for people to determine time and pilgrimage.” Righteousness is not in entering your houses from the back doors. Rather, righteousness is to be mindful ˹of Allah˺. So enter your homes through their ˹proper˺ doors, and be mindful of Allah so you may be successful.

They ask you, [O Prophet], about the new moons. Say, "They are measurements of time for the people and for the Hajj." And it is not righteousness to enter houses from the back, as you were accustomed to in the pre-Islamic era and the beginning of Islam when you entered houses from their back when you were in Ihram for Hajj or Umrah, thinking that to be a means to draw closer to Allah, but righteousness is [in] the one who fears Allah and avoids sins. And enter houses from their doors when you are in Ihram for Hajj or Umrah, and fear Allah in all your affairs, so that you may be successful in all that you love of the good of this world and the Hereafter.

The verse explains that the phases of the moon are for determining time, including the time for pilgrimage. It clarifies that true righteousness lies in fearing Allah and avoiding sin, not in ritualistic practices like entering homes from the back. It encourages following proper ways and being mindful of Allah for success.

Verse 190

وَقَاتِلُوا فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ الَّذِينَ يُقَاتِلُونَكُمْ وَلَا تَعْتَدُوا ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يُحِبُّ الْمُعْتَدِينَ

Fight in the cause of Allah ˹only˺ against those who wage war against you, but do not exceed the limits. Surely Allah does not like transgressors.

Fight in the cause of Allah those who fight you, but do not transgress limits. Indeed, Allah does not like transgressors, who make lawful what Allah and His Messenger have forbidden.

This verse commands fighting against those who wage war, but with limits. It states that Allah does not like those who transgress, emphasizing the importance of observing boundaries and rules in conflict.

Verse 191

وَاقْتُلُوهُمْ حَيْثُ ثَقِفْتُمُوهُمْ وَأَخْرِجُوهُمْ مِنْ حَيْثُ أَخْرَجُوكُمْ ۚ وَالْفِتْنَةُ أَشَدُّ مِنَ الْقَتْلِ ۚ وَلَا تُقَاتِلُوهُمْ عِنْدَ الْمَسْجِدِ الْحَرَامِ حَتَّىٰ يُقَاتِلُوكُمْ فِيهِ ۖ فَإِنْ قَاتَلُوكُمْ فَاقْتُلُوهُمْ ۗ كَذَٰلِكَ جَزَاءُ الْكَافِرِينَ

Kill them wherever you come upon them and drive them out of the places from which they have driven you out. For persecution is far worse than killing. And do not fight them at the Sacred Mosque unless they attack you there. If they do so, then fight them—that is the reward of the disbelievers.

And kill them wherever you find them, and expel them from the place from which they expelled you, which is "Mecca." And persecution - which is disbelief, polytheism, and turning away from Islam - is worse than killing them. And do not begin fighting them at the Sacred Mosque, in reverence for its sanctity, until they begin fighting you there. But if they fight you at the Sacred Mosque, then kill them there. Such is the recompense for the disbelievers.

This verse permits fighting back against those who attack, and to expel them from places they drove Muslims from. It emphasizes that persecution is worse than fighting, and fighting is allowed in the Sacred Mosque if initiated by the enemy.

Verse 192

فَإِنِ انْتَهَوْا فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ

But if they cease, then surely Allah is All-Forgiving, Most Merciful.

But if they cease from their disbelief and fighting you at the Sacred Mosque, and enter into faith, then Allah is Forgiving to His servants, Merciful to them.

If the enemies cease their aggression and fighting, Allah is forgiving and merciful. This highlights that the purpose of fighting is to stop persecution and not for revenge.

Verse 193

وَقَاتِلُوهُمْ حَتَّىٰ لَا تَكُونَ فِتْنَةٌ وَيَكُونَ الدِّينُ لِلَّهِ ۖ فَإِنِ انْتَهَوْا فَلَا عُدْوَانَ إِلَّا عَلَى الظَّالِمِينَ

Fight against them ˹if they persecute you˺ until there is no more persecution, and ˹your˺ devotion will be to Allah ˹alone˺. If they stop ˹persecuting you˺, let there be no hostility except against the aggressors.

And continue - O believers - fighting the polytheists who are aggressing, until there is no more persecution of Muslims from their religion and no polytheism with Allah, and the religion remains for Allah alone, purely, with none else worshipped beside Him. But if they cease from disbelief and fighting, then cease from fighting them; for punishment is only for those who persist in their disbelief and aggression.

Fight against those who persecute until religious freedom is established and worship is for Allah alone. If they stop fighting, there should be no aggression except against the aggressors. This establishes the principle of fighting only when necessary.

Verse 194

الشَّهْرُ الْحَرَامُ بِالشَّهْرِ الْحَرَامِ وَالْحُرُمَاتُ قِصَاصٌ ۚ فَمَنِ اعْتَدَىٰ عَلَيْكُمْ فَاعْتَدُوا عَلَيْهِ بِمِثْلِ مَا اعْتَدَىٰ عَلَيْكُمْ ۚ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ وَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ مَعَ الْمُتَّقِينَ

˹There will be retaliation in˺ a sacred month for ˹an offence in˺ a sacred month, and all violations will bring about retaliation. So, if anyone attacks you, retaliate in the same manner. ˹But˺ be mindful of Allah, and know that Allah is with those mindful ˹of Him˺.

Your fighting, O believers, against the polytheists in the month in which Allah has forbidden fighting is a recompense for their fighting you in the Sacred Month. And whoever transgresses against what Allah has forbidden of place and time will be punished with the like of his action, and of the same kind of deed. So whoever has transgressed against you by fighting or other means, then inflict upon him a similar punishment to his crime, and there is no blame upon you for that; because they are the ones who began the aggression, and fear Allah and do not exceed the likeness in punishment, and know that Allah is with those who fear Him and obey Him by performing His obligations and avoiding His prohibitions.

Fighting in a sacred month is allowed if the enemy attacks first. Retaliation should be proportional to the transgression. Always be mindful of Allah and that He is with those who fear Him.

Verse 195

وَأَنْفِقُوا فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ وَلَا تُلْقُوا بِأَيْدِيكُمْ إِلَى التَّهْلُكَةِ ۛ وَأَحْسِنُوا ۛ إِنَّ اللَّهَ يُحِبُّ الْمُحْسِنِينَ

Spend in the cause of Allah and do not let your own hands throw you into destruction ˹by withholding˺. And do good, for Allah certainly loves the good-doers.

And continue - O believers - in spending wealth to support the religion of Allah, and striving in His cause, and do not cast yourselves into destruction by abandoning the striving in the cause of Allah and not spending in it, and do good in spending and obedience, and make all your actions purely for the sake of Allah. Indeed, Allah loves the people of sincerity and excellence.

Spend in the cause of Allah and do not cause your own destruction by withholding. Do good, for Allah loves those who do good. This encourages charitable giving and righteous actions.

Verse 196

وَأَتِمُّوا الْحَجَّ وَالْعُمْرَةَ لِلَّهِ ۚ فَإِنْ أُحْصِرْتُمْ فَمَا اسْتَيْسَرَ مِنَ الْهَدْيِ ۖ وَلَا تَحْلِقُوا رُءُوسَكُمْ حَتَّىٰ يَبْلُغَ الْهَدْيُ مَحِلَّهُ ۚ فَمَنْ كَانَ مِنْكُمْ مَرِيضًا أَوْ بِهِ أَذًى مِنْ رَأْسِهِ فَفِدْيَةٌ مِنْ صِيَامٍ أَوْ صَدَقَةٍ أَوْ نُسُكٍ ۚ فَإِذَا أَمِنْتُمْ فَمَنْ تَمَتَّعَ بِالْعُمْرَةِ إِلَى الْحَجِّ فَمَا اسْتَيْسَرَ مِنَ الْهَدْيِ ۚ فَمَنْ لَمْ يَجِدْ فَصِيَامُ ثَلَاثَةِ أَيَّامٍ فِي الْحَجِّ وَسَبْعَةٍ إِذَا رَجَعْتُمْ ۗ تِلْكَ عَشَرَةٌ كَامِلَةٌ ۗ ذَٰلِكَ لِمَنْ لَمْ يَكُنْ أَهْلُهُ حَاضِرِي الْمَسْجِدِ الْحَرَامِ ۚ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ وَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ شَدِيدُ الْعِقَابِ

Complete the pilgrimage and minor pilgrimage for Allah. But if prevented ˹from proceeding˺, then ˹offer˺ whatever sacrificial animals you can afford. And do not shave your heads until the sacrificial animal reaches its destination. But if any of you is ill or has a scalp ailment ˹requiring shaving˺, then compensate either by fasting, charity, or a sacrificial offering. In times of peace, you may combine the pilgrimage and minor pilgrimage then make the sacrificial offering you can afford. Whoever cannot afford that ˹offering˺, let them fast three days during pilgrimage and seven after returning ˹home˺—completing ten. These offerings are for those who do not live near the Sacred House. And be mindful of Allah, and know that Allah is severe in punishment.

And complete the Hajj and Umrah for the sake of Allah. But if you are prevented from going to complete them after entering into their sacred state by a hindrance such as an enemy or illness, then it is obligatory upon you to slaughter what is available for you of camels, cows, or sheep as an offering to Allah; in order to exit your sacred state by shaving or shortening the hair of the head. And do not shave your heads if you are prevented until the one who is prevented sacrifices his offering in the place where he is prevented, then releases from his sacred state, as the Prophet (peace be upon him) sacrificed in "Al-Hudaybiyah" then shaved his head, and the one who is not prevented does not sacrifice the offering except in the Sanctuary, which is its place on the day of Eid, the tenth day and what follows of the days of Tashreeq. And whoever among you is sick, or has an ailment of the head which requires him to shave - while he is in a state of Ihram (sacred state) - may shave, and he must then offer expiation: either by fasting three days, or by feeding six poor people, giving each poor person half a Sa' of food, or by sacrificing a sheep for the poor of the Sanctuary. So if you are in safety and health, then whoever enjoys Umrah until Hajj, and that is by making lawful what was forbidden to him because of the Ihram after the completion of his Umrah, must sacrifice what is available of an offering; but if he cannot find an offering to sacrifice, then he must fast three days in the months of Hajj and seven when you have finished the actions of the Hajj and returned to your families, that is ten full days, and they must be fasted. That offering and what is ordained of fasting for it, is for one whose family is not among the residents of the sacred territory. And fear Allah, and maintain the fulfillment of His commands and the avoidance of His prohibitions, and know that Allah is severe in punishment to the one who opposes His commands and commits what He has forbidden.

Complete the pilgrimage (Hajj) and minor pilgrimage (Umrah) for Allah's sake. If prevented, offer a sacrifice. Those who cannot make a sacrifice must fast. This verse explains the rules and requirements for these acts of worship.

Verse 197

الْحَجُّ أَشْهُرٌ مَعْلُومَاتٌ ۚ فَمَنْ فَرَضَ فِيهِنَّ الْحَجَّ فَلَا رَفَثَ وَلَا فُسُوقَ وَلَا جِدَالَ فِي الْحَجِّ ۗ وَمَا تَفْعَلُوا مِنْ خَيْرٍ يَعْلَمْهُ اللَّهُ ۗ وَتَزَوَّدُوا فَإِنَّ خَيْرَ الزَّادِ التَّقْوَىٰ ۚ وَاتَّقُونِ يَا أُولِي الْأَلْبَابِ

˹Commitment to˺ pilgrimage is made in appointed months. Whoever commits to ˹performing˺ pilgrimage, let them stay away from intimate relations, foul language, and arguments during pilgrimage. Whatever good you do, Allah ˹fully˺ knows of it. Take ˹necessary˺ provisions ˹for the journey˺—surely the best provision is righteousness. And be mindful of Me, O people of reason!

The time of Hajj is during well-known months, which are: Shawwal, Dhul-Qadah, and ten days of Dhul-Hijjah. So whoever makes Hajj obligatory upon himself in them by entering into Ihram, then intercourse and its verbal and physical preliminaries are forbidden for him, and it is forbidden for him to disobey Allah the Almighty by committing sins, and arguing during Hajj that leads to anger and hatred. And whatever good you do, Allah knows it, and will reward each one for his deeds. And take for yourselves provision of food and drink for the Hajj journey, and provision of righteous deeds for the Hereafter, for indeed the best provision is the fear of Allah, and fear Me, O people of sound intellect.

Pilgrimage (Hajj) is to be performed during specific months. During this time, pilgrims must abstain from intimacy, bad language, and arguments. Allah is aware of all good deeds, and the best provision is righteousness. The verse also urges people of reason to be mindful of God.

Verse 198

لَيْسَ عَلَيْكُمْ جُنَاحٌ أَنْ تَبْتَغُوا فَضْلًا مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ ۚ فَإِذَا أَفَضْتُمْ مِنْ عَرَفَاتٍ فَاذْكُرُوا اللَّهَ عِنْدَ الْمَشْعَرِ الْحَرَامِ ۖ وَاذْكُرُوهُ كَمَا هَدَاكُمْ وَإِنْ كُنْتُمْ مِنْ قَبْلِهِ لَمِنَ الضَّالِّينَ

There is no blame on you for seeking the bounty of your Lord ˹during this journey˺. When you return from ’Arafât, praise Allah near the sacred place and praise Him for having guided you, for surely before this ˹guidance˺ you were astray.

There is no blame on you if you seek bounty from your Lord by profiting from trade during the days of Hajj. Then when you depart after sunset, returning from 'Arafat' - which is the place where the pilgrims stand on the ninth day of Dhul-Hijjah - then remember Allah by glorifying Him, reciting Talbiyah, and supplication at the Sacred Monument -'Muzdalifah'-, and remember Allah in the correct manner that He has guided you to, and indeed you were before this guidance in error, not knowing the truth with it.

It is permissible to seek Allah's bounty through trade during Hajj. Upon leaving Arafat, remember Allah at the sacred place (Muzdalifah) and thank Him for guidance, as humanity was once astray.

Verse 199

ثُمَّ أَفِيضُوا مِنْ حَيْثُ أَفَاضَ النَّاسُ وَاسْتَغْفِرُوا اللَّهَ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ

Then go forth with the rest of the pilgrims. And seek Allah’s forgiveness. Surely Allah is All-Forgiving, Most Merciful.

And let your departure from 'Arafat', from which Ibrahim, peace be upon him, departed, be in opposition to those among the people of ignorance who do not stand there, and ask Allah to forgive you your sins. Indeed, Allah is Forgiving to His repentant servants, Merciful to them.

Depart from Arafat in a manner that differs from those who don't understand its significance and seek forgiveness from Allah. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful to those who repent.

Verse 200

فَإِذَا قَضَيْتُمْ مَنَاسِكَكُمْ فَاذْكُرُوا اللَّهَ كَذِكْرِكُمْ آبَاءَكُمْ أَوْ أَشَدَّ ذِكْرًا ۗ فَمِنَ النَّاسِ مَنْ يَقُولُ رَبَّنَا آتِنَا فِي الدُّنْيَا وَمَا لَهُ فِي الْآخِرَةِ مِنْ خَلَاقٍ

When you have fulfilled your sacred rites, praise Allah as you used to praise your forefathers ˹before Islam˺, or even more passionately. There are some who say, “Our Lord! Grant us ˹Your bounties˺ in this world,” but they will have no share in the Hereafter.

So when you have completed your acts of worship, and finished the rites of Hajj, then remember Allah frequently and praise Him, like your remembering the glories of your fathers, or even greater than that. For among people is a group whose concern is only the world, so he prays, saying, 'Our Lord, grant us [good] in this world,' [such as] health, wealth, and children, and these people will have no share in the Hereafter, due to their disinclination towards it and limiting their focus to the world.

After completing Hajj rites, remember Allah more fervently than one might remember their ancestors. Some people focus only on worldly gains and will have no share in the Hereafter.

Verse 201

وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ يَقُولُ رَبَّنَا آتِنَا فِي الدُّنْيَا حَسَنَةً وَفِي الْآخِرَةِ حَسَنَةً وَقِنَا عَذَابَ النَّارِ

Yet there are others who say, “Our Lord! Grant us the good of this world and the Hereafter, and protect us from the torment of the Fire.”

And among people is a believing group who says in their prayer: 'Our Lord, grant us in this world well-being, provision, beneficial knowledge, and righteous deeds, and other matters of religion and the world, and in the Hereafter, Paradise, and avert from us the punishment of the Fire.' And this supplication is among the most comprehensive of supplications, and for this reason, it was the most frequent supplication of the Prophet, may Allah bless him and grant him peace, as it is established in the two Sahihs.

Others pray for both worldly good and the good of the Hereafter, also seeking protection from Hellfire. This comprehensive supplication is favored by the Prophet Muhammad (peace be upon him).

Verse 202

أُولَٰئِكَ لَهُمْ نَصِيبٌ مِمَّا كَسَبُوا ۚ وَاللَّهُ سَرِيعُ الْحِسَابِ

It is they who will receive a ˹heavenly˺ reward for the good they have done. Surely Allah is swift in reckoning.

Those who supplicate with this supplication will have a great reward because of what they have earned from righteous deeds. And Allah is swift in account, reckoning the deeds of His servants and recompensing them for them.

Those who make the supplication for both worlds will receive a great reward for their righteous deeds, and Allah is swift in reckoning the deeds of all.

Verse 203

وَاذْكُرُوا اللَّهَ فِي أَيَّامٍ مَعْدُودَاتٍ ۚ فَمَنْ تَعَجَّلَ فِي يَوْمَيْنِ فَلَا إِثْمَ عَلَيْهِ وَمَنْ تَأَخَّرَ فَلَا إِثْمَ عَلَيْهِ ۚ لِمَنِ اتَّقَىٰ ۗ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ وَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّكُمْ إِلَيْهِ تُحْشَرُونَ

And remember Allah during ˹these˺ appointed days. Whoever departs swiftly on the second day is not sinful, neither are those who stay behind ˹till the third—seeking additional reward˺, so long as they are mindful ˹of their Lord˺. And be mindful of Allah, and know that to Him you will ˹all˺ be gathered.

And remember Allah by glorifying and magnifying Him during the appointed days, which are the days of Tashreeq: the eleventh, twelfth, and thirteenth of the month of Dhul-Hijjah. Whoever hastens and leaves "Mina" before the sunset of the twelfth day after stoning the Jamarat, there is no sin upon him. And whoever delays by staying in "Mina" until he stones the Jamarat on the thirteenth day, there is no sin upon him, for whoever fears Allah in his pilgrimage. And delaying is better; because it is an increase in worship and an emulation of the Prophet's actions, peace be upon him. And fear Allah - O Muslims - and observe Him in all your deeds, and know that to Him alone you will be gathered after your death for reckoning and recompense.

This verse instructs believers to remember Allah during the days of Tashreeq (11th-13th of Dhul-Hijjah). It also permits those on pilgrimage to leave Mina early or stay longer, emphasizing that piety and awareness of Allah are most important. All will ultimately be gathered before Him.

Verse 204

وَمِنَ النَّاسِ مَنْ يُعْجِبُكَ قَوْلُهُ فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا وَيُشْهِدُ اللَّهَ عَلَىٰ مَا فِي قَلْبِهِ وَهُوَ أَلَدُّ الْخِصَامِ

There are some ˹hypocrites˺ who impress you with their views regarding worldly affairs and openly call upon Allah to witness what is in their hearts, yet they are your worst adversaries.

And some people from among the hypocrites, their speech pleases you - O Messenger - eloquent speech, by which they seek a portion of the worldly benefits, not the Hereafter, and they swear, calling Allah as a witness to what is in their hearts of love for Islam, and in this is the ultimate audacity towards Allah, and they are extremely hostile and antagonistic to Islam and Muslims.

This verse speaks of hypocrites who use eloquent speech to impress, outwardly claiming love for Islam while harboring hostility towards it and its followers. They deceive with their words, and Allah knows their true intentions.

Verse 205

وَإِذَا تَوَلَّىٰ سَعَىٰ فِي الْأَرْضِ لِيُفْسِدَ فِيهَا وَيُهْلِكَ الْحَرْثَ وَالنَّسْلَ ۗ وَاللَّهُ لَا يُحِبُّ الْفَسَادَ

And when they leave ˹you˺, they strive throughout the land to spread mischief in it and destroy crops and cattle. Allah does not like mischief.

And when he leaves your presence, O Messenger, he strives and goes about in the land to cause corruption therein, and to destroy the crops of the people, and to kill their livestock. And Allah does not love corruption.

Hypocrites are described as those who, when they leave the company of believers, actively engage in spreading corruption, destroying crops, and harming livestock. Allah does not approve of such mischief.

Verse 206

وَإِذَا قِيلَ لَهُ اتَّقِ اللَّهَ أَخَذَتْهُ الْعِزَّةُ بِالْإِثْمِ ۚ فَحَسْبُهُ جَهَنَّمُ ۚ وَلَبِئْسَ الْمِهَادُ

When it is said to them, “Fear Allah,” pride carries them off to sin. Hell will be their proper place. What an evil place to rest!

And if that corrupt hypocrite is advised, and it is said to him: Fear Allah and beware of His punishment, and refrain from corruption in the land, he does not accept the advice. Rather, pride and the zealotry of ignorance drive him to more sins. So, Hell is sufficient for him, and what an evil resting place it is.

When hypocrites are advised to fear Allah, they become arrogant and defiant. They are warned that Hell will be their abode and a terrible place to rest.

Verse 207

وَمِنَ النَّاسِ مَنْ يَشْرِي نَفْسَهُ ابْتِغَاءَ مَرْضَاتِ اللَّهِ ۗ وَاللَّهُ رَءُوفٌ بِالْعِبَادِ

And there are those who would dedicate their lives to Allah’s pleasure. And Allah is Ever Gracious to ˹His˺ servants.

And some people sell themselves seeking Allah's pleasure, through striving in His cause, and adhering to His obedience. And Allah is Kind to His servants, having wide mercy for His believing servants in their present life and their future, and He will reward them with the best reward.

In contrast to hypocrites, there are those who dedicate their lives to seeking Allah's pleasure and striving in His cause. Allah is Kind and Gracious to such devoted servants.

Verse 208

يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا ادْخُلُوا فِي السِّلْمِ كَافَّةً وَلَا تَتَّبِعُوا خُطُوَاتِ الشَّيْطَانِ ۚ إِنَّهُ لَكُمْ عَدُوٌّ مُبِينٌ

O believers! Enter into Islam wholeheartedly and do not follow Satan’s footsteps. Surely he is your sworn enemy.

O you who have believed in Allah as your Lord, and in Muhammad as your prophet and messenger, and in Islam as your religion, enter into all the laws of Islam, acting by all its rulings, and do not leave anything out, and do not follow the ways of Satan in what he calls you to of sins. Indeed, he is for you a clear enemy, so beware of him.

Believers are urged to embrace Islam wholeheartedly and avoid following Satan's ways. He is described as a sworn enemy who leads people towards sin and deviation.

Verse 209

فَإِنْ زَلَلْتُمْ مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا جَاءَتْكُمُ الْبَيِّنَاتُ فَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ عَزِيزٌ حَكِيمٌ

If you falter after receiving the clear proofs, then know that Allah is indeed Almighty, All-Wise.

If you deviate from the path of truth, after the clear proofs have come to you from the Quran and the Sunnah, then know that Allah is Mighty in His dominion, nothing escapes Him, Wise in His command and prohibition, He puts everything in its proper place.

This verse is a warning that if believers turn away from the truth after receiving clear guidance, they should know that Allah is Almighty and Wise. His power and wisdom are absolute.

Verse 210

هَلْ يَنْظُرُونَ إِلَّا أَنْ يَأْتِيَهُمُ اللَّهُ فِي ظُلَلٍ مِنَ الْغَمَامِ وَالْمَلَائِكَةُ وَقُضِيَ الْأَمْرُ ۚ وَإِلَى اللَّهِ تُرْجَعُ الْأُمُورُ

Are they waiting for Allah ˹Himself˺ to come to them in the shade of clouds, along with the angels? ˹If He did˺, then the matter would be settled ˹at once˺. And to Allah ˹all˺ matters will be returned ˹for judgment˺.

What are these stubborn disbelievers waiting for, after the establishment of clear evidence, except that Allah Almighty comes to them in a manner befitting Him, glory be to Him, in canopies of clouds on the Day of Judgment, to decide among them with just judgment, and that the angels come, and at that time Allah Almighty will pass His judgment on them. And to Him alone do all the affairs of creation return.

The verse questions what the disbelievers are waiting for, implying they await Allah's judgment. When Allah and the angels come on the Day of Judgment, the matter will be settled. Ultimately, all matters return to Allah.

Verse 211

سَلْ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ كَمْ آتَيْنَاهُمْ مِنْ آيَةٍ بَيِّنَةٍ ۗ وَمَنْ يُبَدِّلْ نِعْمَةَ اللَّهِ مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا جَاءَتْهُ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ شَدِيدُ الْعِقَابِ

Ask the Children of Israel how many clear signs We have given them. And whoever trades Allah’s favour—after receiving it—˹for disbelief˺ should know that Allah is indeed severe in punishment.

Ask -O Messenger- the obstinate Children of Israel: How many clear signs We gave them in their books to guide them to the truth, but they disbelieved in all of them, turned away from them, and distorted them from their proper places. And whoever exchanges the blessing of Allah -which is His religion- and disbelieves in it after knowing it, and the proof has been established against him, then Allah is severe in punishment to him.

This verse questions the Children of Israel about the numerous clear signs they received, emphasizing that rejecting Allah's favor after it has been made clear is a severe offense, leading to Allah's stern punishment.

Verse 212

زُيِّنَ لِلَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا الْحَيَاةُ الدُّنْيَا وَيَسْخَرُونَ مِنَ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا ۘ وَالَّذِينَ اتَّقَوْا فَوْقَهُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ ۗ وَاللَّهُ يَرْزُقُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ بِغَيْرِ حِسَابٍ

The life of this world has been made appealing to the disbelievers, and they mock the believers. Those who are mindful ˹of Allah˺ will rank above them on the Day of Judgment. And Allah provides for whoever He wills without limit.

Beautified for those who deny the Oneness of Allah is the worldly life and its desires and pleasures, and they mock the believers. And those who fear their Lord will be above all the disbelievers on the Day of Resurrection, where Allah will admit them to the highest degrees of Paradise, and will cast the disbelievers into the lowest depths of Hellfire. And Allah provides for whom He wills of His creation without measure.

This verse contrasts the allure of worldly life for disbelievers with the elevated status of believers on the Day of Judgment. It highlights Allah's limitless provision for whom He wills.

Verse 213

كَانَ النَّاسُ أُمَّةً وَاحِدَةً فَبَعَثَ اللَّهُ النَّبِيِّينَ مُبَشِّرِينَ وَمُنْذِرِينَ وَأَنْزَلَ مَعَهُمُ الْكِتَابَ بِالْحَقِّ لِيَحْكُمَ بَيْنَ النَّاسِ فِيمَا اخْتَلَفُوا فِيهِ ۚ وَمَا اخْتَلَفَ فِيهِ إِلَّا الَّذِينَ أُوتُوهُ مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا جَاءَتْهُمُ الْبَيِّنَاتُ بَغْيًا بَيْنَهُمْ ۖ فَهَدَى اللَّهُ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لِمَا اخْتَلَفُوا فِيهِ مِنَ الْحَقِّ بِإِذْنِهِ ۗ وَاللَّهُ يَهْدِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ إِلَىٰ صِرَاطٍ مُسْتَقِيمٍ

Humanity had once been one community ˹of believers before they lost faith˺. Then Allah raised prophets as deliverers of good news and as warners, and revealed to them the Scriptures in truth to judge among people regarding their disputes. And no one disputed the Scriptures except the very people who received them after clear proofs had come to them—out of jealousy. Then Allah, by His grace, has guided the believers to the truth regarding those disputes. And Allah guides whoever He wills to the Straight Path.

Mankind was one community, agreeing on faith in Allah, then they differed in their religion, so Allah sent the prophets as callers to the religion of Allah, giving good tidings of Paradise to those who obey Allah, and warning of Hellfire those who disbelieve in Him and disobey Him, and He sent down with them the heavenly books with the truth that they contained, to judge thereby between people in what they differed about. And none differed regarding the matter of Muhammad, peace and blessings be upon him, and his book, out of injustice and envy, except those to whom Allah gave the Torah, and who knew what it contained of proofs and laws, so Allah enabled the believers by His grace to distinguish truth from falsehood, and to know what they differed about. And Allah guides whom He wills of His servants to a straight path.

Initially, humanity was united, but disagreements led Allah to send prophets with scriptures to guide them. Those who received the scriptures disputed them out of jealousy. Allah guided believers to the truth, emphasizing that guidance is ultimately from Him.

Verse 214

أَمْ حَسِبْتُمْ أَنْ تَدْخُلُوا الْجَنَّةَ وَلَمَّا يَأْتِكُمْ مَثَلُ الَّذِينَ خَلَوْا مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ ۖ مَسَّتْهُمُ الْبَأْسَاءُ وَالضَّرَّاءُ وَزُلْزِلُوا حَتَّىٰ يَقُولَ الرَّسُولُ وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا مَعَهُ مَتَىٰ نَصْرُ اللَّهِ ۗ أَلَا إِنَّ نَصْرَ اللَّهِ قَرِيبٌ

Do you think you will be admitted into Paradise without being tested like those before you? They were afflicted with suffering and adversity and were so ˹violently˺ shaken that ˹even˺ the Messenger and the believers with him cried out, “When will Allah’s help come?” Indeed, Allah’s help is ˹always˺ near.

Or do you think -O believers- that you will enter Paradise, while you have not yet been afflicted with trials like those that afflicted the believers who passed before you: from poverty, sicknesses, fear, terror, and they were shaken with various kinds of fears, until their Messenger and the believers with him said -hastening the victory from Allah Almighty-: When is the victory of Allah? Surely the victory of Allah is near to the believers.

This verse reminds believers that Paradise requires trials and perseverance, similar to the hardships faced by believers in the past. Despite difficult times, Allah’s help is always near.

Verse 215

يَسْأَلُونَكَ مَاذَا يُنْفِقُونَ ۖ قُلْ مَا أَنْفَقْتُمْ مِنْ خَيْرٍ فَلِلْوَالِدَيْنِ وَالْأَقْرَبِينَ وَالْيَتَامَىٰ وَالْمَسَاكِينِ وَابْنِ السَّبِيلِ ۗ وَمَا تَفْعَلُوا مِنْ خَيْرٍ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ بِهِ عَلِيمٌ

They ask you ˹O Prophet in˺ what ˹way˺ they should donate. Say, “Whatever donations you give are for parents, relatives, orphans, the poor, and ˹needy˺ travellers. Whatever good you do is certainly well known to Allah.”

Your companions ask you -O Prophet- what they should spend of their various kinds of wealth to draw nearer to Allah Almighty, and on whom they should spend? Say to them: Spend whatever good is available to you from the various kinds of lawful, good wealth, and make your spending for parents, relatives from your family and your kin, orphans, the poor, and the needy traveler who is far from his family and wealth. And whatever good you do, then Allah is All-Knowing of it.

This verse instructs on charitable giving, specifying that donations should be for parents, relatives, orphans, the poor, and needy travelers. Allah is aware of all good deeds.

Verse 216

كُتِبَ عَلَيْكُمُ الْقِتَالُ وَهُوَ كُرْهٌ لَكُمْ ۖ وَعَسَىٰ أَنْ تَكْرَهُوا شَيْئًا وَهُوَ خَيْرٌ لَكُمْ ۖ وَعَسَىٰ أَنْ تُحِبُّوا شَيْئًا وَهُوَ شَرٌّ لَكُمْ ۗ وَاللَّهُ يَعْلَمُ وَأَنْتُمْ لَا تَعْلَمُونَ

Fighting has been made obligatory upon you ˹believers˺, though you dislike it. Perhaps you dislike something which is good for you and like something which is bad for you. Allah knows and you do not know.

Allah has prescribed for you - O believers - fighting the disbelievers, and fighting is disliked by you due to its nature; for its hardship and the multitude of its dangers, and you may dislike something which is in reality good for you, and you may love something for what it contains of comfort or immediate pleasure, and it is evil for you. And Allah, Most High, knows what is best for you, and you do not know that. So hasten to Jihad in His path.

This verse states that fighting (Jihad) is obligatory, even though it may be disliked. It emphasizes that Allah's knowledge is greater than ours, and what seems bad may be good, and vice-versa. Believers should trust Allah's wisdom.

Verse 217

يَسْأَلُونَكَ عَنِ الشَّهْرِ الْحَرَامِ قِتَالٍ فِيهِ ۖ قُلْ قِتَالٌ فِيهِ كَبِيرٌ ۖ وَصَدٌّ عَنْ سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ وَكُفْرٌ بِهِ وَالْمَسْجِدِ الْحَرَامِ وَإِخْرَاجُ أَهْلِهِ مِنْهُ أَكْبَرُ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ ۚ وَالْفِتْنَةُ أَكْبَرُ مِنَ الْقَتْلِ ۗ وَلَا يَزَالُونَ يُقَاتِلُونَكُمْ حَتَّىٰ يَرُدُّوكُمْ عَنْ دِينِكُمْ إِنِ اسْتَطَاعُوا ۚ وَمَنْ يَرْتَدِدْ مِنْكُمْ عَنْ دِينِهِ فَيَمُتْ وَهُوَ كَافِرٌ فَأُولَٰئِكَ حَبِطَتْ أَعْمَالُهُمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ ۖ وَأُولَٰئِكَ أَصْحَابُ النَّارِ ۖ هُمْ فِيهَا خَالِدُونَ

They ask you ˹O Prophet˺ about fighting in the sacred months. Say, “Fighting during these months is a great sin. But hindering ˹others˺ from the Path of Allah, rejecting Him, and expelling the worshippers from the Sacred Mosque is ˹a˺ greater ˹sin˺ in the sight of Allah. For persecution is far worse than killing. And they will not stop fighting you until they turn you away from your faith—if they can. And whoever among you renounces their own faith and dies a disbeliever, their deeds will become void in this life and in the Hereafter. It is they who will be the residents of the Fire. They will be there forever.”

The polytheists ask you - O Messenger - about the sacred month: is fighting permissible in it? Say to them: Fighting in the sacred month is a great thing in the sight of Allah, to consider it lawful and to shed blood in it, and your preventing people from entering Islam by torture and intimidation, and your denial of Allah, His Messenger, and His religion, and your preventing Muslims from entering the Sacred Mosque, and your expulsion of the Prophet and the emigrants from it while they are its people and guardians, that is a greater sin, and a greater crime in the sight of Allah than fighting in the Sacred Month. And the polytheism that you are in is greater and more severe than killing in the sacred month. And these disbelievers have not been deterred from their crimes, but they are continuing in them, and they will continue to fight you until they turn you back from Islam to disbelief if they can achieve that. And whoever among you - O Muslims - obeys them and apostatizes from his religion and dies in disbelief, then his work in this world and the hereafter has gone, and he has become one of those who are confined to the fire of Hell, never to leave it.

This verse addresses fighting during sacred months, stating it's a great sin. However, hindering people from Allah’s path, denying Him, and expelling believers from the Sacred Mosque are greater sins. Persecution is worse than killing. Disbelievers will fight to turn believers away from Islam, and apostasy leads to eternal punishment.

Verse 218

إِنَّ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَالَّذِينَ هَاجَرُوا وَجَاهَدُوا فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ أُولَٰئِكَ يَرْجُونَ رَحْمَتَ اللَّهِ ۚ وَاللَّهُ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ

Surely those who have believed, emigrated, and struggled in the Way of Allah—they can hope for Allah’s mercy. And Allah is All-Forgiving, Most Merciful.

Indeed, those who believed in Allah and His Messenger and acted according to His law, and those who left their homes, and strived in the cause of Allah, those are the ones who hope for the bounty of Allah and His reward. And Allah is Forgiving of the sins of His believing servants, Merciful towards them with vast mercy.

This verse highlights that those who believe, emigrate for Allah’s cause, and strive in His path can hope for Allah's mercy. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful to His believing servants.

Verse 219

يَسْأَلُونَكَ عَنِ الْخَمْرِ وَالْمَيْسِرِ ۖ قُلْ فِيهِمَا إِثْمٌ كَبِيرٌ وَمَنَافِعُ لِلنَّاسِ وَإِثْمُهُمَا أَكْبَرُ مِنْ نَفْعِهِمَا ۗ وَيَسْأَلُونَكَ مَاذَا يُنْفِقُونَ قُلِ الْعَفْوَ ۗ كَذَٰلِكَ يُبَيِّنُ اللَّهُ لَكُمُ الْآيَاتِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَتَفَكَّرُونَ

They ask you ˹O Prophet˺ about intoxicants and gambling. Say, “There is great evil in both, as well as some benefit for people—but the evil outweighs the benefit.” They ˹also˺ ask you what they should donate. Say, “Whatever you can spare.” This is how Allah makes His revelations clear to you ˹believers˺, so perhaps you may reflect

The Muslims ask you - O Prophet - about the ruling on consuming alcohol, drinking it, selling it and buying it. And alcohol is every intoxicant that clouds the mind and covers it, whether it is a drink or food, and they ask you about the ruling on gambling - which is taking money or giving it in gambling, which are competitions in which there is a reward from both sides - Say to them: In that there are many harms and evils in religion and this world, in intellect and wealth, and in them are benefits for people from the aspect of earning money and other things, and their sin is greater than their benefit; as they prevent from the remembrance of Allah and from prayer, and they cause enmity and hatred between people, and they waste money. And this was a prelude to their prohibition. And they ask you about the amount they should spend of their wealth as charity and voluntary donation. Say to them: Spend the amount that exceeds your needs. Like that clear explanation, Allah explains to you the verses and rulings of the Sharia; so that you may reflect on what benefits you in this world and the hereafter. And they ask you - O Prophet - about the orphans, how they should deal with them in their livelihood and their wealth? Say to them: Your reforming them is better, so do what is most beneficial for them always, and if you mix with them in all aspects of life, then they are your brothers in religion. And the brother should take care of his brother’s interest. And Allah knows the one who wastes the wealth of orphans from the one who is keen to reform it. And if Allah had willed, He would have made it difficult and hard for you by prohibiting mixing. Indeed, Allah is Mighty in His dominion, Wise in His creation, planning and legislation.

This verse discusses intoxicants and gambling. While they may have some benefits, their harm is greater. It also clarifies that believers should donate what they can spare. Allah explains His verses so people may reflect.

Verse 220

فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ ۗ وَيَسْأَلُونَكَ عَنِ الْيَتَامَىٰ ۖ قُلْ إِصْلَاحٌ لَهُمْ خَيْرٌ ۖ وَإِنْ تُخَالِطُوهُمْ فَإِخْوَانُكُمْ ۚ وَاللَّهُ يَعْلَمُ الْمُفْسِدَ مِنَ الْمُصْلِحِ ۚ وَلَوْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ لَأَعْنَتَكُمْ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ عَزِيزٌ حَكِيمٌ

upon this world and the Hereafter. And they ask you concerning orphans. Say, “Improving their condition is best. And if you partner with them, they are bonded with you ˹in faith˺. And Allah knows who intends harm and who intends good. Had Allah willed, He could have made it difficult for you. Surely Allah is Almighty, All-Wise.”

The Muslims ask you, [O Prophet], about the ruling on consuming intoxicants in drinking, selling, and buying. Intoxicants are all substances that cloud and cover the mind, whether they are drunk or eaten. They ask you about the ruling on gambling - which is taking or giving money through wagering, which are competitions where there is a compensation from both sides. Say to them, “In that are great harms and corruption in religion and the world, intellects, and wealth, and in them are benefits for people from the angle of earning wealth and other things, but their sin is greater than their benefit, as they prevent the remembrance of Allah and from prayer, cause enmity and hatred between people, and destroy wealth.” This was a prelude to their prohibition. And they ask you about the amount they should spend from their wealth voluntarily as charity. Say to them, “Spend the amount that exceeds your need.” Like that clear explanation, Allah makes clear to you the verses and rulings of the Sharia, so that you may reflect on what benefits you in this world and the Hereafter. And they ask you, [O Prophet], about the orphans, how they should deal with them in their livelihood and wealth. Say to them, “Improving their situation is better, so always do what is most beneficial for them. And if you mix with them in all aspects of life, then they are your brothers in religion.” And a brother should look after the interests of his brother. And Allah knows the one who wastes the wealth of the orphans from the one who is keen to improve it. And if Allah had willed, He would have made it difficult and hard for you by prohibiting mixing. Indeed, Allah is Mighty in His kingdom, Wise in His creation, management, and legislation.

This verse addresses questions about intoxicants, gambling, and treatment of orphans. It clarifies that while there may be some benefits, the harm of intoxicants and gambling is greater. It also emphasizes the importance of improving the condition of orphans and treating them as brothers in faith. Allah knows the intentions behind our actions.

Verse 221

وَلَا تَنْكِحُوا الْمُشْرِكَاتِ حَتَّىٰ يُؤْمِنَّ ۚ وَلَأَمَةٌ مُؤْمِنَةٌ خَيْرٌ مِنْ مُشْرِكَةٍ وَلَوْ أَعْجَبَتْكُمْ ۗ وَلَا تُنْكِحُوا الْمُشْرِكِينَ حَتَّىٰ يُؤْمِنُوا ۚ وَلَعَبْدٌ مُؤْمِنٌ خَيْرٌ مِنْ مُشْرِكٍ وَلَوْ أَعْجَبَكُمْ ۗ أُولَٰئِكَ يَدْعُونَ إِلَى النَّارِ ۖ وَاللَّهُ يَدْعُو إِلَى الْجَنَّةِ وَالْمَغْفِرَةِ بِإِذْنِهِ ۖ وَيُبَيِّنُ آيَاتِهِ لِلنَّاسِ لَعَلَّهُمْ يَتَذَكَّرُونَ

Do not marry polytheistic women until they believe; for a believing slave-woman is better than a free polytheist, even though she may look pleasant to you. And do not marry your women to polytheistic men until they believe, for a believing slave-man is better than a free polytheist, even though he may look pleasant to you. They invite ˹you˺ to the Fire while Allah invites ˹you˺ to Paradise and forgiveness by His grace. He makes His revelations clear to the people so perhaps they will be mindful.

And do not marry polytheistic women who worship idols until they embrace Islam. And know that a slave woman who has no wealth or lineage, believing in Allah, is better than a free polytheistic woman, even if the free polytheistic woman impresses you. And do not marry your believing women, whether slaves or free women, to polytheists until they believe in Allah and His Messenger. And know that a believing slave, despite his poverty, is better than a polytheist, even if the polytheist impresses you. Those who are characterized by polytheism, men and women, call all those who associate with them to what leads them to Hellfire. And Allah, the Exalted, calls His servants to His true religion, which leads them to Paradise and forgiveness of their sins, by His permission, and He clarifies His verses and rulings for people so that they may remember and take heed.

This verse prohibits marriage with polytheists, stating that a believing slave is better than a free polytheist, regardless of attractiveness. It emphasizes the importance of faith and warns that polytheists invite to the Fire, while Allah invites to Paradise.

Verse 222

وَيَسْأَلُونَكَ عَنِ الْمَحِيضِ ۖ قُلْ هُوَ أَذًى فَاعْتَزِلُوا النِّسَاءَ فِي الْمَحِيضِ ۖ وَلَا تَقْرَبُوهُنَّ حَتَّىٰ يَطْهُرْنَ ۖ فَإِذَا تَطَهَّرْنَ فَأْتُوهُنَّ مِنْ حَيْثُ أَمَرَكُمُ اللَّهُ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ يُحِبُّ التَّوَّابِينَ وَيُحِبُّ الْمُتَطَهِّرِينَ

They ask you ˹O Prophet˺ about menstruation. Say, “Beware of its harm! So keep away, and do not have intercourse with your wives during their monthly cycles until they are purified. When they purify themselves, then you may approach them in the manner specified by Allah. Surely Allah loves those who always turn to Him in repentance and those who purify themselves.”

And they ask you about menstruation - which is the blood that flows from the wombs of women naturally at specific times. Say to them, [O Prophet], “It is a harmful impurity that harms those who approach it, so abstain from marital relations with women during menstruation until the bleeding stops. Then, when the bleeding has stopped and they have purified themselves, then have relations with them in the place that Allah has permitted for you, which is the vagina, not the anus. Indeed, Allah loves His servants who are abundant in seeking forgiveness and repentance, and He loves His servants who purify themselves, those who stay away from immoralities and impurities.”

This verse explains the rules regarding menstruation, stating that marital relations should be avoided during this time due to impurity. It emphasizes purity and seeking forgiveness, as these are beloved to Allah.

Verse 223

نِسَاؤُكُمْ حَرْثٌ لَكُمْ فَأْتُوا حَرْثَكُمْ أَنَّىٰ شِئْتُمْ ۖ وَقَدِّمُوا لِأَنْفُسِكُمْ ۚ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ وَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّكُمْ مُلَاقُوهُ ۗ وَبَشِّرِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ

Your wives are like farmland for you, so approach them ˹consensually˺ as you please. And send forth something good for yourselves. Be mindful of Allah, and know that you will meet Him. And give good news to the believers.

Your wives are a place of cultivation for you, you place the sperm in their wombs, and from it comes the children by the will of Allah, so have relations with them in the place of intercourse only, which is the vagina, in whatever manner you wish, and put forth for yourselves righteous deeds by observing the commands of Allah, and fear Allah, and know that you will meet Him for accountability on the Day of Judgment. And give good tidings to the believers, [O Prophet], of what pleases and gladdens them from good recompense in the Hereafter.

This verse uses the analogy of wives as farmland, indicating that relations are permissible, but within proper boundaries. It also urges righteous actions and reminds believers of their accountability to Allah and the good tidings for believers.

Verse 224

وَلَا تَجْعَلُوا اللَّهَ عُرْضَةً لِأَيْمَانِكُمْ أَنْ تَبَرُّوا وَتَتَّقُوا وَتُصْلِحُوا بَيْنَ النَّاسِ ۗ وَاللَّهُ سَمِيعٌ عَلِيمٌ

Do not use Allah’s Name in your oaths as an excuse for not doing good, not guarding against evil, or not making peace between people. And Allah is All-Hearing, All-Knowing.

And do not make your oaths by Allah a hindrance to you from righteousness, maintaining family ties, piety, and reconciliation among people, in that you are called to do one of these things, then you argue that you have sworn by Allah not to do it. Rather, the one who has sworn should retract his oath and do good deeds, and atone for his oath, and not make that a habit. And Allah is All-Hearing of your words, All-Knowing of all your conditions.

This verse cautions against using oaths by Allah's name as excuses to avoid good deeds, preventing acts of kindness, or hindering reconciliation. It encourages doing what is right, even if it means breaking an oath, while seeking atonement.

Verse 225

لَا يُؤَاخِذُكُمُ اللَّهُ بِاللَّغْوِ فِي أَيْمَانِكُمْ وَلَٰكِنْ يُؤَاخِذُكُمْ بِمَا كَسَبَتْ قُلُوبُكُمْ ۗ وَاللَّهُ غَفُورٌ حَلِيمٌ

Allah will not hold you accountable for unintentional oaths, but for what you intended in your hearts. And Allah is All-Forgiving, Most Forbearing.

Allah will not hold you accountable for your unintentional oaths, but He will hold you accountable for what your hearts have intended. And Allah is Forgiving to whoever repents to Him, and Forbearing to whoever disobeys Him when He does not hasten the punishment.

Allah does not hold people accountable for unintentional oaths, but for what they intend in their hearts. Allah is Forgiving and Forbearing.

Verse 226

لِلَّذِينَ يُؤْلُونَ مِنْ نِسَائِهِمْ تَرَبُّصُ أَرْبَعَةِ أَشْهُرٍ ۖ فَإِنْ فَاءُوا فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ

Those who swear not to have intercourse with their wives must wait for four months. If they change their mind, then Allah is certainly All-Forgiving, Most Merciful.

For those who swear by Allah that they will not have relations with their wives, there is a waiting period of four months. If they return before the four months have passed, then Allah is Forgiving for what has occurred from their oath due to their return, and Merciful to them.

For those who swear not to have relations with their wives, there is a waiting period of four months. If they reconcile, Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.

Verse 227

وَإِنْ عَزَمُوا الطَّلَاقَ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ سَمِيعٌ عَلِيمٌ

But if they settle on divorce, then Allah is indeed All-Hearing, All-Knowing.

And if they resolve to divorce, by continuing in their oath and abandoning relations, then Allah is Hearing of their words, Knowing of their intentions, and He will recompense them for that.

If they decide on divorce, Allah hears their words and knows their intentions.

Verse 228

وَالْمُطَلَّقَاتُ يَتَرَبَّصْنَ بِأَنْفُسِهِنَّ ثَلَاثَةَ قُرُوءٍ ۚ وَلَا يَحِلُّ لَهُنَّ أَنْ يَكْتُمْنَ مَا خَلَقَ اللَّهُ فِي أَرْحَامِهِنَّ إِنْ كُنَّ يُؤْمِنَّ بِاللَّهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ ۚ وَبُعُولَتُهُنَّ أَحَقُّ بِرَدِّهِنَّ فِي ذَٰلِكَ إِنْ أَرَادُوا إِصْلَاحًا ۚ وَلَهُنَّ مِثْلُ الَّذِي عَلَيْهِنَّ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ ۚ وَلِلرِّجَالِ عَلَيْهِنَّ دَرَجَةٌ ۗ وَاللَّهُ عَزِيزٌ حَكِيمٌ

Divorced women must wait three monthly cycles ˹before they can re-marry˺. It is not lawful for them to conceal what Allah has created in their wombs, if they ˹truly˺ believe in Allah and the Last Day. And their husbands reserve the right to take them back within that period if they desire reconciliation. Women have rights similar to those of men equitably, although men have a degree ˹of responsibility˺ above them. And Allah is Almighty, All-Wise.

Divorced women who menstruate must wait without marriage after the divorce for a period of three purifications or three menstrual cycles as a waiting period; to ensure that the womb is clear of pregnancy. And it is not permissible for them to marry another man during this waiting period until it is over. And it is not lawful for them to conceal what Allah has created in their wombs, of pregnancy or menstruation, if the divorced women are truly believers in Allah and the Last Day. And the husbands of the divorced women have more right to take them back during the waiting period. And that should be with the intention of reconciliation and good, not with the intention of harm, torturing them by prolonging the waiting period. And for women are rights over men, similar to those of men, in a known manner, and for men over women is an added degree of good companionship and association with kindness, and guardianship of the house and ownership of divorce. And Allah is Mighty, possessing absolute might, Wise, He places everything in its proper place.

Divorced women must wait three menstrual cycles before remarrying. They should not hide pregnancies. Husbands have a right to reconcile within this period. Women have rights similar to men, although men have a degree of responsibility. Allah is Almighty and Wise.

Verse 229

الطَّلَاقُ مَرَّتَانِ ۖ فَإِمْسَاكٌ بِمَعْرُوفٍ أَوْ تَسْرِيحٌ بِإِحْسَانٍ ۗ وَلَا يَحِلُّ لَكُمْ أَنْ تَأْخُذُوا مِمَّا آتَيْتُمُوهُنَّ شَيْئًا إِلَّا أَنْ يَخَافَا أَلَّا يُقِيمَا حُدُودَ اللَّهِ ۖ فَإِنْ خِفْتُمْ أَلَّا يُقِيمَا حُدُودَ اللَّهِ فَلَا جُنَاحَ عَلَيْهِمَا فِيمَا افْتَدَتْ بِهِ ۗ تِلْكَ حُدُودُ اللَّهِ فَلَا تَعْتَدُوهَا ۚ وَمَنْ يَتَعَدَّ حُدُودَ اللَّهِ فَأُولَٰئِكَ هُمُ الظَّالِمُونَ

Divorce may be retracted twice, then the husband must retain ˹his wife˺ with honour or separate ˹from her˺ with grace. It is not lawful for husbands to take back anything of the dowry given to their wives, unless the couple fears not being able to keep within the limits of Allah. So if you fear they will not be able to keep within the limits of Allah, there is no blame if the wife compensates the husband to obtain divorce. These are the limits set by Allah, so do not transgress them. And whoever transgresses the limits of Allah, they are the ˹true˺ wrongdoers.

Divorce which allows for reconciliation is twice, one after the other. The rule of Allah after each divorce is to keep the woman with kindness, and good companionship after taking her back, or to release her with good treatment by giving her her rights, and that her ex-husband should not mention her with evil. And it is not permissible for you - O husbands - to take anything of what you have given them of the dowry and the like, unless the spouses fear that they will not uphold the marital rights, then they present their matter to the guardians, and if the guardians fear that the spouses will not uphold the limits of Allah, then there is no blame on the spouses for what the woman pays to the husband in return for her divorce. Those are the limits of Allah that separate between the lawful and unlawful, so do not transgress them, and whoever transgresses the limits of Allah, then those are the wrongdoers to themselves by exposing themselves to the punishment of Allah.

Divorce can be retracted twice. After that, husbands must keep their wives with honor or separate with kindness. Husbands cannot take back dowry unless they fear not upholding marital limits. If so, the wife can compensate for divorce. These are Allah's limits; do not transgress them.

Verse 230

فَإِنْ طَلَّقَهَا فَلَا تَحِلُّ لَهُ مِنْ بَعْدُ حَتَّىٰ تَنْكِحَ زَوْجًا غَيْرَهُ ۗ فَإِنْ طَلَّقَهَا فَلَا جُنَاحَ عَلَيْهِمَا أَنْ يَتَرَاجَعَا إِنْ ظَنَّا أَنْ يُقِيمَا حُدُودَ اللَّهِ ۗ وَتِلْكَ حُدُودُ اللَّهِ يُبَيِّنُهَا لِقَوْمٍ يَعْلَمُونَ

So if a husband divorces his wife ˹three times˺, then it is not lawful for him to remarry her until after she has married another man and then is divorced. Then it is permissible for them to reunite, as long as they feel they are able to maintain the limits of Allah. These are the limits set by Allah, which He makes clear for people of knowledge.

Then if the man divorces his wife for the third time, then she is not lawful for him until she marries another man in a valid marriage, and he consummates the marriage with her, and the marriage is out of desire, not with the intention of making the woman lawful for her first husband.
