If the other husband divorces her, or dies and her waiting period ends, then there is no sin on the woman and her first husband to remarry with a new contract and a new dowry if they believe that they will uphold the rules of Allah that He has legislated for the spouses. And those are the defined laws of Allah, He explains them to a people who know His laws and limits because they are the ones who benefit from them.

If a man divorces his wife three times, she cannot remarry him until she marries and divorces another man. Then, they can remarry if they believe they can maintain Allah’s limits. These are Allah’s laws for those who understand them.

Verse 231

وَإِذَا طَلَّقْتُمُ النِّسَاءَ فَبَلَغْنَ أَجَلَهُنَّ فَأَمْسِكُوهُنَّ بِمَعْرُوفٍ أَوْ سَرِّحُوهُنَّ بِمَعْرُوفٍ ۚ وَلَا تُمْسِكُوهُنَّ ضِرَارًا لِتَعْتَدُوا ۚ وَمَنْ يَفْعَلْ ذَٰلِكَ فَقَدْ ظَلَمَ نَفْسَهُ ۚ وَلَا تَتَّخِذُوا آيَاتِ اللَّهِ هُزُوًا ۚ وَاذْكُرُوا نِعْمَتَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكُمْ وَمَا أَنْزَلَ عَلَيْكُمْ مِنَ الْكِتَابِ وَالْحِكْمَةِ يَعِظُكُمْ بِهِ ۚ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ وَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عَلِيمٌ

When you divorce women and they have ˹almost˺ reached the end of their waiting period, either retain them honourably or let them go honourably. But do not retain them ˹only˺ to harm them ˹or˺ to take advantage ˹of them˺. Whoever does that surely wrongs his own soul. Do not take Allah’s revelations lightly. Remember Allah’s favours upon you as well as the Book and wisdom He has sent down for your guidance. Be mindful of Allah, and know that Allah has ˹perfect˺ knowledge of all things.

And when you have divorced women and they are about to reach the end of their waiting period, then either retain them in a good manner or let them go in a good manner. And do not retain them to harm them, that you may transgress. And whoever does that has certainly wronged himself. And do not take the verses of Allah in jest. And remember the favor of Allah upon you and what He has revealed to you of the Book and wisdom by which He instructs you. And fear Allah and know that Allah is All-Knowing of everything.

This verse addresses divorce, instructing men to either reconcile with their wives honorably or let them go kindly, without causing them harm or taking advantage. It warns against treating Allah's revelations lightly and urges remembrance of His favors and guidance.

Verse 232

وَإِذَا طَلَّقْتُمُ النِّسَاءَ فَبَلَغْنَ أَجَلَهُنَّ فَلَا تَعْضُلُوهُنَّ أَنْ يَنْكِحْنَ أَزْوَاجَهُنَّ إِذَا تَرَاضَوْا بَيْنَهُمْ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ ۗ ذَٰلِكَ يُوعَظُ بِهِ مَنْ كَانَ مِنْكُمْ يُؤْمِنُ بِاللَّهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ ۗ ذَٰلِكُمْ أَزْكَىٰ لَكُمْ وَأَطْهَرُ ۗ وَاللَّهُ يَعْلَمُ وَأَنْتُمْ لَا تَعْلَمُونَ

When you have divorced women and they have reached the end of their waiting period, do not prevent them from re-marrying their ex-husbands if they come to an honourable agreement. This is enjoined on whoever has faith in Allah and the Last Day. This is purer and more dignifying for you. Allah knows and you do not know.

And when you divorce women and they have fulfilled their term, do not prevent them from remarrying their former husbands if they agree among themselves on an acceptable basis. This is an admonition for whoever among you believes in Allah and the Last Day. That is more virtuous for you and purer. And Allah knows, while you do not know.

This verse emphasizes that after divorce, women should not be prevented from remarrying their ex-husbands if they both agree. This promotes dignified relationships and highlights the importance of faith in Allah and the Last Day in decision-making.

Verse 233

وَالْوَالِدَاتُ يُرْضِعْنَ أَوْلَادَهُنَّ حَوْلَيْنِ كَامِلَيْنِ ۖ لِمَنْ أَرَادَ أَنْ يُتِمَّ الرَّضَاعَةَ ۚ وَعَلَى الْمَوْلُودِ لَهُ رِزْقُهُنَّ وَكِسْوَتُهُنَّ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ ۚ لَا تُكَلَّفُ نَفْسٌ إِلَّا وُسْعَهَا ۚ لَا تُضَارَّ وَالِدَةٌ بِوَلَدِهَا وَلَا مَوْلُودٌ لَهُ بِوَلَدِهِ ۚ وَعَلَى الْوَارِثِ مِثْلُ ذَٰلِكَ ۗ فَإِنْ أَرَادَا فِصَالًا عَنْ تَرَاضٍ مِنْهُمَا وَتَشَاوُرٍ فَلَا جُنَاحَ عَلَيْهِمَا ۗ وَإِنْ أَرَدْتُمْ أَنْ تَسْتَرْضِعُوا أَوْلَادَكُمْ فَلَا جُنَاحَ عَلَيْكُمْ إِذَا سَلَّمْتُمْ مَا آتَيْتُمْ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ ۗ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ وَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ بَصِيرٌ

˹Divorced˺ mothers will breastfeed their offspring for two whole years, for those who wish to complete the nursing ˹of their child˺. The child’s father will provide reasonable maintenance and clothing for the mother ˹during that period˺. No one will be charged with more than they can bear. No mother or father should be made to suffer for their child. The ˹father’s˺ heirs are under the same obligation. But if both sides decide—after mutual consultation and consent—to wean a child, then there is no blame on them. And if you decide to have your children nursed by a wet-nurse, it is permissible as long as you pay fairly. Be mindful of Allah, and know that Allah is All-Seeing of what you do.

Mothers may breastfeed their children two whole years for whoever wishes to complete the nursing [period]. Upon the father is the mothers' provision and their clothing, according to what is acceptable. No person is charged with more than his capacity. No mother should be harmed through her child, and no father through his child. And upon the heir is [a duty] like that [of the father]. And if they both desire weaning through mutual consent and consultation, there is no blame upon them. And if you wish to have your children nursed by a substitute, there is no blame upon you as long as you pay what you promised, according to what is acceptable. And fear Allah and know that Allah is Seeing of what you do.

This verse outlines the responsibilities of parents concerning breastfeeding. Mothers can breastfeed for two years, and fathers are responsible for their provision and clothing. Decisions about weaning should be made with mutual consent, and if a wet-nurse is needed, payment should be fair. The verse emphasizes being mindful of Allah and His watchfulness.

Verse 234

وَالَّذِينَ يُتَوَفَّوْنَ مِنْكُمْ وَيَذَرُونَ أَزْوَاجًا يَتَرَبَّصْنَ بِأَنْفُسِهِنَّ أَرْبَعَةَ أَشْهُرٍ وَعَشْرًا ۖ فَإِذَا بَلَغْنَ أَجَلَهُنَّ فَلَا جُنَاحَ عَلَيْكُمْ فِيمَا فَعَلْنَ فِي أَنْفُسِهِنَّ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ ۗ وَاللَّهُ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ خَبِيرٌ

As for those of you who die and leave widows behind, let them observe a waiting period of four months and ten days. When they have reached the end of this period, then you are not accountable for what they decide for themselves in a reasonable manner. And Allah is All-Aware of what you do.

And those who die among you and leave wives behind, they should wait by themselves for a period of four months and ten days. They should not leave the marital home, nor adorn themselves, nor marry. If the mentioned period ends, then there is no blame upon you, O guardians of women, for what they do with themselves in terms of leaving, adorning themselves, and marrying in the manner prescribed by law. And Allah, the Exalted, is Aware of your deeds, both apparent and hidden, and He will recompense you for them.

This verse outlines the waiting period ('iddah) for widows, which is four months and ten days. During this time, they should not remarry. Once the waiting period is over, guardians are not responsible for women’s decisions regarding marriage, as long as it's reasonable. Allah is fully aware of all actions.

Verse 235

وَلَا جُنَاحَ عَلَيْكُمْ فِيمَا عَرَّضْتُمْ بِهِ مِنْ خِطْبَةِ النِّسَاءِ أَوْ أَكْنَنْتُمْ فِي أَنْفُسِكُمْ ۚ عَلِمَ اللَّهُ أَنَّكُمْ سَتَذْكُرُونَهُنَّ وَلَٰكِنْ لَا تُوَاعِدُوهُنَّ سِرًّا إِلَّا أَنْ تَقُولُوا قَوْلًا مَعْرُوفًا ۚ وَلَا تَعْزِمُوا عُقْدَةَ النِّكَاحِ حَتَّىٰ يَبْلُغَ الْكِتَابُ أَجَلَهُ ۚ وَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ يَعْلَمُ مَا فِي أَنْفُسِكُمْ فَاحْذَرُوهُ ۚ وَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ غَفُورٌ حَلِيمٌ

There is no blame on you for subtly showing interest in ˹divorced or widowed˺ women or for hiding ˹the intention˺ in your hearts. Allah knows that you are considering them ˹for marriage˺. But do not make a secret commitment with them—you can only show interest in them appropriately. Do not commit to the bond of marriage until the waiting period expires. Know that Allah is aware of what is in your hearts, so beware of Him. And know that Allah is All-Forgiving, Most Forbearing.

And there is no blame upon you - O men - for what you hint at in proposing marriage to women whose husbands have died, or those divorced irrevocably during their waiting period. Nor is there any sin upon you for what you conceal within yourselves of intending to marry them after their waiting period ends. Allah knows that you will remember the women in their waiting period, and you will not be able to restrain yourselves from speaking about them, due to your weakness. Therefore, He has permitted you to mention them indirectly or to conceal it within yourselves. And beware of making secret promises of marriage with them, by committing adultery or agreeing to marry during the waiting period, unless you speak words that imply that such a woman is desirable to husbands. And do not resolve upon a marriage contract during the waiting period until its term has ended. And know that Allah knows what is in your hearts, so fear Him. And know that Allah is Forgiving to those who repent of their sins, Forbearing towards His servants, He does not hasten punishment upon them.

This verse permits men to subtly express interest in marrying divorced or widowed women during their waiting period, without making secret commitments. Marriage contracts should only be made after the waiting period ends. Allah knows the intentions of the heart, and encourages awareness and repentance.

Verse 236

لَا جُنَاحَ عَلَيْكُمْ إِنْ طَلَّقْتُمُ النِّسَاءَ مَا لَمْ تَمَسُّوهُنَّ أَوْ تَفْرِضُوا لَهُنَّ فَرِيضَةً ۚ وَمَتِّعُوهُنَّ عَلَى الْمُوسِعِ قَدَرُهُ وَعَلَى الْمُقْتِرِ قَدَرُهُ مَتَاعًا بِالْمَعْرُوفِ ۖ حَقًّا عَلَى الْمُحْسِنِينَ

There is no blame if you divorce women before the marriage is consummated or the dowry is settled. But give them a ˹suitable˺ compensation—the rich according to his means and the poor according to his. A reasonable compensation is an obligation on the good-doers.

There is no blame upon you - O husbands - if you divorce women after the contract has been made, but before you have consummated the marriage or specified a dowry for them. Provide for them something beneficial, to compensate them, ward off the distress of divorce, and remove grudges. This provision is obligatory according to the circumstances of the divorcing man: the wealthy according to his means, and the poor according to his ability; provision in the manner known by law. And it is a right established upon those who do good to the divorced women and to themselves by obeying Allah.

This verse states that there is no blame in divorcing a woman before consummation or settling the dowry. However, it emphasizes that a fair compensation should be given to the divorced women. The compensation should be according to the means of the husband, and it is an obligation upon the good-doers.

Verse 237

وَإِنْ طَلَّقْتُمُوهُنَّ مِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ تَمَسُّوهُنَّ وَقَدْ فَرَضْتُمْ لَهُنَّ فَرِيضَةً فَنِصْفُ مَا فَرَضْتُمْ إِلَّا أَنْ يَعْفُونَ أَوْ يَعْفُوَ الَّذِي بِيَدِهِ عُقْدَةُ النِّكَاحِ ۚ وَأَنْ تَعْفُوا أَقْرَبُ لِلتَّقْوَىٰ ۚ وَلَا تَنْسَوُا الْفَضْلَ بَيْنَكُمْ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ بَصِيرٌ

And if you divorce them before consummating the marriage but after deciding on a dowry, pay half of the dowry, unless the wife graciously waives it or the husband graciously pays in full. Graciousness is closer to righteousness. And do not forget kindness among yourselves. Surely Allah is All-Seeing of what you do.

And if you divorce women after the contract has been made, but you have not consummated the marriage, but you have obligated yourselves to a specified dowry for them, then you must give them half of the agreed upon dowry, unless the divorced women forgo it and relinquish half of the dowry due to them, or the husband allows the divorced woman to keep the entire dowry. And your forbearance, O men and women, is closer to the fear of Allah and obedience to Him. And do not forget - O people - the favor and kindness between you, which is giving what is not obligatory upon you, and being lenient in rights. Indeed, Allah is Seeing of what you do, He encourages you towards good and urges you towards virtue.

If a divorce occurs before consummation but after the dowry is settled, half of the dowry should be given to the divorced woman. However, the wife can choose to waive her right to it or the husband can generously pay the full dowry. Kindness and leniency in all dealings are encouraged, as Allah sees all actions.

Verse 238

حَافِظُوا عَلَى الصَّلَوَاتِ وَالصَّلَاةِ الْوُسْطَىٰ وَقُومُوا لِلَّهِ قَانِتِينَ

Observe the ˹five obligatory˺ prayers—especially the middle prayer—and stand in true devotion to Allah.

O Muslims, safeguard the five obligatory prayers by persevering in performing them at their prescribed times, fulfilling their conditions, pillars, and obligations. And safeguard the middle prayer among them, which is the afternoon prayer, and stand in your prayers obedient to Allah, humble and submissive.

This verse emphasizes the importance of maintaining the five daily prayers, especially the middle prayer (often considered the afternoon prayer), with devotion and humility to Allah.

Verse 239

فَإِنْ خِفْتُمْ فَرِجَالًا أَوْ رُكْبَانًا ۖ فَإِذَا أَمِنْتُمْ فَاذْكُرُوا اللَّهَ كَمَا عَلَّمَكُمْ مَا لَمْ تَكُونُوا تَعْلَمُونَ

If you are in danger, pray on foot or while riding. But when you are safe, ˹take time to˺ remember Allah for teaching you what you did not know.

And if you fear an enemy, then pray the prayer of fear while walking or riding, in any way you can, even by gesturing, or facing a direction other than the Qiblah. Then when your fear is gone, perform the prayer of security, and remember Allah in it, and do not diminish it from its original form, and give thanks to Him for what He has taught you of matters of worship and rulings that you did not know.

This verse allows for flexibility in prayer during times of danger, permitting prayer on foot or while riding. However, when safe, Muslims are obligated to remember Allah and perform prayers correctly as taught.

Verse 240

وَالَّذِينَ يُتَوَفَّوْنَ مِنْكُمْ وَيَذَرُونَ أَزْوَاجًا وَصِيَّةً لِأَزْوَاجِهِمْ مَتَاعًا إِلَى الْحَوْلِ غَيْرَ إِخْرَاجٍ ۚ فَإِنْ خَرَجْنَ فَلَا جُنَاحَ عَلَيْكُمْ فِي مَا فَعَلْنَ فِي أَنْفُسِهِنَّ مِنْ مَعْرُوفٍ ۗ وَاللَّهُ عَزِيزٌ حَكِيمٌ

Those of you who die leaving widows should bequeath for them a year’s maintenance without forcing them out. But if they choose to leave, you are not accountable for what they reasonably decide for themselves. And Allah is Almighty, All-Wise.

And the spouses who die and leave behind wives, it is incumbent upon them to make a will for them: that they be provided with maintenance for a full year from the day of death, with residence in the husband's house without the heirs evicting them for the duration of the year, as a consolation to the wife and as righteousness to the deceased. If the wives leave of their own accord before the end of the year, then there is no blame upon you -O heirs- in that, nor is there any blame on the wives for what they do for themselves of permissible matters. And Allah is Mighty in His dominion, Wise in His command and prohibition. And this verse is abrogated by His statement, may He be exalted: (And those of you who die and leave behind wives, they should wait concerning themselves four months and ten days).

This verse addresses the rights of widows, instructing that they should be provided for a year after their husband's death. However, this instruction is understood to be abrogated by a subsequent verse and is no longer in effect. The verse emphasizes the importance of fair treatment of widows.

Verse 241

وَلِلْمُطَلَّقَاتِ مَتَاعٌ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ ۖ حَقًّا عَلَى الْمُتَّقِينَ

Reasonable provisions must be made for divorced women—a duty on those mindful ˹of Allah˺.

And for divorced women is a provision of clothing and maintenance, in a fair and proper manner according to the law, a right upon those who fear Allah and are mindful of Him in His commands and prohibitions.

This verse establishes that divorced women should receive reasonable provision. This emphasizes the responsibility of those who fear Allah to treat divorced women fairly and justly.

Verse 242

كَذَٰلِكَ يُبَيِّنُ اللَّهُ لَكُمْ آيَاتِهِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَعْقِلُونَ

This is how Allah makes His revelations clear to you, so perhaps you will understand.

Like that clear explanation in the rulings concerning children and women, Allah makes clear to you His signs and rulings in all that you need in your livelihood and your Hereafter, so that you may understand them and act upon them.

This verse declares that Allah clarifies His signs and laws to guide people, so that they may understand and follow them in their daily lives.

Verse 243

أَلَمْ تَرَ إِلَى الَّذِينَ خَرَجُوا مِنْ دِيَارِهِمْ وَهُمْ أُلُوفٌ حَذَرَ الْمَوْتِ فَقَالَ لَهُمُ اللَّهُ مُوتُوا ثُمَّ أَحْيَاهُمْ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَذُو فَضْلٍ عَلَى النَّاسِ وَلَٰكِنَّ أَكْثَرَ النَّاسِ لَا يَشْكُرُونَ

Have you ˹O Prophet˺ not seen those who fled their homes in the thousands for fear of death? Allah said to them, “Die!” then He gave them life. Surely Allah is ever Bountiful to humanity, but most people are ungrateful.

Did you not know -O Messenger- the story of those who fled from their lands and homes, and they were many thousands, fearing death from the plague or fighting? So Allah said to them: Die, so they died all at once as a punishment for their fleeing from the decree of Allah. Then Allah brought them back to life after a period, to fulfill their appointed terms and to take heed and repent? Indeed, Allah is the Possessor of great bounty over the people with His many blessings, but most of the people do not give thanks for the bounty of Allah upon them.

This verse tells the story of people who fled their homes to avoid death, and Allah caused them to die and then brought them back to life. This story highlights Allah's power and the importance of gratitude.

Verse 244

وَقَاتِلُوا فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ وَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ سَمِيعٌ عَلِيمٌ

Fight in the cause of Allah, and know that Allah is All-Hearing, All-Knowing.

And fight -O Muslims- the disbelievers in support of the religion of Allah, and know that Allah is Hearing of your words, Knowing of your intentions and actions.

This verse commands Muslims to fight for the cause of Allah and reminds them that Allah is All-Hearing and All-Knowing.

Verse 245

مَنْ ذَا الَّذِي يُقْرِضُ اللَّهَ قَرْضًا حَسَنًا فَيُضَاعِفَهُ لَهُ أَضْعَافًا كَثِيرَةً ۚ وَاللَّهُ يَقْبِضُ وَيَبْسُطُ وَإِلَيْهِ تُرْجَعُونَ

Who will lend to Allah a good loan which Allah will multiply many times over? It is Allah ˹alone˺ who decreases and increases ˹wealth˺. And to Him you will ˹all˺ be returned.

Who is it that will lend to Allah a goodly loan, expecting the reward, so that He will multiply it many times over with a reward and good recompense that cannot be counted? And Allah withholds and grants abundantly, so spend and do not worry, for He is the Provider, He restricts the provision for whom He wills among His servants, and expands it for others, and He has the supreme wisdom in that. And to Him alone you will return after death, and He will recompense you for your deeds.

This verse encourages charitable giving as a loan to Allah which He will multiply. This highlights Allah's power to increase or decrease wealth and the return to Allah after death for final recompense.

Verse 246

أَلَمْ تَرَ إِلَى الْمَلَإِ مِنْ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ مِنْ بَعْدِ مُوسَىٰ إِذْ قَالُوا لِنَبِيٍّ لَهُمُ ابْعَثْ لَنَا مَلِكًا نُقَاتِلْ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ ۖ قَالَ هَلْ عَسَيْتُمْ إِنْ كُتِبَ عَلَيْكُمُ الْقِتَالُ أَلَّا تُقَاتِلُوا ۖ قَالُوا وَمَا لَنَا أَلَّا نُقَاتِلَ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ وَقَدْ أُخْرِجْنَا مِنْ دِيَارِنَا وَأَبْنَائِنَا ۖ فَلَمَّا كُتِبَ عَلَيْهِمُ الْقِتَالُ تَوَلَّوْا إِلَّا قَلِيلًا مِنْهُمْ ۗ وَاللَّهُ عَلِيمٌ بِالظَّالِمِينَ

Have you not seen those chiefs of the Children of Israel after Moses? They said to one of their prophets, “Appoint for us a king, ˹and˺ we will fight in the cause of Allah.” He said, “Are you not going to cower if ordered to fight?” They replied, “How could we refuse to fight in the cause of Allah, while we were driven out of our homes and ˹separated from˺ our children?” But when they were ordered to fight, they fled, except for a few of them. And Allah has ˹perfect˺ knowledge of the wrongdoers.

Did you not know - O Messenger - the story of the nobles and dignitaries of the Children of Israel after the time of Moses? When they asked their prophet to appoint a king over them, under whose leadership they could unite and fight their enemies in the way of Allah. Their prophet said to them: Is it as I expect, that if fighting in the way of Allah is ordained for you, you will not fight? For I expect your cowardice and flight from battle. They said, rejecting their prophet's expectation: And what prevents us from fighting in the way of Allah, when our enemy has driven us out of our homes and separated us from our children by killing and captivity? But when Allah ordained fighting for them with the king He appointed for them, they became cowardly and fled from battle, except for a few of them who stood firm by the grace of Allah. And Allah is Knowing of the wrongdoers who break their covenants.

This verse recounts how the Children of Israel, after Moses, asked their prophet for a king to lead them in battle. Despite their initial eagerness to fight, most of them turned away when ordered to do so. This highlights the hypocrisy and weakness of some of their convictions.

Verse 247

وَقَالَ لَهُمْ نَبِيُّهُمْ إِنَّ اللَّهَ قَدْ بَعَثَ لَكُمْ طَالُوتَ مَلِكًا ۚ قَالُوا أَنَّىٰ يَكُونُ لَهُ الْمُلْكُ عَلَيْنَا وَنَحْنُ أَحَقُّ بِالْمُلْكِ مِنْهُ وَلَمْ يُؤْتَ سَعَةً مِنَ الْمَالِ ۚ قَالَ إِنَّ اللَّهَ اصْطَفَاهُ عَلَيْكُمْ وَزَادَهُ بَسْطَةً فِي الْعِلْمِ وَالْجِسْمِ ۖ وَاللَّهُ يُؤْتِي مُلْكَهُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ ۚ وَاللَّهُ وَاسِعٌ عَلِيمٌ

Their prophet told them, “Allah has appointed Saul to be your king.” They protested, “How can he be our king when some of us are more deserving of kingship than he, and he has not been blessed with vast riches?” He replied, “Allah has chosen him over you and blessed him with knowledge and stature. Allah grants kingship to whoever He wills. And Allah is All-Bountiful, All-Knowing.”

And their prophet said to them: Indeed, Allah has sent to you Saul as a king in response to your request, to lead you in fighting your enemy as you requested. The leaders of the Children of Israel said: How can Saul be a king over us, when he does not deserve it? For he is not from the tribe of kings, nor from the house of prophethood, and he has not been given much wealth to use in his kingdom. So we are more deserving of the kingdom than him, because we are from the tribe of kings and from the house of prophethood. Their prophet said to them: Indeed, Allah has chosen him over you, and He is Most Knowing of the affairs of His servants, and He has increased him in knowledge and physical strength to fight the enemy. And Allah is the Owner of the kingdom; He gives His kingdom to whom He wills of His servants, and Allah is vast in bounty and bestowal, Knowing of the realities of things; nothing is hidden from Him.

The prophet told them that Allah had appointed Saul as their king. The Children of Israel objected, citing Saul's lack of wealth and noble lineage. The prophet clarified that Allah chooses leaders based on knowledge and stature, emphasizing that Allah grants power to whomever He wills.

Verse 248

وَقَالَ لَهُمْ نَبِيُّهُمْ إِنَّ آيَةَ مُلْكِهِ أَنْ يَأْتِيَكُمُ التَّابُوتُ فِيهِ سَكِينَةٌ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ وَبَقِيَّةٌ مِمَّا تَرَكَ آلُ مُوسَىٰ وَآلُ هَارُونَ تَحْمِلُهُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ ۚ إِنَّ فِي ذَٰلِكَ لَآيَةً لَكُمْ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ مُؤْمِنِينَ

Their prophet further told them, “The sign of Saul’s kingship is that the Ark will come to you—containing reassurance from your Lord and relics of the family of Moses and the family of Aaron, which will be carried by the angels. Surely in this is a sign for you, if you ˹truly˺ believe.”

And their prophet said to them: Indeed, the sign of his kingship is that the chest will come to you, in which is the Torah - and their enemies had seized it from them - within it is tranquility from your Lord, which strengthens the hearts of the sincere, and within it is a remnant of some things left by the family of Moses and the family of Aaron, such as the staff and fragments of the tablets, which the angels will carry. Indeed, in that is a great proof for you of the selection of Saul as a king over you by the command of Allah, if you are believers in Allah and His messengers.

The prophet revealed a sign of Saul's kingship: the return of the Ark of the Covenant, containing relics from Moses and Aaron, carried by angels. This serves as proof of divine selection for those who truly believe.

Verse 249

فَلَمَّا فَصَلَ طَالُوتُ بِالْجُنُودِ قَالَ إِنَّ اللَّهَ مُبْتَلِيكُمْ بِنَهَرٍ فَمَنْ شَرِبَ مِنْهُ فَلَيْسَ مِنِّي وَمَنْ لَمْ يَطْعَمْهُ فَإِنَّهُ مِنِّي إِلَّا مَنِ اغْتَرَفَ غُرْفَةً بِيَدِهِ ۚ فَشَرِبُوا مِنْهُ إِلَّا قَلِيلًا مِنْهُمْ ۚ فَلَمَّا جَاوَزَهُ هُوَ وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا مَعَهُ قَالُوا لَا طَاقَةَ لَنَا الْيَوْمَ بِجَالُوتَ وَجُنُودِهِ ۚ قَالَ الَّذِينَ يَظُنُّونَ أَنَّهُمْ مُلَاقُو اللَّهِ كَمْ مِنْ فِئَةٍ قَلِيلَةٍ غَلَبَتْ فِئَةً كَثِيرَةً بِإِذْنِ اللَّهِ ۗ وَاللَّهُ مَعَ الصَّابِرِينَ

When Saul marched forth with his army, he cautioned: “Allah will test you with a river. So whoever drinks ˹his fill˺ from it is not with me, and whoever does not taste it—except a sip from the hollow of his hands—is definitely with me.” They all drank ˹their fill˺ except for a few! When he and the ˹remaining˺ faithful with him crossed the river, they said, “Now we are no match for Goliath and his warriors.” But those ˹believers˺ who were certain they would meet Allah reasoned, “How many times has a small force vanquished a mighty army by the Will of Allah! And Allah is ˹always˺ with the steadfast.”

When Saul went out with his troops to fight the Amalekites, he said to them: Allah is testing your patience with a river in front of you that you will cross, in order to distinguish the believer from the hypocrite. Whoever drinks from the water of the river is not of me, and is not fit to fight with me. And whoever does not taste the water, then he is of me, because he is obedient to my command and fit for jihad, except for the one who takes a single handful with his hand, then there is no blame on him. When they reached the river, they fell upon the water, and overindulged in drinking from it, except for a few of them who endured thirst and heat, and sufficed with a handful of their hand. At that point, the disobedient were left behind. When Saul crossed the river with the few believers who were with him - and they were three hundred and some men - to meet the enemy, and they saw the large number of their enemy and their equipment, they said: We have no power today against Goliath and his mighty soldiers. Then those who were certain of meeting Allah, reminding their brothers of Allah and His power, said: How many small groups of patient believers have overcome, by the permission and command of Allah, a large group of disbelieving and rebellious people. And Allah is with the patient by granting them success, victory, and a good reward.

Saul tested his army with a river, distinguishing the obedient from the disobedient. A small group remained steadfast, showing that victory comes from faith and reliance on Allah, not just numbers. This verse highlights that small, steadfast groups can overcome large forces by the will of Allah.

Verse 250

وَلَمَّا بَرَزُوا لِجَالُوتَ وَجُنُودِهِ قَالُوا رَبَّنَا أَفْرِغْ عَلَيْنَا صَبْرًا وَثَبِّتْ أَقْدَامَنَا وَانْصُرْنَا عَلَى الْقَوْمِ الْكَافِرِينَ

When they advanced to face Goliath and his warriors, they prayed, “Our Lord! Shower us with perseverance, make our steps firm, and give us victory over the disbelieving people.”

And when they appeared before Goliath and his soldiers, and saw the danger with their own eyes, they turned to Allah with supplication and humility, saying: Our Lord, send down upon our hearts great patience, and make our feet firm, and make them steadfast in fighting the enemy, not fleeing from the horrors of war, and help us with Your assistance and support against the disbelieving people.

Faced with the enemy, the believers prayed for patience, steadfastness, and victory from Allah. Their prayer highlights their reliance on Allah in times of difficulty and warfare.

Verse 251

فَهَزَمُوهُمْ بِإِذْنِ اللَّهِ وَقَتَلَ دَاوُودُ جَالُوتَ وَآتَاهُ اللَّهُ الْمُلْكَ وَالْحِكْمَةَ وَعَلَّمَهُ مِمَّا يَشَاءُ ۗ وَلَوْلَا دَفْعُ اللَّهِ النَّاسَ بَعْضَهُمْ بِبَعْضٍ لَفَسَدَتِ الْأَرْضُ وَلَٰكِنَّ اللَّهَ ذُو فَضْلٍ عَلَى الْعَالَمِينَ

So they defeated them by Allah’s Will, and David killed Goliath. And Allah blessed David with kingship and wisdom and taught him what He willed. Had Allah not repelled a group of people by ˹the might of˺ another, corruption would have dominated the earth, but Allah is Gracious to all.

So they defeated them by the permission of Allah, and David, peace be upon him, killed Goliath, the leader of the giants. And Allah Almighty gave David after that the kingdom and prophethood in the Children of Israel, and taught him what He willed of sciences. If it were not that Allah repels some people—who are those obedient to Him and believe in Him—by others, who are disobedient to Allah and associate partners with Him, the earth would have been corrupted by the dominance of disbelief and the establishment of tyranny, and people of disobedience. But Allah is full of bounty to all of creation.

By the Will of Allah, they defeated their enemies; David killed Goliath. Allah granted David kingship and wisdom. This verse illustrates Allah's way of preventing corruption by balancing powers. It highlights Allah's favor and support for believers.

Verse 252

تِلْكَ آيَاتُ اللَّهِ نَتْلُوهَا عَلَيْكَ بِالْحَقِّ ۚ وَإِنَّكَ لَمِنَ الْمُرْسَلِينَ

These are Allah’s revelations which We recite to you ˹O Prophet˺ in truth. And you are truly one of the messengers.

These are the proofs and evidences of Allah, We narrate them to you - O Prophet - with truth, and you are surely among the truthful messengers.

These are the clear signs and messages from Allah, revealed truthfully to the Prophet, affirming his role as a messenger of Allah. This is a confirmation of the truth of the Quran.

Verse 253

تِلْكَ الرُّسُلُ فَضَّلْنَا بَعْضَهُمْ عَلَىٰ بَعْضٍ ۘ مِنْهُمْ مَنْ كَلَّمَ اللَّهُ ۖ وَرَفَعَ بَعْضَهُمْ دَرَجَاتٍ ۚ وَآتَيْنَا عِيسَى ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ الْبَيِّنَاتِ وَأَيَّدْنَاهُ بِرُوحِ الْقُدُسِ ۗ وَلَوْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ مَا اقْتَتَلَ الَّذِينَ مِنْ بَعْدِهِمْ مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا جَاءَتْهُمُ الْبَيِّنَاتُ وَلَٰكِنِ اخْتَلَفُوا فَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ آمَنَ وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ كَفَرَ ۚ وَلَوْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ مَا اقْتَتَلُوا وَلَٰكِنَّ اللَّهَ يَفْعَلُ مَا يُرِيدُ

We have chosen some of those messengers above others. Allah spoke directly to some, and raised some high in rank. To Jesus, son of Mary, We gave clear proofs and supported him with the holy spirit. If Allah had willed, succeeding generations would not have fought ˹among themselves˺ after receiving the clear proofs. But they differed—some believed while others disbelieved. Yet if Allah had willed, they would not have fought one another. But Allah does what He wills.

These noble messengers, Allah favored some of them over others, according to what Allah bestowed upon them: among them are those whom Allah spoke to, like Moses and Muhammad, peace be upon them. And in this is confirmation of the attribute of speech for Allah, the Almighty, in a manner befitting His Majesty. And among them are those whom Allah raised to high ranks, like Muhammad, peace be upon him, due to the universality of his message, the sealing of prophethood with him, and the preference of his nation over all nations, and other things. And Allah the Most High gave Jesus, the son of Mary, peace be upon him, clear miraculous signs, like curing the one born blind by Allah's permission, and the one afflicted with leprosy by Allah's permission, and giving life to the dead by Allah's permission, and He supported him with Gabriel, peace be upon him. If Allah had willed, those who came after these messengers would not have fought after the clear signs had come to them, but they differed among themselves: some of them remained steadfast in their faith, and some of them persisted in their disbelief. If Allah had willed after the disagreement occurred among them, which led to fighting, they would not have fought, but Allah guides whom He wills to His obedience and faith in Him, and He forsakes whom He wills, so he disobeys Him and disbelieves in Him. He does what He wills and chooses.

This verse highlights that Allah favored some messengers over others, granting them different distinctions. Some, like Moses, received direct communication, while others, like Muhammad, were elevated in status. Jesus was given miracles and supported by the Holy Spirit. Despite clear proofs, people differed, with some believing and some disbelieving. Allah's will ultimately prevails in all matters.

Verse 254

يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا أَنْفِقُوا مِمَّا رَزَقْنَاكُمْ مِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ يَأْتِيَ يَوْمٌ لَا بَيْعٌ فِيهِ وَلَا خُلَّةٌ وَلَا شَفَاعَةٌ ۗ وَالْكَافِرُونَ هُمُ الظَّالِمُونَ

O believers! Donate from what We have provided for you before the arrival of a Day when there will be no bargaining, friendship, or intercession. Those who disbelieve are ˹truly˺ the wrongdoers.

O you who have believed in Allah and believed in His Messenger and acted according to his guidance, give the obligatory charity (Zakat), and give in charity from what Allah has given you before the Day of Resurrection comes when there will be no selling, so there will be no profit, and no wealth with which you can ransom yourselves from the punishment of Allah, nor friendship that will save you, nor an intercessor who can lessen the punishment for you. And the disbelievers are the wrongdoers who transgress the limits of Allah.

Believers are encouraged to donate from what Allah has provided them before the Day of Judgment arrives, a day when no wealth or friendship can help. The verse warns that disbelievers are wrongdoers who have transgressed against Allah's limits.

Verse 255

اللَّهُ لَا إِلَٰهَ إِلَّا هُوَ الْحَيُّ الْقَيُّومُ ۚ لَا تَأْخُذُهُ سِنَةٌ وَلَا نَوْمٌ ۚ لَهُ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الْأَرْضِ ۗ مَنْ ذَا الَّذِي يَشْفَعُ عِنْدَهُ إِلَّا بِإِذْنِهِ ۚ يَعْلَمُ مَا بَيْنَ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَمَا خَلْفَهُمْ ۖ وَلَا يُحِيطُونَ بِشَيْءٍ مِنْ عِلْمِهِ إِلَّا بِمَا شَاءَ ۚ وَسِعَ كُرْسِيُّهُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضَ ۖ وَلَا يَئُودُهُ حِفْظُهُمَا ۚ وَهُوَ الْعَلِيُّ الْعَظِيمُ

Allah! There is no god ˹worthy of worship˺ except Him, the Ever-Living, All-Sustaining. Neither drowsiness nor sleep overtakes Him. To Him belongs whatever is in the heavens and whatever is on the earth. Who could possibly intercede with Him without His permission? He ˹fully˺ knows what is ahead of them and what is behind them, but no one can grasp any of His knowledge—except what He wills ˹to reveal˺. His Seat encompasses the heavens and the earth, and the preservation of both does not tire Him. For He is the Most High, the Greatest.

Allah, there is no deity worthy of worship except Him, the Ever-Living, who possesses all the meanings of complete life as befits His Majesty, the Sustainer of all that exists. Neither drowsiness nor sleep overtakes Him. To Him belongs all that is in the heavens and all that is on earth. None dares to intercede with Him except by His permission. His knowledge encompasses all beings, past, present, and future. He knows what is before the creation of future matters and what is behind them of past matters. And none of the creation can comprehend anything of His knowledge except what Allah informs him and reveals to him. His Kursi (Footstool) extends over the heavens and the earth, and the Kursi is the place of the feet of the Lord – may His Majesty be glorified – and no one knows its nature except Allah, the Exalted. And the preservation of them does not weary Him, and He is the Most High, in His Essence and attributes, over all His creation, the Possessor of all attributes of greatness and majesty. This verse is the greatest verse in the Quran, and it is called: (Ayat al-Kursi).

This is *Ayat al-Kursi*, considered the greatest verse in the Quran. It emphasizes the absolute uniqueness of Allah: He is the Ever-Living and Sustainer of all. Nothing is beyond His knowledge and power, and He is the Most High and Greatest. The verse also establishes that no one can intercede without His permission.

Verse 256

لَا إِكْرَاهَ فِي الدِّينِ ۖ قَدْ تَبَيَّنَ الرُّشْدُ مِنَ الْغَيِّ ۚ فَمَنْ يَكْفُرْ بِالطَّاغُوتِ وَيُؤْمِنْ بِاللَّهِ فَقَدِ اسْتَمْسَكَ بِالْعُرْوَةِ الْوُثْقَىٰ لَا انْفِصَامَ لَهَا ۗ وَاللَّهُ سَمِيعٌ عَلِيمٌ

Let there be no compulsion in religion, for the truth stands out clearly from falsehood. So whoever renounces false gods and believes in Allah has certainly grasped the firmest, unfailing hand-hold. And Allah is All-Hearing, All-Knowing.

Due to the perfection of this religion and the clarity of its signs, there is no need for compulsion into it for those from whom the jizya (tribute) is accepted. The proofs are clear, by which the truth is distinguished from falsehood, and guidance from misguidance. So whoever disbelieves in all that is worshipped besides Allah and believes in Allah, then he has firmly and rightly adhered to the best way, and has held onto the strongest cause of religion, which will not cease. And Allah is Hearing of the statements of His servants, Knowing of their actions and intentions, and He will recompense them for that.

This verse clarifies that there should be no compulsion in matters of faith. Truth is distinct from falsehood. Whoever rejects false deities and believes in Allah has grasped the most solid handhold. Allah hears all statements and knows all actions.

Verse 257

اللَّهُ وَلِيُّ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا يُخْرِجُهُمْ مِنَ الظُّلُمَاتِ إِلَى النُّورِ ۖ وَالَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا أَوْلِيَاؤُهُمُ الطَّاغُوتُ يُخْرِجُونَهُمْ مِنَ النُّورِ إِلَى الظُّلُمَاتِ ۗ أُولَٰئِكَ أَصْحَابُ النَّارِ ۖ هُمْ فِيهَا خَالِدُونَ

Allah is the Guardian of the believers—He brings them out of darkness and into light. As for the disbelievers, their guardians are false gods who lead them out of light and into darkness. It is they who will be the residents of the Fire. They will be there forever.

Allah takes charge of the believers by His victory, success, and protection, bringing them out of the darkness of disbelief into the light of faith. And those who disbelieve, their supporters and allies are the rivals and idols whom they worship besides Allah, they bring them out from the light of faith into the darkness of disbelief. Those are the companions of the Fire, who will abide therein, remaining eternally, never to leave it.

This verse highlights the contrast between believers and disbelievers. Allah is the protector of believers, guiding them from darkness (disbelief) to light (faith). Disbelievers are led by false gods from light into darkness, and they will abide in Hell forever.

Verse 258

أَلَمْ تَرَ إِلَى الَّذِي حَاجَّ إِبْرَاهِيمَ فِي رَبِّهِ أَنْ آتَاهُ اللَّهُ الْمُلْكَ إِذْ قَالَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ رَبِّيَ الَّذِي يُحْيِي وَيُمِيتُ قَالَ أَنَا أُحْيِي وَأُمِيتُ ۖ قَالَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ يَأْتِي بِالشَّمْسِ مِنَ الْمَشْرِقِ فَأْتِ بِهَا مِنَ الْمَغْرِبِ فَبُهِتَ الَّذِي كَفَرَ ۗ وَاللَّهُ لَا يَهْدِي الْقَوْمَ الظَّالِمِينَ

Are you ˹O Prophet˺ not aware of the one who argued with Abraham about his Lord because Allah had granted him kingship? ˹Remember˺ when Abraham said, “My Lord is the One Who has power to give life and cause death.” He argued, “I too have the power to give life and cause death.” Abraham challenged ˹him˺, “Allah causes the sun to rise from the east. So make it rise from the west.” And so the disbeliever was dumbstruck. And Allah does not guide the wrongdoing people.

Have you seen -O Messenger- the most amazing case of this man who argued with Abraham, peace be upon him, about the Oneness of Allah Almighty and His Lordship; because Allah had given him the kingdom, he became arrogant and asked Abraham: Who is your Lord? He, peace be upon him, said: My Lord is the one who gives life to the creatures, and takes life so they die, He is the one and only who gives life and death. He said: I give life and death, that is, I kill whom I want to kill and keep whom I want to keep alive. So Abraham said to him: Indeed, Allah, whom I worship, brings the sun from the east, so can you change this divine law by making it come from the west? This disbeliever was bewildered and his argument was cut off, like the wrongdoers, Allah does not guide them to truth and righteousness.

This verse narrates Prophet Abraham's argument with a king who disbelieved in Allah. The king, arrogant due to his power, challenged Abraham about who gives life and death. Abraham then challenged the king to change the sun's course, leaving him speechless, as Allah doesn't guide those who reject the truth.

Verse 259

أَوْ كَالَّذِي مَرَّ عَلَىٰ قَرْيَةٍ وَهِيَ خَاوِيَةٌ عَلَىٰ عُرُوشِهَا قَالَ أَنَّىٰ يُحْيِي هَٰذِهِ اللَّهُ بَعْدَ مَوْتِهَا ۖ فَأَمَاتَهُ اللَّهُ مِائَةَ عَامٍ ثُمَّ بَعَثَهُ ۖ قَالَ كَمْ لَبِثْتَ ۖ قَالَ لَبِثْتُ يَوْمًا أَوْ بَعْضَ يَوْمٍ ۖ قَالَ بَلْ لَبِثْتَ مِائَةَ عَامٍ فَانْظُرْ إِلَىٰ طَعَامِكَ وَشَرَابِكَ لَمْ يَتَسَنَّهْ ۖ وَانْظُرْ إِلَىٰ حِمَارِكَ وَلِنَجْعَلَكَ آيَةً لِلنَّاسِ ۖ وَانْظُرْ إِلَى الْعِظَامِ كَيْفَ نُنْشِزُهَا ثُمَّ نَكْسُوهَا لَحْمًا ۚ فَلَمَّا تَبَيَّنَ لَهُ قَالَ أَعْلَمُ أَنَّ اللَّهَ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ

Or ˹are you not aware of˺ the one who passed by a city which was in ruins. He wondered, “How could Allah bring this back to life after its destruction?” So Allah caused him to die for a hundred years then brought him back to life. Allah asked, “How long have you remained ˹in this state˺?” He replied, “Perhaps a day or part of a day.” Allah said, “No! You have remained here for a hundred years! Just look at your food and drink—they have not spoiled. ˹But now˺ look at ˹the remains of˺ your donkey! And ˹so˺ We have made you into a sign for humanity. And look at the bones ˹of the donkey˺, how We bring them together then clothe them with flesh!” When this was made clear to him, he declared, “˹Now˺ I know that Allah is Most Capable of everything.”

Or have you seen -O Messenger- the one who passed by a town whose houses had collapsed and fallen on their foundations, and he said: How will Allah revive this town after its death? So Allah caused him to die for a hundred years, then returned his soul to him, and said to him: How long have you remained dead? He said: I have remained a day or part of a day, so he informed him that he remained dead for a hundred years, and commanded him to look at his food and drink, and how Allah preserved them from changing for this long period, and commanded him to look at his donkey how Allah revived it after it was scattered bones? And he said to him: We will make you a sign for the people, that is: a clear indication of Allah’s ability to resurrect after death, and ordered him to look at the bones how Allah raises some of them above others, and joins some with others, then covers them with flesh after joining, and then restores life to them? When that became clear to him, he acknowledged the greatness of Allah, and that He is capable of all things, and became a sign for the people.

This verse tells the story of a person who doubted Allah's ability to resurrect a ruined city. Allah caused him to die for 100 years and then resurrected him, showing him that his food and drink remained intact and then brought his donkey back to life, showing him Allah's absolute power over life and death.

Verse 260

وَإِذْ قَالَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ رَبِّ أَرِنِي كَيْفَ تُحْيِي الْمَوْتَىٰ ۖ قَالَ أَوَلَمْ تُؤْمِنْ ۖ قَالَ بَلَىٰ وَلَٰكِنْ لِيَطْمَئِنَّ قَلْبِي ۖ قَالَ فَخُذْ أَرْبَعَةً مِنَ الطَّيْرِ فَصُرْهُنَّ إِلَيْكَ ثُمَّ اجْعَلْ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ جَبَلٍ مِنْهُنَّ جُزْءًا ثُمَّ ادْعُهُنَّ يَأْتِينَكَ سَعْيًا ۚ وَاعْلَمْ أَنَّ اللَّهَ عَزِيزٌ حَكِيمٌ

And ˹remember˺ when Abraham said, “My Lord! Show me how you give life to the dead.” Allah responded, “Do you not believe?” Abraham replied, “Yes I do, but just so my heart can be reassured.” Allah said, “Then bring four birds, train them to come to you, ˹then cut them into pieces,˺ and scatter them on different hilltops. Then call them back, they will fly to you in haste. And ˹so you will˺ know that Allah is Almighty, All-Wise.”

And remember - O Messenger - Abraham's request to his Lord to show him how the resurrection occurs. Allah said to him: “Do you not believe?” He said: “Yes, but I ask that I may be more certain.” Allah said: “Then take four birds, draw them to yourself, slaughter them, cut them into pieces, then place a part of them on each mountain, then call them, they will come to you in haste.” So Abraham called, peace be upon him, and each part returned to its place, and there they came rushing. And know that Allah is Mighty, nothing can overcome Him, Wise in His words, actions, law, and decree.

Prophet Abraham asked Allah to show him how He gives life to the dead to reassure his heart. Allah instructed him to take four birds, train them, then scatter their pieces on hilltops. When called, the birds returned, demonstrating Allah's power and wisdom.

Verse 261

مَثَلُ الَّذِينَ يُنْفِقُونَ أَمْوَالَهُمْ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ كَمَثَلِ حَبَّةٍ أَنْبَتَتْ سَبْعَ سَنَابِلَ فِي كُلِّ سُنْبُلَةٍ مِائَةُ حَبَّةٍ ۗ وَاللَّهُ يُضَاعِفُ لِمَنْ يَشَاءُ ۗ وَاللَّهُ وَاسِعٌ عَلِيمٌ

The example of those who spend their wealth in the cause of Allah is that of a grain that sprouts into seven ears, each bearing one hundred grains. And Allah multiplies ˹the reward even more˺ to whoever He wills. For Allah is All-Bountiful, All-Knowing.

And among the greatest things that benefit the believers is spending in the cause of Allah. And the likeness of those who spend their wealth in the cause of Allah is as the likeness of a grain sown in good soil, then it brings forth a stalk from which seven ears branch out, for each one is a cluster, and in each cluster is a hundred grains. And Allah multiplies the reward for whom He wills, according to the faith and complete sincerity in the heart of the one who spends. And the bounty of Allah is vast, and He is All-Knowing of who deserves it, aware of the intentions of His servants.

Spending in Allah's cause is likened to a seed that grows into seven ears, each bearing one hundred grains. Allah multiplies rewards for those who spend sincerely, as He is All-Bountiful and All-Knowing.

Verse 262

الَّذِينَ يُنْفِقُونَ أَمْوَالَهُمْ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ ثُمَّ لَا يُتْبِعُونَ مَا أَنْفَقُوا مَنًّا وَلَا أَذًى ۙ لَهُمْ أَجْرُهُمْ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ وَلَا خَوْفٌ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا هُمْ يَحْزَنُونَ

Those who spend their wealth in the cause of Allah and do not follow their charity with reminders of their generosity or hurtful words—they will get their reward from their Lord, and there will be no fear for them, nor will they grieve.

Those who spend their wealth in jihad and various good deeds, then do not follow up what they have spent of good deeds with reminders of favor upon those they gave to, nor harm with word or deed that makes them feel obliged, for them is their great reward with their Lord, and no fear will be upon them in what they face of the Hereafter, nor will they grieve over anything that has passed them by in this world.

Those who spend in Allah's cause and do not follow it with reminders or hurtful words will receive their reward from Allah. They will have no fear in the Hereafter, nor will they grieve.

Verse 263

قَوْلٌ مَعْرُوفٌ وَمَغْفِرَةٌ خَيْرٌ مِنْ صَدَقَةٍ يَتْبَعُهَا أَذًى ۗ وَاللَّهُ غَنِيٌّ حَلِيمٌ

Kind words and forgiveness are better than charity followed by injury. And Allah is Self-Sufficient, Most Forbearing.

Kind speech and forgiveness for what has occurred from the petitioner of importunity in the question, is better than charity followed by harm and offense from the one giving charity. And Allah is free of need of the charity of His servants, forbearing, He does not hasten their punishment.

Kind words and forgiveness are better than charity followed by injury. Allah is Self-Sufficient and Most Forbearing, not needing the charity of His servants.

Verse 264

يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تُبْطِلُوا صَدَقَاتِكُمْ بِالْمَنِّ وَالْأَذَىٰ كَالَّذِي يُنْفِقُ مَالَهُ رِئَاءَ النَّاسِ وَلَا يُؤْمِنُ بِاللَّهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ ۖ فَمَثَلُهُ كَمَثَلِ صَفْوَانٍ عَلَيْهِ تُرَابٌ فَأَصَابَهُ وَابِلٌ فَتَرَكَهُ صَلْدًا ۖ لَا يَقْدِرُونَ عَلَىٰ شَيْءٍ مِمَّا كَسَبُوا ۗ وَاللَّهُ لَا يَهْدِي الْقَوْمَ الْكَافِرِينَ

O believers! Do not waste your charity with reminders ˹of your generosity˺ or hurtful words, like those who donate their wealth just to show off and do not believe in Allah or the Last Day. Their example is that of a hard barren rock covered with a thin layer of soil hit by a strong rain—leaving it just a bare stone. Such people are unable to preserve the reward of their charity. Allah does not guide ˹such˺ disbelieving people.

O you who have believed in Allah and the Last Day, do not invalidate the reward of what you give in charity by reminders of favor and harm, for this is similar to the one who spends his wealth for people to see, so they will praise him, and he does not believe in Allah nor is certain of the Last Day. So the example of that is like a smooth rock covered with soil, heavy rain falls upon it and removes the soil, leaving it smooth with nothing on it, and likewise these hypocrites, their deeds will diminish with Allah, and they will not find any reward for what they have spent. And Allah does not guide the disbelievers to achieve the truth in their spending and other matters.

Believers should not nullify their charity with reminders or hurtful words, like those who give to show off and do not believe in Allah or the Last Day. Their charity is like a thin layer of soil on a rock, washed away by rain, leaving no reward. Allah does not guide disbelievers.

Verse 265

وَمَثَلُ الَّذِينَ يُنْفِقُونَ أَمْوَالَهُمُ ابْتِغَاءَ مَرْضَاتِ اللَّهِ وَتَثْبِيتًا مِنْ أَنْفُسِهِمْ كَمَثَلِ جَنَّةٍ بِرَبْوَةٍ أَصَابَهَا وَابِلٌ فَآتَتْ أُكُلَهَا ضِعْفَيْنِ فَإِنْ لَمْ يُصِبْهَا وَابِلٌ فَطَلٌّ ۗ وَاللَّهُ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ بَصِيرٌ

And the example of those who donate their wealth, seeking Allah’s pleasure and believing the reward is certain, is that of a garden on a fertile hill: when heavy rain falls, it yields up twice its normal produce. If no heavy rain falls, a drizzle is sufficient. And Allah is All-Seeing of what you do.

And the example of those who spend their wealth seeking the pleasure of Allah and with firm conviction in the truth of His promise, is like a great garden on high, good land, upon which heavy rain falls, and its fruits are doubled. And if heavy rain does not fall upon it, then the drizzle is sufficient to give the doubled fruit. Likewise, the expenses of the sincere are accepted by Allah and multiplied, whether they are little or much. For Allah is aware of the secrets, the Seeing of the apparent and the hidden, and He rewards each according to his sincerity.

This verse compares sincere charity to a fruitful garden on fertile land. Whether it receives heavy rain or a drizzle, it yields abundant produce, showing that even small acts of charity, when done sincerely for Allah, are multiplied in reward. Allah sees all actions and intentions.

Verse 266

أَيَوَدُّ أَحَدُكُمْ أَنْ تَكُونَ لَهُ جَنَّةٌ مِنْ نَخِيلٍ وَأَعْنَابٍ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهَا الْأَنْهَارُ لَهُ فِيهَا مِنْ كُلِّ الثَّمَرَاتِ وَأَصَابَهُ الْكِبَرُ وَلَهُ ذُرِّيَّةٌ ضُعَفَاءُ فَأَصَابَهَا إِعْصَارٌ فِيهِ نَارٌ فَاحْتَرَقَتْ ۗ كَذَٰلِكَ يُبَيِّنُ اللَّهُ لَكُمُ الْآيَاتِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَتَفَكَّرُونَ

Would any of you wish to have a garden with palm trees, grapevines, and all kinds of fruits with rivers flowing underneath and as they grow very old with dependent children, a fiery whirlwind hits the garden, burning it all up? This is how Allah makes His revelations clear to you, so perhaps you will reflect.

Would any of you wish to have a garden of palm trees and grapevines, with rivers flowing beneath its trees, and have all kinds of fruits in it, and he has reached old age and cannot plant such a planting, and he has young children in need of this garden. And in this state, a fierce wind, with scorching fire, blows upon it and burns it. Such is the state of those who are not sincere in their spending. They will come on the Day of Resurrection with no good deeds. And with such an explanation, Allah makes clear to you what benefits you, so that you may reflect and make your spending sincere for Allah.

This verse presents a parable of a prosperous garden destroyed by fire, representing the state of insincere charity. It highlights the loss that comes from not being sincere, likening it to a person who loses their hard work just when they need it the most. It encourages reflection on the intention behind charitable acts.

Verse 267

يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا أَنْفِقُوا مِنْ طَيِّبَاتِ مَا كَسَبْتُمْ وَمِمَّا أَخْرَجْنَا لَكُمْ مِنَ الْأَرْضِ ۖ وَلَا تَيَمَّمُوا الْخَبِيثَ مِنْهُ تُنْفِقُونَ وَلَسْتُمْ بِآخِذِيهِ إِلَّا أَنْ تُغْمِضُوا فِيهِ ۚ وَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ غَنِيٌّ حَمِيدٌ

O believers! Donate from the best of what you have earned and of what We have produced for you from the earth. Do not pick out worthless things for donation, which you yourselves would only accept with closed eyes. And know that Allah is Self-Sufficient, Praiseworthy.

O you who have believed in Me and followed My messengers, spend from the lawful and good things you have earned and from what We have brought forth for you from the earth. And do not intend the bad thereof to give to the poor, for if it were given to you, you would not take it except with overlooking what is in it of badness and deficiency. So how do you accept for Allah what you do not accept for yourselves? And know that Allah, who has provided for you, is free of need of your charity, worthy of praise, and praiseworthy in every condition.

This verse urges believers to donate from the best of their wealth, rather than giving what is worthless. It reminds them that Allah is Self-Sufficient and worthy of praise, emphasizing sincerity and generosity in giving.

Verse 268

الشَّيْطَانُ يَعِدُكُمُ الْفَقْرَ وَيَأْمُرُكُمْ بِالْفَحْشَاءِ ۖ وَاللَّهُ يَعِدُكُمْ مَغْفِرَةً مِنْهُ وَفَضْلًا ۗ وَاللَّهُ وَاسِعٌ عَلِيمٌ

The Devil threatens you with ˹the prospect of˺ poverty and bids you to the shameful deed ˹of stinginess˺, while Allah promises you forgiveness and ˹great˺ bounties from Him. And Allah is All-Bountiful, All-Knowing.

This stinginess and choosing the bad for charity is from Satan, who frightens you with poverty, and incites you to stinginess, and commands you to disobedience and opposition to Allah Almighty. And Allah, glory be to Him, promises you forgiveness for your sins and abundant provision for your spending. And Allah is vast in bounty, knowing of deeds and intentions.

This verse contrasts the whispering of Satan, who creates fear of poverty and encourages stinginess, with the promise of Allah, who offers forgiveness and bounty for those who give charity. It underscores that Allah is All-Bountiful and All-Knowing.

Verse 269

يُؤْتِي الْحِكْمَةَ مَنْ يَشَاءُ ۚ وَمَنْ يُؤْتَ الْحِكْمَةَ فَقَدْ أُوتِيَ خَيْرًا كَثِيرًا ۗ وَمَا يَذَّكَّرُ إِلَّا أُولُو الْأَلْبَابِ

Allah grants wisdom to whoever He wills. And whoever is granted wisdom is certainly blessed with a great privilege. But none will be mindful ˹of this˺ except people of reason.

Allah grants correctness in speech and action to whom He wills of His servants, and whoever Allah has bestowed this upon, has been given much good. And none remember this and benefit from it except those of enlightened minds with the light and guidance of Allah.

This verse states that Allah grants wisdom to whomever He wills, emphasizing that wisdom is a great blessing. It also highlights that only people of understanding reflect on this and benefit from it.

Verse 270

وَمَا أَنْفَقْتُمْ مِنْ نَفَقَةٍ أَوْ نَذَرْتُمْ مِنْ نَذْرٍ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ يَعْلَمُهُ ۗ وَمَا لِلظَّالِمِينَ مِنْ أَنْصَارٍ

Whatever charities you give or vows you make are surely known to Allah. And the wrongdoers will have no helpers.

And whatever you spend of wealth or other things, much or little, that you give in charity seeking the pleasure of Allah, or you have made obligatory upon yourselves something of wealth or other things, then Allah knows it, and He is aware of your intentions, and He will reward you for that. And whoever withholds the right of Allah is unjust, and the unjust will have no helpers to protect them from the punishment of Allah.

Allah is fully aware of all charitable acts and vows made. Those who do wrong will have no one to help them on the Day of Judgment.

Verse 271

إِنْ تُبْدُوا الصَّدَقَاتِ فَنِعِمَّا هِيَ ۖ وَإِنْ تُخْفُوهَا وَتُؤْتُوهَا الْفُقَرَاءَ فَهُوَ خَيْرٌ لَكُمْ ۚ وَيُكَفِّرُ عَنْكُمْ مِنْ سَيِّئَاتِكُمْ ۗ وَاللَّهُ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ خَبِيرٌ

To give charity publicly is good, but to give to the poor privately is better for you, and will absolve you of your sins. And Allah is All-Aware of what you do.

If you show what you give in charity for Allah, then excellent is that which you give in charity. But if you conceal it and give it to the poor, that is better for you, because it is further from hypocrisy, and in charity - with sincerity - is the erasure of your sins. And Allah, who knows the details of matters, nothing of your conditions is hidden from Him, and He will recompense each one for his deeds.

Giving charity openly is good, but giving it privately to the poor is better and can lead to forgiveness of sins. Allah is aware of everything you do.

Verse 272

لَيْسَ عَلَيْكَ هُدَاهُمْ وَلَٰكِنَّ اللَّهَ يَهْدِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ ۗ وَمَا تُنْفِقُوا مِنْ خَيْرٍ فَلِأَنْفُسِكُمْ ۚ وَمَا تُنْفِقُونَ إِلَّا ابْتِغَاءَ وَجْهِ اللَّهِ ۚ وَمَا تُنْفِقُوا مِنْ خَيْرٍ يُوَفَّ إِلَيْكُمْ وَأَنْتُمْ لَا تُظْلَمُونَ

You are not responsible for people’s guidance ˹O Prophet˺—it is Allah Who guides whoever He wills. Whatever you ˹believers˺ spend in charity, it is for your own good—as long as you do so seeking the pleasure of Allah. Whatever you donate will be paid back to you in full, and you will not be wronged.

You, [O Messenger], are not responsible for the guidance of the disbelievers, but Allah guides whom He wills to His religion and enables him to it. And whatever you spend of wealth, its benefit will return to you from Allah, and the believers do not spend except seeking the pleasure of Allah. And whatever you spend of wealth - sincerely for Allah - its reward will be fulfilled, and you will not be reduced anything of that. And in the verse is the affirmation of the attribute of the Face for Allah the Most High in a manner befitting Him, Glory be to Him.

The Prophet is not responsible for guiding people; Allah guides whom He wills. Charity is for your own benefit when done for Allah's pleasure, and you will receive full reward without any injustice.

Verse 273

لِلْفُقَرَاءِ الَّذِينَ أُحْصِرُوا فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ لَا يَسْتَطِيعُونَ ضَرْبًا فِي الْأَرْضِ يَحْسَبُهُمُ الْجَاهِلُ أَغْنِيَاءَ مِنَ التَّعَفُّفِ تَعْرِفُهُمْ بِسِيمَاهُمْ لَا يَسْأَلُونَ النَّاسَ إِلْحَافًا ۗ وَمَا تُنْفِقُوا مِنْ خَيْرٍ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ بِهِ عَلِيمٌ

˹Charity is˺ for the needy who are too engaged in the cause of Allah to move about in the land ˹for work˺. Those unfamiliar with their situation will think they are not in need ˹of charity˺ because they do not beg. You can recognize them by their appearance. They do not beg people persistently. Whatever you give in charity is certainly well known to Allah.

Make your charities for the poor Muslims who are unable to travel seeking livelihood because of their preoccupation with fighting in the cause of Allah. He who does not know them thinks them free of need because of their abstention from begging. You know them by their marks and the traces of need in them. They do not ask people at all, and if they ask out of necessity, they do not insist on asking. And whatever you spend of wealth in the cause of Allah, nothing of it is hidden from Allah, and He will recompense for it with the fullest and most complete reward on the Day of Resurrection.

Charity should be given to those in need who are dedicated to Allah's cause and cannot seek livelihood. They are recognized by their appearance and do not beg persistently. Allah knows all charity given.

Verse 274

الَّذِينَ يُنْفِقُونَ أَمْوَالَهُمْ بِاللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ سِرًّا وَعَلَانِيَةً فَلَهُمْ أَجْرُهُمْ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ وَلَا خَوْفٌ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا هُمْ يَحْزَنُونَ

Those who spend their wealth in charity day and night, secretly and openly—their reward is with their Lord, and there will be no fear for them, nor will they grieve.

Those who spend their wealth seeking the pleasure of Allah by night and by day, secretly and openly, then they will have their reward with their Lord, and no fear will be upon them regarding what they will face in the Hereafter, nor will they grieve for what they have missed of the gains of this world. That wise divine legislation is the method of Islam in spending because it contains the filling of the need of the poor with dignity and honor, and the purification of the wealth of the rich, and the achievement of cooperation on righteousness and piety; seeking the Face of Allah without compulsion or coercion.

Those who give charity day and night, secretly and openly, will receive their reward from Allah, and they will not fear nor grieve. This verse emphasizes the importance of continuous and sincere charity.

Verse 275

الَّذِينَ يَأْكُلُونَ الرِّبَا لَا يَقُومُونَ إِلَّا كَمَا يَقُومُ الَّذِي يَتَخَبَّطُهُ الشَّيْطَانُ مِنَ الْمَسِّ ۚ ذَٰلِكَ بِأَنَّهُمْ قَالُوا إِنَّمَا الْبَيْعُ مِثْلُ الرِّبَا ۗ وَأَحَلَّ اللَّهُ الْبَيْعَ وَحَرَّمَ الرِّبَا ۚ فَمَنْ جَاءَهُ مَوْعِظَةٌ مِنْ رَبِّهِ فَانْتَهَىٰ فَلَهُ مَا سَلَفَ وَأَمْرُهُ إِلَى اللَّهِ ۖ وَمَنْ عَادَ فَأُولَٰئِكَ أَصْحَابُ النَّارِ ۖ هُمْ فِيهَا خَالِدُونَ

Those who consume interest will stand ˹on Judgment Day˺ like those driven to madness by Satan’s touch. That is because they say, “Trade is no different than interest.” But Allah has permitted trading and forbidden interest. Whoever refrains—after having received warning from their Lord—may keep their previous gains, and their case is left to Allah. As for those who persist, it is they who will be the residents of the Fire. They will be there forever.

Those who deal with usury - which is the increase on the principal - will not rise in the Hereafter from their graves except like the one whom Satan confuses with madness; that is because they said: Indeed, selling is like usury, in that both are permissible and lead to an increase in wealth. But Allah has denied them and clarified that He has made selling lawful and prohibited usury because of the benefit in buying and selling for individuals and groups, and because of the exploitation, loss, and destruction in usury. So whoever receives a prohibition from Allah regarding usury and refrains, then he is entitled to what passed before the prohibition reached him, and there is no sin upon him in that. And his matter is with Allah in what remains of his time. If he continues in his repentance, then Allah does not waste the reward of the good-doers. And whoever returns to usury and does it after the prohibition from Allah reached him, then he has deserved the punishment and the proof has been established against him. That is why He, the Exalted, said: "Those are the companions of the Fire; they will abide therein eternally."

This verse describes the severe state of those who consume interest, comparing them to those driven mad by Satan. It emphasizes that Allah has forbidden interest while allowing trade, and warns of eternal punishment in Hell for those who persist in dealing with interest.

Verse 276

يَمْحَقُ اللَّهُ الرِّبَا وَيُرْبِي الصَّدَقَاتِ ۗ وَاللَّهُ لَا يُحِبُّ كُلَّ كَفَّارٍ أَثِيمٍ

Allah has made interest fruitless and charity fruitful. And Allah does not like any ungrateful evildoer.

Allah destroys usury entirely or deprives its owner of the blessing of his money, so he does not benefit from it, and He increases charities and makes them abundant, and multiplies the reward for those who give charity, and blesses them in their wealth. And Allah does not love every persistent disbeliever, who deems the consumption of usury lawful, and continues in sin, wrongdoing, and disobedience to Allah.

This verse highlights the contrasting outcomes of interest and charity. Allah diminishes the gains from interest, making it fruitless, while He blesses and increases charity. The verse also states that Allah dislikes those who are ungrateful and persist in wrongdoing.

Verse 277

إِنَّ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ وَأَقَامُوا الصَّلَاةَ وَآتَوُا الزَّكَاةَ لَهُمْ أَجْرُهُمْ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ وَلَا خَوْفٌ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا هُمْ يَحْزَنُونَ

Indeed, those who believe, do good, establish prayer, and pay alms-tax will receive their reward from their Lord, and there will be no fear for them, nor will they grieve.

Indeed, those who believed in Allah and His Messenger, and did good deeds, and performed prayer as Allah and His Messenger commanded, and gave the zakat of their wealth, they have a great reward specifically for them with their Lord and Provider. And they will have no fear in their Hereafter, nor will they grieve over what they have missed of the pleasures of their worldly life.

This verse promises a great reward from Allah for believers who perform good deeds, establish prayer, and pay Zakat (alms-tax). They will have no fear or grief in the Hereafter.

Verse 278

يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا اتَّقُوا اللَّهَ وَذَرُوا مَا بَقِيَ مِنَ الرِّبَا إِنْ كُنْتُمْ مُؤْمِنِينَ

O believers! Fear Allah, and give up outstanding interest if you are ˹true˺ believers.

O you who have believed in Allah and followed His Messenger, fear Allah, and abandon what remains for you of increase over your principal amounts that were yours before the prohibition of usury, if you are truthful in your faith in word and deed.

This verse is a direct command to believers to fear Allah and to abandon all outstanding interest. This is presented as a condition of true faith.

Verse 279

فَإِنْ لَمْ تَفْعَلُوا فَأْذَنُوا بِحَرْبٍ مِنَ اللَّهِ وَرَسُولِهِ ۖ وَإِنْ تُبْتُمْ فَلَكُمْ رُءُوسُ أَمْوَالِكُمْ لَا تَظْلِمُونَ وَلَا تُظْلَمُونَ

If you do not, then beware of a war with Allah and His Messenger! But if you repent, you may retain your principal—neither inflicting nor suffering harm.

But if you do not refrain from what Allah has forbidden you, then be certain of war from Allah and His Messenger. And if you return to your Lord and abandon the taking of usury, then you are entitled to take what is owed to you of debts without increase. Neither shall you wrong anyone by taking more than your principal amounts, nor shall anyone wrong you by deducting from what you lent.

This verse warns those who do not give up interest of a war against Allah and His Messenger. However, it also provides a way out through repentance, allowing people to take back their original principal without any increase or decrease.

Verse 280

وَإِنْ كَانَ ذُو عُسْرَةٍ فَنَظِرَةٌ إِلَىٰ مَيْسَرَةٍ ۚ وَأَنْ تَصَدَّقُوا خَيْرٌ لَكُمْ ۖ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ تَعْلَمُونَ

If it is difficult for someone to repay a debt, postpone it until a time of ease. And if you waive it as an act of charity, it will be better for you, if only you knew.

And if the debtor is unable to repay, then give him respite until Allah makes it easy for him and provides him with sustenance, so he can pay you your money. And if you waive the principal entirely or part of it and forgive the debtor, then it is better for you, if you know the virtue of that, and that it is better for you in this world and the Hereafter.

This verse addresses the matter of debts. It instructs believers to give respite to debtors in financial hardship and encourages forgiving debts as an act of charity, stating that it is better for them if they knew.

Verse 281

وَاتَّقُوا يَوْمًا تُرْجَعُونَ فِيهِ إِلَى اللَّهِ ۖ ثُمَّ تُوَفَّىٰ كُلُّ نَفْسٍ مَا كَسَبَتْ وَهُمْ لَا يُظْلَمُونَ

Be mindful of the Day when you will ˹all˺ be returned to Allah, then every soul will be paid in full for what it has done, and none will be wronged.

And beware, O people, of a Day in which you will be returned to Allah, which is the Day of Resurrection, where you will be presented to Allah to be reckoned, and He will recompense each one of you for what he has done of good or evil without being wronged. And in the verse is a sign that avoiding what Allah has forbidden of usurious earnings, is a completion of faith and its rights of establishing prayer, giving zakat, and doing good deeds.

This verse is a reminder of the Day of Judgment, where all will return to Allah and be recompensed for their deeds. It emphasizes the importance of avoiding forbidden earnings like interest as part of fulfilling the rights of faith.

Verse 282

يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا إِذَا تَدَايَنْتُمْ بِدَيْنٍ إِلَىٰ أَجَلٍ مُسَمًّى فَاكْتُبُوهُ ۚ وَلْيَكْتُبْ بَيْنَكُمْ كَاتِبٌ بِالْعَدْلِ ۚ وَلَا يَأْبَ كَاتِبٌ أَنْ يَكْتُبَ كَمَا عَلَّمَهُ اللَّهُ ۚ فَلْيَكْتُبْ وَلْيُمْلِلِ الَّذِي عَلَيْهِ الْحَقُّ وَلْيَتَّقِ اللَّهَ رَبَّهُ وَلَا يَبْخَسْ مِنْهُ شَيْئًا ۚ فَإِنْ كَانَ الَّذِي عَلَيْهِ الْحَقُّ سَفِيهًا أَوْ ضَعِيفًا أَوْ لَا يَسْتَطِيعُ أَنْ يُمِلَّ هُوَ فَلْيُمْلِلْ وَلِيُّهُ بِالْعَدْلِ ۚ وَاسْتَشْهِدُوا شَهِيدَيْنِ مِنْ رِجَالِكُمْ ۖ فَإِنْ لَمْ يَكُونَا رَجُلَيْنِ فَرَجُلٌ وَامْرَأَتَانِ مِمَّنْ تَرْضَوْنَ مِنَ الشُّهَدَاءِ أَنْ تَضِلَّ إِحْدَاهُمَا فَتُذَكِّرَ إِحْدَاهُمَا الْأُخْرَىٰ ۚ وَلَا يَأْبَ الشُّهَدَاءُ إِذَا مَا دُعُوا ۚ وَلَا تَسْأَمُوا أَنْ تَكْتُبُوهُ صَغِيرًا أَوْ كَبِيرًا إِلَىٰ أَجَلِهِ ۚ ذَٰلِكُمْ أَقْسَطُ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ وَأَقْوَمُ لِلشَّهَادَةِ وَأَدْنَىٰ أَلَّا تَرْتَابُوا ۖ إِلَّا أَنْ تَكُونَ تِجَارَةً حَاضِرَةً تُدِيرُونَهَا بَيْنَكُمْ فَلَيْسَ عَلَيْكُمْ جُنَاحٌ أَلَّا تَكْتُبُوهَا ۗ وَأَشْهِدُوا إِذَا تَبَايَعْتُمْ ۚ وَلَا يُضَارَّ كَاتِبٌ وَلَا شَهِيدٌ ۚ وَإِنْ تَفْعَلُوا فَإِنَّهُ فُسُوقٌ بِكُمْ ۗ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ ۖ وَيُعَلِّمُكُمُ اللَّهُ ۗ وَاللَّهُ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عَلِيمٌ

O believers! When you contract a loan for a fixed period of time, commit it to writing. Let the scribe maintain justice between the parties. The scribe should not refuse to write as Allah has taught them to write. They will write what the debtor dictates, bearing Allah in mind and not defrauding the debt. If the debtor is incompetent, weak, or unable to dictate, let their guardian dictate for them with justice. Call upon two of your men to witness. If two men cannot be found, then one man and two women of your choice will witness—so if one of the women forgets the other may remind her. The witnesses must not refuse when they are summoned. You must not be against writing ˹contracts˺ for a fixed period—whether the sum is small or great. This is more just ˹for you˺ in the sight of Allah, and more convenient to establish evidence and remove doubts. However, if you conduct an immediate transaction among yourselves, then there is no need for you to record it, but call upon witnesses when a deal is finalized. Let no harm come to the scribe or witnesses. If you do, then you have gravely exceeded ˹your limits˺. Be mindful of Allah, for Allah ˹is the One Who˺ teaches you. And Allah has ˹perfect˺ knowledge of all things.

O you who have believed, when you contract a debt for a specified term, write it down. This is for the preservation of wealth and the prevention of disputes. And let a trustworthy and capable man write it, and let not the one whom Allah has taught writing refuse to do so. And let the debtor dictate what he owes, and let him fear his Lord, and not reduce anything from his debt. And if the debtor is incompetent because of his extravagance and wastefulness, or is a minor, or insane, or unable to speak because of muteness, or lacks full ability to speak, then let the one who is in charge of the debtor dictate, and seek the testimony of two Muslim men who are of age and sound mind and of good character. And if two men are not found, then seek the testimony of a man and two women from whom you are satisfied with their testimony, so that if one of them forgets, the other may remind her. And the witnesses should respond when they are called upon to bear witness, and they should perform it when they are called to it, and do not be weary of writing it, whether it be small or large, for its specified time. That is more just in the law of Allah and His guidance, and a greater aid to establishing testimony and fulfilling it, and closer to removing doubt about the kind of debt, its amount and its term. But if the issue is a matter of buying and selling, taking a commodity and paying its price on the spot, then there is no need to write it down, and it is recommended to have witnesses to prevent conflict and division. And it is obligatory for the witness and the scribe to bear witness truthfully and to write as Allah commanded. And it is not permissible for the owner of the right and the one who owes the right to harm the scribes and the witnesses, and likewise it is not permissible for the scribes and the witnesses to harm those who need their writing or testimony, and if you do what you are forbidden from, then that is disobedience to Allah, and its consequence will befall you. And fear Allah in all that He has commanded you with and forbade you from, and Allah will teach you all that will benefit you in this world and the hereafter. And Allah is All-Knowing of everything, nothing of your affairs is hidden from Him, and He will recompense you for it.

This verse emphasizes the importance of documenting financial transactions, particularly loans, to ensure fairness and prevent disputes. It outlines the procedures for writing contracts, including choosing a just scribe, having the debtor dictate the terms, and obtaining reliable witnesses (two men or one man and two women). It also advises against harming the scribe or witnesses and stresses the importance of being mindful of Allah in all dealings, as He is the source of all knowledge.

Verse 283

وَإِنْ كُنْتُمْ عَلَىٰ سَفَرٍ وَلَمْ تَجِدُوا كَاتِبًا فَرِهَانٌ مَقْبُوضَةٌ ۖ فَإِنْ أَمِنَ بَعْضُكُمْ بَعْضًا فَلْيُؤَدِّ الَّذِي اؤْتُمِنَ أَمَانَتَهُ وَلْيَتَّقِ اللَّهَ رَبَّهُ ۗ وَلَا تَكْتُمُوا الشَّهَادَةَ ۚ وَمَنْ يَكْتُمْهَا فَإِنَّهُ آثِمٌ قَلْبُهُ ۗ وَاللَّهُ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ عَلِيمٌ

If you are on a journey and a scribe cannot be found, then a security can be taken. If you trust one another, then ˹there is no need for a security, but˺ the debtor should honour this trust ˹by repaying the debt˺—and let them fear Allah, their Lord. And do not conceal the testimony, for whoever conceals it, their hearts are indeed sinful. And Allah ˹fully˺ knows what you do.

And if you are traveling and cannot find a scribe, then let a pledge be taken as security. And if you trust one another, then there is no blame upon you if you do not write or have witnesses, and the debt remains a trust upon the debtor, who must fulfill it. He must be mindful of Allah and not betray his companion. And if the debtor denies what he owes, and there was someone who attended and witnessed, then he must declare his testimony. And whoever conceals this testimony, then he has a treacherous and wicked heart. And Allah is aware of the secrets, His knowledge encompasses all your affairs, and He will hold you accountable for that.

This verse addresses financial transactions during travel, advising on taking security if a scribe is unavailable. It stresses honoring trusts and the importance of truthful testimony. Concealing testimony is a grave sin, and Allah is aware of all actions.

Verse 284

لِلَّهِ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الْأَرْضِ ۗ وَإِنْ تُبْدُوا مَا فِي أَنْفُسِكُمْ أَوْ تُخْفُوهُ يُحَاسِبْكُمْ بِهِ اللَّهُ ۖ فَيَغْفِرُ لِمَنْ يَشَاءُ وَيُعَذِّبُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ ۗ وَاللَّهُ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ

To Allah ˹alone˺ belongs whatever is in the heavens and whatever is on the earth. Whether you reveal what is in your hearts or conceal it, Allah will call you to account for it. He forgives whoever He wills, and punishes whoever He wills. And Allah is Most Capable of everything.

To Allah belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth and what is within them, in ownership, management, and encompassing knowledge; nothing is hidden from Him. And whether you disclose what is within your selves or conceal it, then Allah knows it. And He will hold you accountable for it, then forgive whom He wills and punish whom He wills. And Allah is powerful over all things. And Allah honored the Muslims after that and forgave for thoughts and whispers of the heart as long as it was not followed by speech or action, as that has been confirmed from the Messenger of Allah, peace and blessings be upon him.

This verse emphasizes Allah's absolute ownership and knowledge of all creation. Whether thoughts or actions are revealed or concealed, Allah will hold everyone accountable. However, He has the power to forgive or punish as He wills, highlighting His complete control.

Verse 285

آمَنَ الرَّسُولُ بِمَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْهِ مِنْ رَبِّهِ وَالْمُؤْمِنُونَ ۚ كُلٌّ آمَنَ بِاللَّهِ وَمَلَائِكَتِهِ وَكُتُبِهِ وَرُسُلِهِ لَا نُفَرِّقُ بَيْنَ أَحَدٍ مِنْ رُسُلِهِ ۚ وَقَالُوا سَمِعْنَا وَأَطَعْنَا ۖ غُفْرَانَكَ رَبَّنَا وَإِلَيْكَ الْمَصِيرُ

The Messenger ˹firmly˺ believes in what has been revealed to him from his Lord, and so do the believers. They ˹all˺ believe in Allah, His angels, His Books, and His messengers. ˹They proclaim,˺ “We make no distinction between any of His messengers.” And they say, “We hear and obey. ˹We seek˺ Your forgiveness, our Lord! And to You ˹alone˺ is the final return.”

The Messenger of Allah, Muhammad, peace and blessings be upon him, believed and was certain of what was revealed to him from his Lord, and it is his right to be certain. And the believers also believed and acted upon the Great Quran. Each of them believed in Allah as Lord and God, described with attributes of majesty and perfection, and that Allah has honored angels, and that He sent down books, and sent messengers to His creation. We - the believers - do not believe in some of them and deny others; rather, we believe in them all. And the Messenger and the believers said: 'We have heard, our Lord, what You have revealed, and we obey in all of that. We hope that You will forgive - by Your grace - our sins, for You are the One who nurtured us with what You have bestowed upon us, and to You - alone - is our return and destiny.'

This verse affirms the faith of the Prophet Muhammad and the believers in Allah, His angels, scriptures, and messengers, without distinction. It reflects the believers' submission to Allah's commands and their seeking of His forgiveness, recognizing that all will return to Him.

Verse 286

لَا يُكَلِّفُ اللَّهُ نَفْسًا إِلَّا وُسْعَهَا ۚ لَهَا مَا كَسَبَتْ وَعَلَيْهَا مَا اكْتَسَبَتْ ۗ رَبَّنَا لَا تُؤَاخِذْنَا إِنْ نَسِينَا أَوْ أَخْطَأْنَا ۚ رَبَّنَا وَلَا تَحْمِلْ عَلَيْنَا إِصْرًا كَمَا حَمَلْتَهُ عَلَى الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِنَا ۚ رَبَّنَا وَلَا تُحَمِّلْنَا مَا لَا طَاقَةَ لَنَا بِهِ ۖ وَاعْفُ عَنَّا وَاغْفِرْ لَنَا وَارْحَمْنَا ۚ أَنْتَ مَوْلَانَا فَانْصُرْنَا عَلَى الْقَوْمِ الْكَافِرِينَ

Allah does not require of any soul more than what it can afford. All good will be for its own benefit, and all evil will be to its own loss. ˹The believers pray,˺ “Our Lord! Do not punish us if we forget or make a mistake. Our Lord! Do not place a burden on us like the one you placed on those before us. Our Lord! Do not burden us with what we cannot bear. Pardon us, forgive us, and have mercy on us. You are our ˹only˺ Guardian. So grant us victory over the disbelieving people.”

The religion of Allah is easy, with no hardship in it, so Allah does not ask of His servants what they cannot bear. Whoever does good will attain good, and whoever does evil will attain evil. Our Lord, do not punish us if we forget something of what You have obligated upon us, or if we err in doing something that You have forbidden us from doing. Our Lord, do not place upon us a burden of difficult deeds as You placed upon those before us from the disobedient as a punishment for them. Our Lord, do not impose on us what we cannot bear of obligations and calamities, and erase our sins, and conceal our faults, and be gracious to us. You are the Owner of our affairs and its manager, so grant us victory over those who deny Your religion and deny Your Oneness, and who disbelieved Your Prophet Muhammad, peace and blessings be upon him, and make the outcome for us over them in this world and the Hereafter.

This verse states that Allah does not burden anyone beyond their capacity. It also includes a prayer asking for forgiveness for mistakes, not to be burdened like those before, and for help in overcoming challenges. Allah is acknowledged as the ultimate guardian and source of victory.
